### [1] [From Awareness to Action: How Developers Engage with Accessibility Innovation in LLM-Assisted Development](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10311v1)
*Thayssa Águila da Rocha,Luciane Silva,Ana Duarte,Marcelle Pereira Mota,Gustavo Pinto*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 研究发现，由残障人士主导的无障碍项目更可能产生包容性创新；企业采用参与式方法可将无障碍从合规要求转化为创新驱动力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发者难以设计真正无障碍的数字化解决方案，且企业通常将无障碍视为合规要求而非创新机会。

Method: 分析14份基于LLM的无障碍项目提案，并在巴西一家科技公司组织焦点小组讨论（9名参与者）。

Result: 当倡议由残障人士（PWD）领导时，包容性创新尤其容易涌现。

Conclusion: 组织若采用参与式方法，无障碍将从事后考虑演变为技术卓越和文化变革的驱动力。

中文摘要：开发人员在企业环境中常常难以设计真正无障碍的数字解决方案。在这些环境中，无障碍通常被视为合规要求而非创新机会。通过分析巴西一家科技公司的14份基于LLM的无障碍项目提案以及与9名参与者进行的焦点小组讨论，我们发现，当倡议由残障人士（PWD）自己领导时，包容性创新尤其可能出现。如果组织采用类似的参与式方法，无障碍将从事后考虑演变为技术卓越和文化变革的驱动力。

Original abstract: Developers often struggle to design truly accessible digital solutions in corporate environments. In these environments, accessibility is usually treated as a compliance requirement rather than an innovation opportunity. By analyzing 14 LLM-based accessibility project proposals and focus group discussions with 9 participants at a Brazilian tech company, we found that inclusive innovation can emerge particularly when initiatives are led by People with Disabilities (PWD) themselves. If organizations adopt similar participatory approaches, accessibility would evolve from an afterthought into a driving force for technological excellence and cultural transformation.

</details>


### [2] [Communication Skills in Software Engineering: A Multivocal Review](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10320v1)
*Dannilo Rabelo,Deisy Peres,Emmanuel Dias,Thayssa Rocha,Enne Rebeca de Freitas,Kiev Gama,Gustavo Pinto*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过多语言文献综述，发现学术和灰色文献均视沟通为软件工程核心能力，但侧重点不同：学术侧重概念化与实证，灰色文献侧重实践后果与行业趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 沟通技巧在软件工程中的讨论分散于学术和灰色文献，阻碍了对其重要性的全面理解。

Method: 采用多语言文献综述方法，系统比较学术和灰色文献。

Result: 学术和灰色文献在将沟通视为核心能力上高度一致；差异在于学术强调概念化和实证证据，而灰色文献强调实际后果和新兴行业实践。

Conclusion: 需要弥合学术与行业视角，以更全面理解沟通在软件工程中的角色。

中文摘要：沟通技巧在软件工程中越来越被认可为必不可少，然而关于它们的讨论在学术和灰色文献中仍然分散。这种分散是有问题的，因为它限制了对沟通在教育和工作环境中如何被重视、教授和应用的更广泛理解。通过多语言文献综述，我们发现学术和灰色来源在将沟通视为核心能力方面有强烈的一致性，同时也发现了侧重点的差异，学术界侧重于概念化和实证证据，而灰色文献强调实际后果和新兴行业实践。

Original abstract: Communication skills are increasingly recognized as essential in Software Engineering, yet discussions about them remain fragmented across academic and gray literature. This fragmentation is problematic because it limits a broader understanding of how communication is valued, taught, and applied in both educational and professional settings. Through a multivocal literature review, we found strong convergence between academic and gray sources in treating communication as a core competency, while also identifying differences in emphasis, with academia focusing on conceptualization and empirical evidence and gray literature stressing practical consequences and emerging industry practices.

</details>


### [3] [Beyond Coverage and Kill Scores: Empirically Measuring Test Suite Behavioural Gaps](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10417v1)
*Partha Protim Paul,Reid Holmes*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出自动化方法从文档和代码中提取预期行为并识别测试缺口，实验发现17.5%预期行为未测试，且行为覆盖率独立于代码覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统测试度量（如代码覆盖率）以实现为中心，无法检测预期行为与实际行为之间的差距，需要新方法来发现这些缺口。

Method: 从自然语言文档和源代码中提取预期的方法级行为，映射到现有测试用例，通过比对识别未测试的行为。

Result: 在10个Java库（8,922个方法）中提取20,729个行为，精确率93.1%；保守估计17.5%预期行为未测试；EVOSUITE和ASTER分别遗漏20.6%和27.1%；大多数未测试行为发生在高行覆盖率或高变异得分的方法中。

Conclusion: 行为覆盖率是测试充分性的独立维度，可补充传统结构度量，用于更全面地评估测试套件质量。

中文摘要：传统的测试充分性度量衡量的是系统的实现，而不是系统是否遵循其预期行为。尽管开发者严重依赖代码覆盖率和变异测试来评估测试套件的质量，但这些度量本质上是以实现为中心的，无法检测代码预期行为与实际行为之间的差距。不幸的是，此前一直没有可靠的方法来检测这些差异；在本文中，我们引入了一种自动化的概念验证方法以调查这些差距。该方法从自然语言文档和源代码中提取预期的方法级行为，将它们映射到现有的测试用例，并识别预期行为与已验证行为之间的差距。我们在十个流行的开源Java库（共包含8,922个方法）上评估了该方法，提取了20,729个行为，精确率为93.1%。我们的实证分析保守估计，17.5%的检测到的预期行为完全未被测试，我们将其称为测试套件的行为差距。为了确定这些差距是否仅仅是人类驱动测试的产物，我们评估了最先进的自动化测试生成器（EVOSUITE / ASTER），发现它们同样未能验证至少20.6% / 27.1%的检测到的预期行为。我们进一步证明，行为差距无法由传统结构度量预测：大多数未测试的行为发生在已经具有高行覆盖率的函数中，超过一半发生在高变异得分函数中。这些结果表明，行为覆盖率作为测试套件充分性的一个独立维度，可以补充传统的结构度量。

Original abstract: Traditional test adequacy metrics measure a system's implementation, not whether it adheres to its expected behaviour. While developers rely heavily on code coverage and mutation testing to assess test suite quality, these metrics are fundamentally implementation-centric and cannot detect gaps between what the code is expected to do and what it actually does. Unfortunately, there has been no way to reliably detect these discrepancies; in this paper we introduce an automated proof-of-concept approach to investigate these gaps. The approach extracts expected method-level behaviours from natural language documentation and source code, maps them to existing test cases, and identifies gaps between expected and validated behaviours. We evaluate the approach across ten popular open-source Java libraries comprising 8,922 methods, extracting 20,729 behaviours with 93.1% precision. Our empirical analysis conservatively estimates that 17.5% of detected expected behaviours remain entirely untested, which we term as the test suite's behavioural gap. To determine if these gaps are merely an artifact of human-driven testing, we evaluate state-of-the-art automated test generators (EVOSUITE / ASTER), finding that they similarly fail to validate at least 20.6% / 27.1% of detected expected behaviours. We further demonstrate that behavioural gaps are not predicted by traditional structural metrics: the majority of untested behaviours occur in methods that already have high line coverage, and over half persist in methods with high mutation kill score. These results suggest behavioural coverage acts as an independent dimension of test suite adequacy that can complement traditional structural metrics.

</details>


### [4] [MASTOR: A Multi-Agent Approach to Semantic Test Oracle Generation for RESTful APIs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10465v1)
*Sida Deng,Rubing Huang,Zhenzhen Yang,Man Zhang,Xuan Xie,Rongcun Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出MASTOR，一个多智能体方法，基于源代码为RESTful API生成语义测试预言，包括源码分析和预言生成两阶段，通过挑战者代理评审和规范化生成更有效的预言。在13个开源项目上评估，获得75.4%突变得分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RESTful API测试方法仅依赖简单检查，无法检测语义错误、业务逻辑违规和状态依赖不一致。

Method: MASTOR包含源码分析和预言生成两个阶段。源码分析阶段通过源码提取代理构建每个端点操作的源码上下文；预言生成阶段有两条并行路径：单操作路径生成状态和字段预言，多操作路径生成行为一致性预言。两条路径都经过挑战者代理评审和规范化。

Result: 在13个开源项目（296个操作，251k行代码）上评估，平均突变得分75.4%，生成10,022个预言。比Direct Prompting高30.1pp，比SATORI高49.4pp。

Conclusion: MASTOR通过基于源代码的多智能体方法有效生成语义测试预言，显著优于现有方法。

中文摘要：现有的自动化RESTful API测试方法通常依赖于简单的检查（如HTTP状态码、模式一致性），这不足以检测语义错误、业务逻辑违规和状态依赖的不一致性。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了MASTOR，一种基于实现源代码为RESTful API生成语义测试预言的多智能体方法。MASTOR包含两个阶段：源码分析和预言生成。前者使用源码提取代理，通过分析相关源文件的传递导入闭包，为每个端点操作构建一个源码上下文。后者在收集的上下文上采用两条并行的预言生成路径：单操作路径，为每个操作生成状态和字段预言；多操作路径，通过利用跨操作语义关联为操作序列生成行为一致性预言。两条路径都应用挑战者代理评审，其中专门的评审者识别弱点并发出改进提示以指导有针对性的重新生成，随后进行预言规范化以过滤结构上无效的预言。我们在来自WFD和PRAB数据集的13个开源RESTful API项目（296个操作，251,303行代码）的基准上评估了MASTOR。MASTOR实现了平均75.4%的变异得分，生成了10,022个预言。这些预言通过ToJUnit和ToPostmanAssertify转换为可执行的断言，并通过ToReadable转换为人类可读的描述。在50个选定操作的基线比较中，MASTOR比Direct Prompting高出30.1个百分点（69.9% vs. 39.8%），比SATORI高出49.4个百分点（69.9% vs. 20.5%）。

Original abstract: Existing automated RESTful API testing approaches commonly rely on simple checks (e.g., HTTP status codes, schema conformance), which are insufficient for detecting semantic faults, business logic violations, and state-dependent inconsistencies. To address this, we propose MASTOR, a Multi-Agent approach for generating Semantic Test Oracles for RESTful APIs based on implementation source code. MASTOR consists of two phases: source analysis and oracle generation. The former employs a source extraction agent to construct a source context for each endpoint operation by analyzing a transitive import closure of relevant source files. The latter employs two parallel oracle-generation paths over the collected contexts: a single-operation path producing status and field oracles per operation, and a multi-operation path generating behavioral consistency oracles for operation sequences by leveraging cross-operation semantic associations. Both paths apply a challenger-agent review, where a dedicated reviewer identifies weaknesses and issues improvement hints to guide targeted regeneration, followed by oracle normalization to filter out structurally invalid oracles. We evaluated MASTOR on a benchmark of 13 open-source RESTful API projects (296 operations, 251,303 lines of code) from the WFD and PRAB datasets. MASTOR achieved an average mutation score of 75.4%, generating 10,022 oracles. These oracles were translated into executable assertions via ToJUnit and ToPostmanAssertify, and into human-readable descriptions via ToReadable. In a baseline comparison on 50 selected operations, MASTOR outperformed Direct Prompting by 30.1 percentage points (69.9% vs. 39.8%) and SATORI by 49.4 percentage points (69.9% vs. 20.5%).

</details>


### [5] [Exploring and Complementing End Users' Requirements in IoT enabled System](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10598v1)
*Haotian Li,Xiaohong Chen,Zhi Jin,Shuyuan Xiao,Chenxu Wang,Haoxiang Yan,Xiaoyi Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出意图驱动的需求补全方法，通过双向可追溯树和多智能体框架，显著提升规则补全率并减少逻辑冲突。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 用户创建的物联网自动化规则碎片化，只描述设备操作而非意图，导致条件缺失、逻辑冲突和安全问题。

Method: 提出双向需求可追溯树三层模型和多智能体框架，结合LLM推理与结构化可追溯性，实现从碎片规则重建意图再生成规则并嵌入安全。

Result: 规则补全率提高43%，逻辑冲突减少21%以上，优于基线。

Conclusion: 意图驱动的方法将范式从用户责任转向系统责任，从功能正确性转向整体可信赖性。

中文摘要：最终用户通过触发器-动作编程创建物联网自动化规则，但他们的表达往往是碎片化的，捕捉设备操作而非高层次意图。这种差距导致条件缺失、逻辑冲突以及忽视安全约束，从而引发危险行为。为解决此问题，我们提出了一种意图驱动的需求补全方法，将规则补全重构为双重过程：从碎片化规则中重建意图，然后从该意图重新生成规则，并全程嵌入安全性。我们引入了双向需求可追溯树，这是一个三层模型，连接规则、意图和质量关注点，并设计了一个多智能体框架，结合大语言模型推理与结构化可追溯性。这使得补全既能功能完备又固有安全，同时保持可追溯性和可解释性。评估表明，我们的方法显著优于基线，规则补全率提高了43%，逻辑冲突减少了超过21%。通过将补全建立在意图理解之上，我们将范式从用户责任转向系统责任，从功能正确性转向整体可信赖性。

Original abstract: End users create IoT automation rules via trigger action programming, but their expressions are often fragmented, capturing device operations rather than high level intents. This gap leads to missing conditions, logical conflicts, and overlooked safety constraints, risking hazardous behaviors. To address this, we propose an intent driven requirements completion approach that reframes rule completion as a dual process: reconstructing intent from fragmented rules, then regenerating rules from that intent, with safety embedded throughout. We introduce a Bidirectional Requirements Traceability Tree, a three layer model linking rules, intents, and quality concerns, and design a multiagent framework that combines LLM reasoning with structured traceability. This enables completions that are both functionally complete and inherently safe, while remaining traceable and explainable. Evaluation shows our method significantly outperforms the baselines, improving the rule completion rate by 43% and reducing logical conflicts by over 21%. By grounding completion in intent understanding, we shift the paradigm from user to system responsibility, and from functional correctness to holistic trustworthiness.

</details>


### [6] [Watts and Debts of Agentic Frameworks: An Empirical Study (Registered Report)](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10702v1)
*Aneetta Sara Shany,Chandrasekar S,Karthik Vaidhyanathan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过验证性实验探究自我承认的技术债务与智能体框架运行时能耗之间的相关性，以评估代码质量是否能为能源高效的框架选择提供早期预警。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 每个投入生产的智能体AI系统都隐藏着累积的技术债务和未监控的运行时能源成本，而内部结构质量与动态能耗之间的经验关联尚未被探索，造成可持续性和运营预算管理的盲点。

Method: 评估五个开源智能体框架，在受控环境中执行标准化任务套件；通过自动化Python注释挖掘提取SATD，利用微调提示的LLM进行分类；在硬件级别测量运行时能耗；调查三个核心研究问题（技术债务存在性、能耗架构差异、债务与能耗的统计相关性）。

Result: 研究将建立技术债务与运行时能耗之间的统计相关性，验证自动化源代码分析能否作为能源高效框架选择的可靠早期预警代理。

Conclusion: 研究结果将确定自动化源代码分析是否可以作为能源高效框架选择的可靠早期预警代理，从而促进绿色软件工程和智能体AI质量研究。

中文摘要：背景：每个投入生产环境的智能体AI系统都隐藏着两个风险：累积的技术债务和未监控的运行时能源成本。虽然功能基准测试很常见，但内部结构质量（特别是技术债务）与执行过程中动态能耗之间的经验关联尚未被探索，这给管理可持续性和大规模运营预算的从业者和组织带来了盲点。目标：我们提出一项验证性实证研究，将自我承认的技术债务（SATD）与智能体框架的硬件级运行时能耗关联起来，以确定代码质量能否驱动能源意识的设计决策。方法：我们将通过在严格受控的环境中执行标准化任务套件来评估五个开源智能体框架。SATD将通过基于Python的自动注释挖掘提取，并通过使用微调提示的基于LLM的分类进行分类，而运行时能耗将在硬件级别测量。我们的研究将调查三个核心研究问题：（RQ1）这些框架中是否存在技术债务；（RQ2）不同架构间运行时能耗的差异；（RQ3）框架的技术债务与其任务级能耗之间的统计相关性。结论：研究结果将确定自动化源代码分析是否可以作为能源高效框架选择的可靠早期预警代理，从而促进绿色软件工程和智能体AI质量研究。

Original abstract: Context: Every agentic AI system shipped to production carries two hidden risks: accumulated Technical Debt (TD) and unmonitored runtime energy costs. While functional benchmarking is common, the empirical link between internal structural quality (specifically TD) and dynamic energy consumption during execution remains unexplored, creating a blind spot for practitioners and organizations managing sustainability and operational budgets at scale. Goal: We propose a confirmatory empirical study correlating Self-Admitted Technical Debt (SATD) with hardware-level runtime energy consumption across agentic frameworks, to determine whether code quality can drive energy-aware design decisions. Method: We will evaluate five open-source agentic frameworks by executing a standardized task suite in a strictly controlled environment. SATD will be extracted via automated Python-based comment mining and categorized via LLM-based classification using fine-tuned prompt, while runtime energy will be measured at the hardware level. Our study will investigate three core research questions: (RQ1) the presence of TD within these frameworks; (RQ2) the variance in runtime energy consumption across architectures; and (RQ3) the statistical correlation between a framework's TD and its task-level energy consumption. Conclusion: The findings will establish whether automated source code analysis can serve as a reliable, early-warning proxy for energy-efficient framework selection, thereby advancing both green software engineering and agentic AI quality research.

</details>


### [7] [DeNovoSWE: Scaling Long-Horizon Environments for Generating Entire Repositories from Scratch](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10728v2)
*Jiale Zhao,Guoxin Chen,Fanzhe Meng,Wayne Xin Zhao,Ruihua Song,Ji-Rong Wen,Kai Jia*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出DeNovoSWE数据集及自动构建方法，微调模型将长周期SWE基准性能从5.8%提升至47.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏大规模、可验证的完整仓库生成数据，难以训练长周期软件工程代理。

Method: 通过沙盒代理工作流自动生成数据集，采用分治与批评-修复策略，并引入难度感知轨迹过滤。

Result: 微调Qwen3-30B-A3B后，在BeyondSWE-Doc2Repo基准上得分从5.8%提升至47.2%。

Conclusion: DeNovoSWE可有效提升LLM代理的完整仓库生成能力，自动化构建方案具备可扩展性。

中文摘要：随着基于大语言模型的代码代理能力不断增强，其预期角色正从现有代码库中的局部错误修复扩展到根据高级规范设计和实现完整的软件仓库。然而，对此类长周期软件工程任务进行代理训练仍然困难，因为缺乏大规模、可验证的完整仓库生成数据。在本文中，我们引入了DeNovoSWE，一个用于完整仓库生成的大规模数据集。DeNovoSWE包含4,818个高质量实例，每个实例需要根据文档生成完整的仓库。我们的数据集通过精心设计的沙盒代理工作流自动构建，无需人工标注即可实现可扩展的整理。DeNovoSWE采用“分而治之”和批评-修复的理念构建。为了平衡数据质量和多样性，我们进一步引入了难度感知的轨迹过滤策略。在DeNovoSWE上微调Qwen3-30B-A3B显著提升了长周期软件工程性能，在具有挑战性的BeyondSWE-Doc2Repo基准测试上，其得分从5.8%提高到47.2%。

Original abstract: As the capabilities of LLM-based code agents continue to advance, their expected role is expanding beyond localized bug fixing in existing codebases toward architecting and implementing complete software repositories from high-level specifications. However, training agents for such long-horizon software engineering tasks remains difficult due to the scarcity of large-scale, verifiable whole-repository generation data. In this paper, we introduce \textbf{DeNovoSWE}, a large-scale dataset for whole-repository generation. DeNovoSWE comprises 4,818 high-quality instances, where each instance requires generating a complete repository from documentation. Our dataset is automatically constructed through a carefully designed sandboxed agentic workflow, enabling scalable curation without human annotation. DeNovoSWE is constructed with "divide and conquer" and critic-repair philosophy. To balance data quality and diversity, we further introduce a difficulty-aware trajectory filtering strategy. Fine-tuning Qwen3-30B-A3B on DeNovoSWE substantially improves long-horizon SWE performance, raising its score on the challenging BeyondSWE-Doc2Repo benchmark from 5.8% to 47.2%.

Original abstract: The rapid advancement of autonomous driving systems (ADS) has introduced significant challenges, particularly in the creation of realistic and complex scenarios for testing and validation. This paper introduces Modular2Simple, a tool designed to address these challenges by simplifying and enhancing the process of creating complex ADS scenarios. Modular2Simple seamlessly integrates with the CARLA simulator and is applicable to any software that supports the OpenSCENARIO format. By leveraging existing simple scenarios in the OpenSCENARIO format, the tool enables developers to create easily customizable modular scenarios through the combination of multiple simple or modular scenarios, significantly simplifying the scenario creation process while maintaining flexibility in scenario design. This approach not only facilitates the development of complex scenarios, reducing both development time and effort, but also promotes scenario reuse and customization, which leads to a significant reduction in code complexity and enhanced efficiency in scenario design and testing compared to traditional scenario development methods.

### [9] [From Perception to Action: Can UI Interventions Foster Sustainable LLM Chatbot](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10861v1)
*Nitish Patkar,Pooja Rani,Jack Glässer,Simon Lüscher,Martin Kropp*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 面向可持续性的用户界面干预（如模式切换和能源反馈）能提高用户对AI能源使用的意识，并促使他们更频繁地选择节能模式，从而在不降低可用性的情况下支持更节能的聊天机器人交互。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有缓解LLM聊天机器人能源消耗的策略主要集中在模型或基础设施效率上，而用户界面层具有塑造用户交互行为的潜力却未被充分探索，因此研究旨在探索UI干预能否在保持可用性的同时提高能源意识和促进节能行为。

Method: 首先进行77人的基线调查评估意识和接受度；然后基于说服技术和选择架构设计了一个包含三模式开关、响应能源反馈、发送前估计、仪表板和能源类比的原型；最后在11人参与的为期五天的实地研究中评估效果。

Result: 基线调查中88.3%误估能耗，仅39%愿为节能牺牲性能；实地研究中节能模式占55.8%提示，90.9%在不需要高准确性时主动选择节能模式，提示长度未减少，模式切换为主要行为机制。

Conclusion: 面向可持续性的UI干预能提高能源意识并支持更节能的交互模式，这些效应作为行为和模型估计补充后端效率工作，原型和复制包促进进一步研究。

中文摘要：基于LLM的聊天机器人越来越多地嵌入到日常工作中，其能源使用引发了可持续性问题。大多数缓解策略侧重于模型或基础设施效率，而用户界面层尽管具有塑造交互行为的潜力，但仍未得到充分探索。我们调查了面向可持续性的用户界面干预是否能提高用户的能源意识，并鼓励更节能的聊天机器人使用，同时不降低可用性。我们首先进行了一项基线调查，有77名参与者评估对干预概念的意识和接受度。受先前关于说服技术和选择架构的工作启发，我们实现了一个基于网页的聊天机器人原型，具有三模式切换（节能、平衡、性能）、每次响应能源反馈、发送前能源估计、使用指标仪表板和能源类比。然后我们在一项为期五天的实地研究中评估了该原型，有11名参与者。在基线调查中，94.8%的受访者报告至少对AI能源使用有一定意识，但88.3%的人错误估计了实际消耗。尽管对环境影响担忧很高，只有39.0%表示愿意接受性能权衡以降低能源使用。在实地研究中，节能模式占记录提示的55.8%，而90.9%自我报告在不需要高准确性时主动选择节能模式。参与者没有减少提示长度，这表明模式切换是主要的行为机制。面向可持续性的用户界面干预可以提高意识并支持LLM聊天机器人中更节能的交互模式。这些效应最好被解释为行为和基于模型的估计，补充后端效率工作，所提供的原型和复制包支持进一步研究能源感知的对话式AI设计。

Original abstract: LLM-powered chatbots are increasingly embedded in everyday workflows, raising sustainability concerns due to their energy use. Most mitigation strategies emphasize model or infrastructure efficiency, while the user-interface (UI) layer remains underexplored despite its potential to shape interaction behavior. We investigate whether sustainability-oriented UI interventions can increase users' energy awareness and encourage more energy-responsible chatbot use without reducing usability. We first conducted a baseline survey with 77 participants to assess awareness and receptiveness to intervention concepts. Guided by prior work on persuasive technology and choice architecture, we implemented a web-based chatbot prototype with a three-mode switch (Energy-efficient, Balanced, Performance), per-response energy feedback, pre-send energy estimates, a usage metrics dashboard, and energy analogies. We then evaluated the prototype in a five-day field study with 11 participants. In the baseline survey, 94.8% of respondents reported at least some awareness of AI energy use, yet 88.3% misestimated actual consumption. Although concern about environmental impact was high, only 39.0% indicated willingness to accept a performance trade-off for lower energy use. In the field study, Energy-efficient mode accounted for 55.8% of logged prompts, while 90.9% self-reported actively choosing Eco-mode when high accuracy was not required. Participants did not reduce prompt length, suggesting mode switching as the primary behavioral mechanism. Sustainability-oriented UI interventions can improve awareness and support more energy-responsible interaction patterns in LLM chatbots. These effects are best interpreted as behavioral and model-based estimates that complement backend efficiency work, and the provided prototype and replication package support further research on energy-aware conversational AI design.

### [10] [Writing Better Software Explanations: A Guideline-Based Approach](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10880v1)
*Martin Obaidi,Jean-Carl Kremser,Hannah Deters,Jakob Droste,Marc Herrmann,Kurt Schneider*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合LLM和质量指南的软件解释表述支持工具，通过两阶段评估显示工具支持能提高效率和用户满意度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确保自然语言解释的一致性、相关性和良好表述仍然是一个主要挑战，纯自动LLM生成缺乏可靠性和可控性。

Method: 开发了指南驱动的表述支持工具，结合LLM文本生成和经验质量指南，将写作过程分为生成、质量检查和迭代修订，保留开发者的领域控制。通过两阶段研究：开发者实验和用户调查进行评估。

Result: 工具支持表述平均快24.4%（仅趋势），用户调查中工具支持的解释满意度显著高于手动（p=0.003，秩双列相关系数=0.86）。

Conclusion: 指南驱动的LLM辅助可能带来效率提升和更高的感知表述质量，未来需研究长期工业使用和集成。

中文摘要：随着软件系统越来越依赖自然语言解释来满足需求沟通和支持中用户报告的解释需求，确保这些解释一致、相关且表述良好仍然是一个主要挑战。完全自动的大型语言模型（LLM）生成往往缺乏可靠的依据和可控的输出质量。在本文中，我们提出了一种基于指南的软件解释表述支持工具，该工具将LLM辅助文本生成与经验得出的质量指南相结合。该工具将写作过程结构化为生成、质量检查和迭代修订，同时将领域控制权保留给开发者。我们通过一个由基于访谈的开发者实验和受控用户调查组成的两阶段研究评估了该方法。六名具有软件开发或DevOps经验的行业从业者在纯人工手动条件和人机LLM支持条件下为真实的解释需求制定了解释。在这个小规模评估中，工具支持的表述平均快24.4%，尽管推断性分析仅显示出效率趋势。在后续的17名参与者和204个配对比较的用户研究中，工具支持的解释在总体满意度上显著高于手动解释（p=0.003，秩双列相关系数=0.86）。我们的发现表明，通过指南驱动的LLM辅助，可以实现潜在效率提升和更高的表述质量感知。未来的工作应检查长期工业使用和与现有开发工作流程的集成。

Original abstract: As software systems increasingly rely on natural-language explanations to address user-reported explanation needs in requirements communication and support, ensuring that such explanations are consistent, relevant, and well formulated remains a major challenge. Purely automatic large language model (LLM) generation often lacks reliable grounding and controllable output quality. In this paper, we present a guideline-based formulation support tool for software explanations that combines LLM-assisted text generation with an empirically derived quality guideline. The tool structures the writing process into generation, quality checking, and iterative revision, while keeping domain control with developers. We evaluated the approach in a two-phase study consisting of an interview-based developer experiment and a controlled user survey. Six industry practitioners with software development or DevOps experience formulated explanations for real explanation needs in a human-only manual condition and in a human-with-LLM-support condition. In this small-scale evaluation, tool-supported formulation was on average 24.4% faster, although inferential analyses indicated only a trend for efficiency. In a subsequent user study with 17 participants and 204 paired comparisons, tool-supported explanations were rated significantly higher in overall satisfaction than manual explanations (p=0.003, rank-biserial correlation=0.86). Our findings suggest potential efficiency gains and higher perceived formulation quality through guideline-driven LLM assistance. Future work should examine long-term industrial use and integration into existing development workflows.

### [11] [From Quality Properties to Practice: A Guideline and Workflow for Explainability Requirements](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10882v1)
*Martin Obaidi,Jakob Droste,Hannah Deters,Marc Herrmann,Michel Krahl,Kurt Schneider*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出基于指南的工作流和工具制定可解释性需求，评估表明可减少时间且质量与手动相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可解释性需求常被临时编写，无指导的LLM支持易产生模糊或不一致，需要系统化方法。

Method: 通过文献综述和访谈获取候选属性，在线调查优先级排序形成10个核心属性的指南，开发支持迭代修订的网络工具，并在两个实验（需求工程师工作坊和软件开发人员在线研究）中评估。

Result: 工作坊中工具支持减少23.5%制定时间（p=0.021）；在线研究中工具支持与手动编写的需求在可实施性和质量上评分相当，描述性上略有偏好工具支持版本。

Conclusion: 结合优先化质量指南与轻量级LLM支持可减少制定工作量，同时保持需求质量与手动编写相当。

中文摘要：可解释性在AI赋能的软件系统中越来越被要求以支持透明度、用户信任和合规性。然而，可解释性需求通常是临时编写的，而未经指导的大型语言模型支持可能会产生模糊、不一致或不完整的陈述。本文提出了一种顺序的、指南驱动的工作流程，用于制定可解释性需求，并评估了其基于工具的操作化。我们首先通过结构化文献综述和开发者访谈引出候选质量属性。然后，我们在一个在线调查中与从业者（n=20）对这些属性进行优先级排序，并得出了一个包含十个核心属性的简明指南，以及可操作的制定说明。接下来，我们将该指南操作化为一个基于网络的工具，支持起草、基于属性的检查和修订的迭代工作流程。我们在两个互补的研究中评估了该工作流程。在一个与需求工程师（n=6）的工作坊中，工具支持平均减少了23.5%的制定时间（Wilcoxon p=0.021）。在一个与软件开发人员（n=18）的独立在线研究中，工具支持和手动编写的需求在可实施性和制定质量方面获得了可比较的评分，描述性上略有偏好工具支持版本的倾向。总体而言，我们的结果表明，将优先化的质量指南与轻量级LLM支持相结合，可以减少制定工作量，同时产生与手动编写的需求感知相当的需求。

Original abstract: Explainability is increasingly required in AI-enabled software systems to support transparency, user trust, and compliance. Yet, explainability requirements are often written ad hoc, and unguided large language model support can yield vague, inconsistent, or incomplete statements. This paper presents a sequential, guideline-driven workflow for formulating explainability requirements and evaluates its tool-based operationalization. We first elicited candidate quality properties through a structured literature review and developer interviews. We then prioritized these properties in an online survey with practitioners (n=20) and derived a concise guideline of ten core properties with actionable formulation instructions. Next, we operationalized the guideline in a web-based tool that supports an iterative workflow of drafting, property-based checks, and revision. We evaluated the workflow in two complementary studies. In a workshop with requirements engineers (n=6), tool support reduced formulation time by 23.5% on average (Wilcoxon p=0.021). In an independent online study with software developers (n=18), tool-supported and manually written requirements received comparable ratings for implementability and formulation quality, with a descriptive slight preference tendency toward the tool-supported versions. Overall, our results suggest that combining a prioritized quality guideline with lightweight LLM support can reduce formulation effort while producing requirements that are perceived comparably to manually written ones.

### [12] [Early Comparative Evaluation of Transformer Models for Multilingual Software Vulnerability Detection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10925v1)
*Fiza Naseer,Javad Khan,Muhammad Yaqoob,Alexios Mylonas*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代应用多语言混合，现有漏洞检测方法缺乏针对多语言的系统评估，需要探索不同预训练模型的效果。

Method: 使用CVEFixes数据集，对BERT、RoBERTa和CodeBERT在HTML、Python、JavaScript、PHP四种语言上进行三折分层交叉验证的二进制漏洞检测实验。

Result: 不同语言上模型性能存在明显差异，没有单一模型在所有语言上表现最优。

Conclusion: 多语言漏洞检测需要开发更具语言意识和鲁棒性的transformer建模策略，以应对跨语言性能差异。

Original abstract: Software vulnerability detection is increasingly important as modern applications combine multiple programming languages. ### [13] [GapFuzz: Cross-Plane Divergence Fuzzing for Distributed SDN Controllers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11035v2)
*Moustapha Awwalou Diouf,Samuel Ouya,Jacques Klein,Tegawendé F. Bissyandé*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: GapFuzz是一种针对分布式SDN集群的状态并发模糊测试工具，通过注入冲突请求并重构跨平面状态，有效检测因异步复制导致的控制平面与数据平面分歧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SDN模糊测试工具局限于控制平面、针对单控制器或未引导并发，无法发现分布式SDN集群中因异步复制引起的跨平面状态不一致问题。

Method: GapFuzz在两个非主节点上以可控延迟注入成对冲突北向请求，通过查询所有副本和内核数据路径重构全局跨平面状态；采用两阶段时间搜索检测分歧并界定注入窗口，生命周期探测将结果分类。

Result: 在三节点ONOS 2.7集群上，81.7%的尝试产生分歧结果，其中99.4%持续超过30秒；第二阶段识别出5毫秒竞争窗口和六种倍增上限模式；使用用户空间探针替换内核探针导致检测率下降26.6至46.5个百分点。

Conclusion: GapFuzz能有效发现分布式SDN集群中的跨平面状态分歧，且内核数据路径探测对检测至关重要。

中文摘要：分布式软件定义网络（SDN）集群在主节点与其备份节点之间异步复制流状态，这留下了一个窗口期，期间两个备份节点可以各自提交一条冲突规则，主节点可以将两者序列化到数据平面，并且内核数据路径可以锁定到一个没有节点认为是权威的操作。现有的SDN模糊测试工具未能发现此故障：它们将预测限制在控制平面，针对单个控制器，或者不引导并发以引发复制竞争。

我们提出GapFuzz，一种用于分布式SDN集群的状态并发模糊测试工具。GapFuzz在两个非主节点上以可控的注入间延迟Δt注入成对的冲突北向请求，并通过ovs-appctl ofproto/trace查询每个副本和内核数据路径动作来重构全局跨平面状态。两阶段时间搜索检测是否存在分歧，然后对Δt进行倍增和二分法以界定注入时间窗口；生命周期探测将每个结果标记为瞬时或持久，并将其归类为源自ONOS 2.7源代码的四个跨平面状态类别之一。

在一个三节点ONOS 2.7集群上，GapFuzz在81.7%的尝试中产生分歧结果（N=50，Wilson 95%置信区间[77.3, 85.4]%）；每个分歧都位于集群权威状态与内核数据路径之间。第二阶段将一个模板的5毫秒竞争窗口与其他六个模板的倍增上限制度（Δt_max=10.24秒）区分开来，99.4%的分歧持续超过30秒。用先前模糊测试工具使用的OpenFlow用户空间探测替换内核数据路径探测，整体检测率下降26.6个百分点，排除规范化强制结果后下降46.5个百分点。

Original abstract: Distributed Software-Defined Networking (SDN) clusters replicate flow state asynchronously between a master node and its backups, leaving a window during which two backup nodes can each commit a contradictory rule, the master can serialize both into the data plane, and the kernel datapath can latch onto an action that no node believes authoritative. Existing SDN fuzzers miss this fault: they confine their oracle to the control plane, target a single controller, or do not steer concurrency to provoke replication races.
  We present GapFuzz, a stateful concurrency fuzzer for distributed SDN clusters. GapFuzz injects pairs of contradictory Northbound requests on two non-master nodes with controlled inter-injection delay $Δt$, and reconstructs the global cross-plane state by querying every replica and the kernel-datapath action through ovs-appctl ofproto/trace. A two-phase timing search detects whether a divergence exists, then doubles and bisects on $Δt$ to bound the injection-time window; a lifetime probe labels each verdict transient or persistent and assigns it to one of four cross-plane state classes derived from the ONOS 2.7 source.
  On a three-node ONOS 2.7 cluster, GapFuzz produces a divergent verdict in 81.7% of attempts ($N=50$, Wilson 95% CI $[77.3, 85.4]$%); every divergence sits between the cluster's authoritative state and the kernel datapath. Phase 2 separates a 5 ms race window for one template from a doubling-cap regime ($Δt_{\max}=10.24$ s) for six others, and 99.4% of divergences persist past 30 s. Replacing the kernel-datapath probe with the OpenFlow user-space probe used by prior fuzzers drops detection by 26.6 percentage points overall and by 46.5 points after excluding canonicalization-forced verdicts.

</details>


### [14] [Making Software Meaningful](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11051v1)
*Eagon Meng,Abutalib Namazov,Carmel Schare,Alcino Cunha,Daniel Jackson*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出通过承诺明确含义（单一共享行为表示）来改善软件质量，并给出三个领域的应用实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前软件开发中可用性、模块化和问责性不足，需要一种统一的方法来协调利益相关者。

Method: 构建并约定软件在应用域中的行为表示，将现象（个体、行动、事实）组织成概念，作为共同词汇。

Result: 在三个领域展示效果：可用性设计（用户与设计师对齐）、LLM生成模块化代码（含义到代码映射）、代理问责（行为准则）。

Conclusion: 承诺明确含义能同时提升可用性、模块化和问责性，具有广泛适用性。

中文摘要：采用单一措施可以提高软件的可使用性、模块化和问责性：对明确含义的承诺。这包括构建并就软件在应用领域中的行为表示达成一致。构成该行为的现象成为基础词汇，用于所有利益相关者之间关于软件的所有讨论，以及所有制品和活动。这些现象是个体；它们参与的行动；以及行动产生的事实。通过划分行动集合，可以将这些现象组织成概念，提供更大的含义单元。给出了利用含义的三个例子：设计可用性（通过将用户和设计师对齐到单一共享含义）；使用LLM生成模块化代码（通过将含义单元映射到代码单元，不仅实现模块化还实现可读性）；以及使代理负责（通过让它们遵守定义其预期行为的行为准则）。

Original abstract: Adopting a single measure can improve the usability, modularity and accountability of software: a commitment to explicit meaning. This entails constructing and agreeing upon a representation of the behavior of the software, as observed in the domain of application. The phenomena comprising this behavior become a vocabulary that grounds all discourse about the software, among all stakeholders, and for all artifacts and activities. These phenomena are individuals; actions they participate in; and facts that result from actions. They can be organized, by partitioning the set of actions, into concepts, offering larger units of meaning. Examples of exploiting meaning are given in three areas: designing for usability (by aligning user and designer on a single shared meaning); generating modular code with LLMs (by mapping units of meaning to units of code, achieving not only modularity but also legibility); and making agents accountable (by having them adhere to a code of conduct that defines their intended behavior).

</details>


### [15] [Operationalizing Property-Based Testing for Data-Intensive Scalable Computing Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11132v1)
*Yaoxuan Wu,Ingrid Lee,Ahmad Humayun,Muhammad Ali Gulzar,Miryung Kim*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: DiscPBT是一个针对Apache Spark的基于属性的测试引擎，通过八个元属性和生成器有效发现语义问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模糊测试的浅层预言无法捕捉DISC框架中的语义漂移和优化相关错误，而基于属性的测试虽然能解决但难以系统化。

Method: 提出DiscPBT，引入八个可重用元属性（涵盖等价重写、数据分解、计算分解和算子局部语义关系），并提供生成器和实例化框架以合成有效工作负载和数据。

Result: 在PySpark上评估，分支覆盖率是CometFuzz的1.2倍，计划多样性是1153倍，在66个属性上发现跨版本语义漂移及NaN/空输入陷阱。

Conclusion: 系统的基于属性的测试对揭示DISC框架中的语义问题具有重要价值。

中文摘要：虽然模糊测试能有效捕获崩溃，但其浅层预言通常无法捕捉数据密集型可扩展计算（DISC）框架中的语义漂移和优化相关错误。基于属性的测试（PBT）通过检查跨不同工作负载和输入的一般语义不变性，而不是依赖于特定的预期输出，来解决这一局限性。然而，系统地将PBT应用于DISC系统仍然困难，因为它既需要可重用的属性定义，也需要有效地实例化为有效的工作负载和数据。我们提出了DiscPBT，一个针对Apache Spark的基于属性的测试引擎。DiscPBT引入了八个可重用的元属性用于DISC语义测试，涵盖等价重写、数据分解、计算分解和算子局部语义关系。为了将这些元属性实例化，DiscPBT提供了可重用的生成器，用于合成有效的工作负载骨架和输入数据，以及一个实例化框架，通过兼容的算子、表达式和UDF在模式兼容的上下文中实现每个元属性。我们在PySpark上的评估表明，DiscPBT的分支覆盖率是CometFuzz的1.2倍，计划多样性是CometFuzz的1153倍。在66个具体属性上，DiscPBT揭示了跨版本语义漂移以及涉及NaN和空输入的微妙边缘情况陷阱，这些是仅基于崩溃的模糊测试无法捕获的。这些结果证明了系统的PBT在揭示DISC框架中语义问题方面的价值。

Original abstract: While fuzzing effectively catches crashes, its shallow oracles often miss semantic drifts and optimization-related errors in data-intensive scalable computing (DISC) frameworks. Property-based testing (PBT) addresses this limitation by checking general semantic invariants across diverse workloads and inputs, rather than relying on specific expected outputs. However, systematically operationalizing PBT for DISC systems remains difficult because it requires both reusable property definitions and effective instantiation into valid workloads and data.
  We present DiscPBT, a property-based testing engine for Apache Spark. DiscPBT introduces eight reusable meta-properties for DISC semantic testing, spanning equivalence rewriting, data decomposition, computation decomposition, and operator-local semantic relations. To operationalize these meta-properties, DiscPBT provides reusable generators for synthesizing valid workload skeletons and input data, together with an instantiation framework that realizes each meta-property in schema-compatible contexts through compatible operators, expressions, and UDFs.
  Our evaluation on PySpark shows that DiscPBT achieves 1.2$\times$ higher branch coverage and 1153$\times$ greater plan diversity than CometFuzz. Across 66 concrete properties, DiscPBT reveals cross-version semantic drift as well as subtle corner-case pitfalls involving NaN and empty inputs, that are not captured by crash-based fuzzing alone. These results demonstrate the value of systematic PBT for uncovering semantic issues in DISC frameworks.

</details>


### [16] [Web-Native Graphical EMF Model Editors](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11442v1)
*Susanne Göbel,Ralf Lämmel*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: EMFular是一个纯Web框架，无需后端即可管理EMF模型，通过生成Angular项目实现图形化编辑器，支持标准编辑操作、EMF一致性及与现有工具互操作，并提供可定制的扩展点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图形化模型编辑从桌面转向Web，现有框架存在生成工作量大、定制困难、部署复杂等问题，需要一种低工作量、高定制性和易部署的Web框架。

Method: 分析现有框架特性，推导设计原则，开发EMFular框架及其生成器，将Ecore模型映射为基于Angular的编辑器，利用扩展点实现定制化。

Result: EMFular编辑器支持模型创建、检查、导航、编辑、撤销/重做、包含和反向引用处理，与EMF工具集互操作；生成的项目可定制和扩展。评估显示编辑器适宜性和适应性良好，生成稳健。

Conclusion: EMFular提供了一种有效的Web图形化模型编辑方案，实现了低工作量、高定制性和易部署，适用于EMF模型管理。

中文摘要：图形化模型编辑正从桌面应用程序转向基于Web的工具。我们分析了现有框架的特性，并基于此分析，推导出一组设计原则，这些原则意味着低生成工作量、广泛的定制可能性以及所生成编辑器的直接部署。在此基础上，我们介绍了EMFular，一个纯基于Web的框架，用于管理EMF模型而无需任何后端。随附的EMFular生成器将给定的Ecore模型（一个EMF元模型）映射到一个即用型且可定制的图形化编辑器。EMFular编辑器提供“EMF一致性”，即它们不仅支持标准建模操作如创建、检查、导航、编辑和撤销/重做，而且还以紧密符合EMF的方式处理包含和反向引用；它们还通过兼容的序列化/反序列化提供与现有EMF工具集的互操作性。生成的编辑器是一个带有指定扩展点的Angular项目，这使得开发者能够利用Angular及其生态系统的表达能力，在EMFular的扩展点引导下，定制和扩展编辑器的所有方面。我们从编辑器适宜性（可用的编辑能力）、适应性（定制机制和所需工作量）以及生成的稳健性方面评估了EMFular。

Original abstract: Graphical model editing is shifting from desktop applications to web-based tools. We analyze the characteristics of existing frameworks and, based on this analysis, we derive a set of design principles that imply low-effort generation, extensive customization possibilities, and straightforward deployment of the resulting editors. On these grounds, we introduce EMFular, a purely web-based framework for managing EMF models without any backend. The accompanying EMFular generator maps a given Ecore model (an EMF metamodel) to a ready-to-use and ready-to-customize graphical editor. EMFular editors provide 'EMF consistency', that is, they not only support standard modeling operations such as creation, inspection, navigation, editing, and undo/redo, but they also handle containment and inverse references in close alignment with EMF; they also provide interoperability with existing EMF tooling through compatible de-/serialization. A generated editor is an Angular project with designated extension points, which allows developers to customize and extend all aspects of the editor using the expressive power of Angular and its ecosystem, guided by the extension points of EMFular. We evaluate EMFular in terms of editor adequacy (available editing capabilities), adaptability (customization mechanisms and required effort), and robustness of the generation.

### [17] [Defeater Cards: Characterizing and Managing Safety Assurance Case Defeaters](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11462v1)
*Usman Gohar,Michael C. Hunter,Salil Purandare,Jordan J. Rios,Myra B. Cohen,Robyn R. Lutz*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出挫败者卡片（Defeater Cards），一种结构化文档工件，用于系统性地描述和管理安全案例中的挫败者，通过案例研究展示其有效性，并开源供社区使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有挫败者概念缺乏结构化支持、描述不一致、难以审查和缺乏文档标准，需要一种系统化的方法来管理安全案例中的挫败者。

Method: 通过文献调查和主题分析，基于5W1H框架确定文档标准，设计挫败者卡片结构，并通过两个跨领域案例研究验证其适用性。

Result: 挫败者卡片能暴露隐藏假设、揭示推理漏洞，支持安全保证案例的持续演进，并实现跨系统重用。

Conclusion: 挫败者卡片是一种有效的结构化工具，可提高安全案例的批判性分析、可追溯性和可审计性，开源库有助于社区采纳和知识共享。

中文摘要：安全保证案例提供了结构化论证，说明安全关键系统满足其安全要求。最近，挫败者（defeaters）的概念作为一种严格挑战安全论证有效性的手段出现。挫败者的例子可能包括过于严格的声明、不可靠的证据或推理漏洞。然而，挫败者仍然是临时性的，缺乏结构化支持进行批判性反思，描述不一致，难以审查，并且缺乏文档标准。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了挫败者卡片（Defeater Cards），这是一种新的结构化文档工件，用于系统性地表征、推理和管理安全案例中的挫败者。通过文献调查和主题分析，我们确定了基于5W1H框架的文档标准，用于指导卡片的结构。挫败者卡片旨在支持知情分析和演进，提高可追溯性和可审计性，并实现挫败者知识在系统和产品变体中的重用。我们通过两个跨领域案例研究展示了其适用性，展示了它们如何暴露隐藏假设、揭示推理漏洞并支持安全保证案例的持续演进。为了支持采用和社区重用，我们还发布了一个开源的知识库挫败者卡片库，作为研究人员和从业者构建和描述经验教训的基线。

Original abstract: Safety assurance cases provide structured justifications that safety-critical systems meet their safety requirements. Recently, the notion of defeaters has emerged as a rigorous means of challenging the validity of safety arguments. Examples of defeaters might include overly strict claims, unreliable evidence, or reasoning gaps. However, defeaters remain ad hoc, lack structured support for critical reflection, are inconsistently described, are difficult to review, and lack documentation standards. To address this, we propose Defeater Cards, a new structured documentation artifact for systematically characterizing, reasoning about, and managing defeaters in safety cases. Drawing on a literature survey and thematic analysis, we identify documentation criteria that inform the card's structure, based on the 5W1H framework. Defeater Cards are designed to support informed analysis and evolution, improve traceability and auditability, and enable the reuse of defeater knowledge across systems and product variants. We demonstrate their applicability through two cross-domain case studies, showing how they expose hidden assumptions, surface reasoning gaps, and support ongoing safety assurance case evolution. To support adoption and community reuse, we also release an open-source repository of defeater cards as a baseline upon which researchers and practitioners can build and describe lessons learned.

### [18] [SentTrack: Sentiment-Driven Bottleneck Detection in GitHub Issue Repositories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11476v1)
*Xinyu Hu,Ali Behbahani,Daniel Moon,Yaren Dogan,Nasir U. Eisty*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出SentTrack框架，从GitHub问题讨论中检测社会技术瓶颈，发现49%线程停滞，仅13%解决，并提供加权评分工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具忽略对话动态，需要自动化检测工作流低效和早期风险。

Method: 双管道：水平管道（LLM摘要+聚类）和垂直管道（ABCDE分类），加权评分。

Result: 在9000线程中，49%停滞，13%解决，识别出解决差距为主要信号。

Conclusion: SentTrack有效检测瓶颈，提供可解释的优先级工具。

中文摘要：软件工程团队越来越依赖GitHub问题线程来协调工作、报告错误和协商技术决策，但大多数存储库健康工具关注代码指标，而忽略了推动或阻碍开发的对话动态。本文介绍了SentTrack，一个用于从GitHub问题讨论中检测社会技术瓶颈的双透镜框架。应用于AvaloniaUI开源存储库的大约9,000个问题线程，该框架解决了三个问题：如何从实时对话数据中自动化工作流低效检测，情感信号是否能够比传统的基于标签的方法更早地发现风险，以及如何在混合媒体问题文本中将人类叙述与机器生成的噪声分离。SentTrack结合了两个互补的管道。水平管道使用大型语言模型将原始问题报告转化为干净的摘要，提取中间级别的关注短语，并通过UMAP和HDBSCAN进行聚类，从首批处理的3,608个问题中产生613个语义聚类。垂直管道应用ABCDE协作交互框架对每条评论进行分类，并推断线程级别的结果。在整个语料库中，49%的线程以停滞结束，只有13%达到解决，其中解决差距被确定为主要的瓶颈信号。一个加权评分引擎结合了消极性、停滞、解决差距和线程长度，为主持人提供了一个可解释的优先级排序工具，用于在开发停滞之前识别高摩擦的讨论。

Original abstract: Software engineering teams increasingly depend on GitHub issue threads to coordinate work, report bugs, and negotiate technical decisions, yet most repository health tools focus on code metrics and ignore the conversational dynamics that drive or stall development. This paper presents SentTrack, a dual-lens framework for detecting socio-technical bottlenecks from GitHub issue discussions. Applied to the AvaloniaUI open-source repository across approximately 9,000 issue threads, the framework addresses three questions: how to automate workflow-inefficiency detection from real-time conversational data, whether sentiment signals can surface risk earlier than traditional label-based methods, and how to isolate human narrative from machine-generated noise in mixed-media issue text. SentTrack combines two complementary pipelines. A horizontal pipeline translates raw issue reports into clean summaries using a large language model, extracts mid-level concern phrases, and clusters them through UMAP and HDBSCAN, producing 613 semantic clusters from the first 3,608 issues processed. A vertical pipeline applies the ABCDE collaborative interaction framework to classify each comment and infer thread-level outcomes. Across the full corpus, 49\% of threads ended in stagnation and only 13\% reached resolution, with the resolution gap identified as the dominant bottleneck signal. A weighted scoring engine that combines negativity, stagnation, resolution gap, and thread length gives maintainers an interpretable prioritization tool for high-friction discussions before they stall development.

</details>

### [19] [Sim2Schedule: A Simulator-Guided LLM Framework for Autonomous Open-Pit Mine Scheduling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10286v1)
*Mustavi Ibne Masum,Thiago Eustaquio Alves de Oliveira,Mahzabeen Emu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 模拟器引导LLM agent调度，方法可迁移至代码优化中的反馈机制

TL;DR: 提出模拟器约束的大语言模型框架，零样本生成露天矿调度计划，达到MILP最优NPV的94%-99%，且计算时间线性增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MILP虽理论最优但计算复杂且无法实时适应，需一种实际可扩展的替代方案。

Method: 将LLM作为决策代理，每一步由定制模拟器（编码地质和运营约束）引导行动生成，完全零样本且无需微调。

Result: 在不同规模实例上，LLM框架恢复MILP最优NPV的94%-99%，计算时间线性扩展。

Conclusion: 模拟器约束的LLM代理是长期工业调度的实用且可扩展替代方案。

中文摘要：露天矿调度是在复杂的地质和运营约束下最大化经济回报的关键过程。尽管混合整数线性规划（MILP）提供了数学上的最优基线，但其指数级计算复杂性和无法实时适应的能力限制了其在动态工业环境中的实际部署。这项工作引入了一个模拟器驱动的大语言模型（LLM）调度框架，其中LLM作为自主决策代理，每一步都由一个定制模拟器引导，该模拟器将地质优先关系、提取-处理耦合和动态容量约束直接编码到行动生成机制中。完全在封闭、数据安全的环境中以零样本方式运行，该框架生成完整、可解释的提取和处理计划，无需基于云的推理、领域特定微调或重新训练。为了提供可信的性能基准，开发了一种新颖的MILP公式，该公式结合了现实的操作和地质约束。在不同规模和时段的开采实例上进行评估，基于LLM的框架恢复了MILP最优NPV的94%到99%，同时计算时间呈线性扩展。这些结果表明，模拟器约束的LLM代理是在复杂操作约束下进行长期工业调度的实用且可扩展的替代方案。

Original abstract: Open-pit mine scheduling is a critical process for maximizing economic return under complex geotechnical and operational constraints. While Mixed-Integer Linear Programming (MILP) provides mathematically optimal baselines, its exponential computational complexity and inability to adapt in real time limit its practical deployment in dynamic industrial environments. This work introduces a simulator-driven Large Language Model (LLM) scheduling framework in which the LLM acts as an autonomous decision-making agent, guided at each step by a custom simulator that encodes geotechnical precedence, extraction-processing coupling, and dynamic capacity constraints directly into the action generation mechanism. Operating entirely zero-shot within a closed, data-secure environment, the framework produces complete, interpretable extraction and processing schedules without cloud-based inference, domain-specific fine-tuning, or retraining. To provide a trustworthy performance benchmark, a novel MILP formulation is developed that incorporates realistic operational and geotechnical constraints. Evaluated across mining instances of varying scale and time periods, the LLM-based framework recovers between 94\% and 99\% of the MILP optimal NPV while scaling linearly in computation time. These results position simulator-constrained LLM agents as a practical and scalable alternative to classical optimization for long-horizon industrial scheduling under complex operational constraints.

</details>


### [20] [What Spatial Memory Must Store: Occlusion as the Test for Language-Agent Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10299v1)
*Doeon Kwon,Junho Bang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 语言agent空间记忆研究，对agent记忆设计有启发

TL;DR: 本文通过实验验证了在语言智能体记忆宫殿系统中，几何主导的回忆权重和可见性谓词能显著提升性能，并成功通过预注册实验确认，揭示了空间记忆的存储与读取应分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证记忆宫殿系统中几何信息是否确实提供了文本无法提供的价值，并通过实验测量其影响，以明确空间记忆的设计原则。

Method: 进行预注册的回忆实验比较线性混合与几何主导权重；设计基于DDA的可见性谓词并与文本和视场锥对比；在脚本化世界中执行预注册实验验证可见性谓词的有效性。

Result: 几何主导权重在回忆中胜出（+0.3208 vs -0.0375）；DDA可见性谓词在墙后目标达0.982（文本和视场锥为0.000）；预注册实验将假可见从1.000降至0.000，所有结果统计显著。

Conclusion: 遮挡需要几何近乎同义反复，但贡献在于通过测量和隔离明确了空间记忆的存储内容与读取方式的分离，为后续研究奠定基础。

中文摘要：语言智能体'记忆宫殿'系统将每条记忆锚定到一个世界坐标，基于这样的直觉：几何提供了文本无法提供的信息。我们将这一直觉变得可测试，并报告三个结果。第一，记忆宫殿默认将空间邻近性折叠到与近因和重要性相结合的线性混合中，这种做法没有帮助，甚至可能有害：在一项预注册的回忆实验中，已发布的混合未能通过其自身的冻结测试（平均Delta-Hit@5 -0.0375，Wilcoxon p=0.306），与位置盲基线持平，而几何主导的权重则决定性地获胜（+0.3208，p<10^-15）：当查询模式是空间性时，几何必须主导回忆。第二，记忆回忆和可见性必须分离：回忆在设计上是遮挡盲的（你正确记得墙后的下一个房间），而可见性是对存储几何的感知谓词，实时系统从未计算过。一行射线与体素数字微分分析器（DDA），从智能体已经投射的注视射线重新指向，提供了可见性：文本和实时视场锥在849个墙后目标上均得分为0.000，而锥体加DDA达到0.982（精确McNemar检验p<10^-6）；坐标回忆单独解决了余弦空值无法解决的近似重复位置（1.000 vs 0.533，n=150）。第三，可见性谓词在git提交的预注册下得到实时确认（SPMEM-OCC-LIVE-v1：八个脚本化世界，自动预言评分，96个墙后目标，假可见从1.000降至0.000，合并精确McNemar检验p=2.5x10^-29），这次运行发现并修复了一个真实的中继锚点缺陷。我们承认遮挡需要几何近乎同义反复；贡献在于测量和隔离，将空间记忆必须存储的内容与如何读取分开。这些预实验为一项冻结的确认性研究（SPMEM-ZERO-REAL-PREREG-v1）提供动力；完整的人工编写多世界研究（带盲评者）仍是未来工作。

Original abstract: Language-agent "memory palace" systems anchor each memory to a world coordinate, on the intuition that geometry adds something text cannot. We make that intuition testable and report three results. First, the memory-palace default of folding spatial proximity into a linear blend beside recency and importance does not help and can hurt: in a pre-registered recall experiment the shipped blend fails its own frozen test (mean Delta-Hit@5 -0.0375, Wilcoxon p=0.306), sitting at a position-blind baseline, while a geometry-led weighting wins decisively (+0.3208, p<10^-15): geometry must lead recall when the query regime is spatial. Second, memory recall and visibility must be separated: recall is occlusion-blind by design (you correctly remember the next room behind a wall), while visibility is a perception predicate over stored geometry that the live system never computed. A one-line ray-versus-voxel digital differential analyzer (DDA), re-pointed from the gaze ray the agent already casts, supplies it: text and the live FoV cone both score 0.000 on 849 behind-wall targets while cone-plus-DDA reaches 0.982 (exact McNemar p<10^-6); coordinate recall separately resolves near-duplicate locations a cosine null cannot (1.000 vs 0.533, n=150). Third, the visibility predicate is confirmed live under a git-committed pre-registration (SPMEM-OCC-LIVE-v1: eight scripted worlds, automated oracle scoring, 96 behind-wall targets, false-visible 1.000->0.000, pooled exact McNemar p=2.5x10^-29), a run that surfaced and fixed a real relay anchor defect. We concede that occlusion-needs-geometry is near-tautological; the contribution is the measurement and isolation, separating what spatial memory must store from how it is read. These pilots power a frozen confirmatory study (SPMEM-ZERO-REAL-PREREG-v1); the full human-authored multi-world study with blind raters remains future work.

</details>


### [21] [Self-Distillation Policy Optimization via Visual Feedback: Bridging Code and Visual Artifacts](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10334v1)
*Haoyu Dong*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 代码生成agent利用视觉反馈自蒸馏优化，直接提升代码输出质量

TL;DR: Visual-SDPO通过视觉反馈自蒸馏和视觉接地代码信用加权，提升了代码生成可视化产物的质量，并在多个基准上显著优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码生成LLM因在渲染前确定代码，导致可视化产物常有缺陷（如重叠、裁剪等），现有方法缺乏对渲染后视觉反馈的有效利用。本研究旨在利用视觉反馈自蒸馏来改善代码生成质量。

Method: 提出Visual-SDPO框架，包括：1）视觉反馈自蒸馏，将渲染后视觉反馈作为教师特权上下文蒸馏给学生；2）视觉接地代码信用加权，追溯缺陷到代码语句并放大蒸馏信号；3）序列级GRPO奖励高质量执行，同时失败执行通过自蒸馏路径学习。

Result: 在ChartMimic、Design2Code和AeSlides基准上，Visual-SDPO相比零样本基线提升>10绝对点，相比GRPO提升≥2.4点，训练步骤更少，无额外推理成本。

Conclusion: Visual-SDPO有效利用视觉反馈自蒸馏，显著提升代码生成可视化产物的质量，优于现有方法，且高效。

中文摘要：生成代码的大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地通过编写由不可微渲染器执行的程序来产生可视化产物，如图表、网页和幻灯片，在观察渲染结果之前就确定了代码。因此，原本可执行的代码常常产生具有视觉显著缺陷的产物，包括重叠元素、裁剪文本、对齐断裂、低对比度和溢出。我们研究了代码生成可视化产物的视觉反馈自蒸馏。我们提出了Visual-SDPO，一个自蒸馏策略优化框架，它将渲染后的视觉反馈视为权重共享教师模型的特权上下文，并将这种反馈蒸馏到编码学生模型中。为了使得监督在空间上具有针对性而非均匀性，我们引入了视觉接地代码信用加权，它将每个检测到的缺陷追溯到影响该元素的代码语句，并放大这些语句上的蒸馏信号。一个序列级别的GRPO（组相对策略优化）项补充了密集的token级别目标，通过奖励可执行且视觉高质量的 rollout，而失败的执行仍然可以通过自蒸馏路径进行学习，通过将执行错误作为特权上下文传递给教师模型。我们为图表、网页/UI和幻灯片生成实例化了Visual-SDPO，使用了统一的Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct主干网络。在图表到代码、UI到代码和幻灯片生成基准测试（ChartMimic、Design2Code和AeSlides）上，Visual-SDPO在主要指标上比零样本基线提高了超过10个绝对点，比GRPO提高了至少2.4点，且训练步骤更少，无额外推理成本。

Original abstract: Code-generating large language models (LLMs) increasingly produce visual artifacts such as charts, web pages, and slides by writing programs that are executed by non-differentiable renderers, committing to code before observing the render. As a result, otherwise executable code often yields artifacts with visually salient defects, including overlapping elements, clipped text, broken alignment, low contrast, and overflow. We study visual-feedback self-distillation for code-generated visual artifacts. We propose Visual-SDPO, a self-distillation policy-optimization framework that treats rendered visual feedback as privileged context for a weight-sharing teacher and distills this feedback into a coding student. To make supervision spatially targeted rather than uniform, we introduce Visual-Grounded Code Credit Weighting, which traces each detected defect back to the code statements responsible for the affected elements and amplifies the distillation signal on those statements. A sequence-level GRPO (Group Relative Policy Optimization) term complements the dense token-level objective by rewarding executable, visually high-quality rollouts, while failed executions remain learnable through the self-distillation path by passing execution errors as privileged context to the teacher. We instantiate Visual-SDPO for chart, web/UI, and slide generation with a unified Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct backbone. Across chart-to-code, UI-to-code, and slide-generation benchmarks (ChartMimic, Design2Code, and AeSlides), Visual-SDPO improves over the zero-shot base by more than 10 absolute points in the primary metric and over GRPO by at least 2.4 points, with fewer training steps and no added inference-time cost.

</details>


### [22] [Reasoning or Memorization? Direction-Aware Diversity Exploration in LLM Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10346v1)
*Jiangnan Xia,Yucheng Shi,Yu Yang,Kishan Panaganti,Zhenwen Liang,Ninghao Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM RL方向感知探索，可迁移至agent训练策略

TL;DR: 提出方向感知强化学习框架DiRL，通过区分推理和记忆驱动的探索来提升大模型的推理能力，在GRPO中集成并取得显著改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有探索方法未区分推理驱动和记忆驱动的多样性，可能鼓励记忆而非真正的推理改进。

Method: 从模型表示中提取推理-记忆方向，构建方向加权梯度特征，并据此调整奖励以优先推理探索。

Result: 在数学和通用推理基准上显著优于多种现有探索方法。

Conclusion: DiRL通过方向感知奖励有效引导探索朝向推理改进，是一种有效且可集成的方法。

中文摘要：强化学习已成为激发大型语言模型推理能力的关键范式，其中探索对于发现有效解决方案轨迹至关重要。现有的探索方法通常鼓励语义或梯度空间中的多样性，而不区分驱动这种多样性的因素。一个轨迹可能看起来新颖，因为它遵循了新的推理过程，也可能因为它在变化记忆模式与捷径。对这两种情况给予同等奖励可能会将探索导向记忆而非真正的推理改进。在本文中，我们提出了DiRL，一种方向感知的强化学习框架，将探索锚定到策略的内部推理-记忆方向。具体而言，DiRL从模型表示中提取该方向，构建方向加权梯度特征以表征轨迹更新，并塑造奖励以放大推理对齐的探索同时抑制记忆对齐的变化。DiRL无缝集成到标准的组相对策略优化（GRPO）中。在数学和通用推理基准上的大量实验证明了DiRL的有效性，显示其相对于各种现有探索方法的显著改进。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning has become a key paradigm for eliciting reasoning abilities in large language models, where exploration is crucial for discovering effective solution trajectories. Existing exploration methods typically encourage diversity in semantic or gradient spaces, without distinguishing what drives this diversity. A trajectory may appear novel because it follows a new reasoning process, or because it varies memorized patterns and shortcuts. Rewarding both cases equally may steer exploration toward memorization rather than genuine reasoning improvement. In this paper, we propose DiRL, a Direction-Aware Reinforcement Learning framework that anchors exploration to an internal reasoning-memorization direction of the policy. Specifically, DiRL extracts this direction from model representations, constructs direction-weighted gradient features to characterize rollout updates, and shapes rewards to amplify reasoning-aligned exploration while suppressing memorization-aligned variations. DiRL integrates seamlessly into standard Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). Extensive experiments on mathematical and general reasoning benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of DiRL, showing significant improvements over various existing exploration methods.

</details>


### [23] [Beyond Static Evaluation: Co-Evolutionary Mechanisms for LLM-Driven Strategy Evolution in Adversarial Games](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10389v1)
*Haoran Li,Zengle Ge,Ziyang Zhang,Xiaomin Yuan,Yui Lo,Qianhui Liu,Bocheng An,Dongke Rong,Jiaqun Liu,Annan Li,Jianmin Wu,Dawei Yin,Dou Shen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM驱动代码进化用于对抗游戏，直接关联自动代码优化与多agent演化

TL;DR: 提出FAMOU框架，通过评估器协同进化、分层深度评估和弱点压力三种机制，解决对抗多智能体游戏中因评估环境变化导致的进化停滞问题，在MCTF任务上取得最优性能，并生成全新战术结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在LLM驱动的代码进化用于对抗性多智能体游戏时，固定评估器因策略提升而变得不可靠，导致进化停滞，需要动态评估机制。

Method: 提出三种机制：评估器协同进化（将最优策略加入对手池）、分层深度评估（统计可靠评估替代噪声得分）、弱点压力（动态增加困难对手权重），并在FAMOU框架中实现。

Result: 在MCTF 2026任务中，FAMOU取得最高综合分0.526和61.7%的胜率，超越基线；消融实验证明各机制有效；生成前向搜索等新策略，并在实际竞赛中获得第一名/第三名。

Conclusion: 代码级进化能够在对抗环境中产生非平凡的算法创新，FAMOU的方法有效解决了评估环境变化问题，并具有良好的现实可迁移性。

中文摘要：近年来，基于大语言模型的代码进化技术通过迭代生成和改进程序，实现了自动化发现。然而，将这些方法应用于对抗性多智能体游戏时面临一个根本性挑战：随着策略的提升，评估环境也在变化，导致固定的评估器变得不可靠，进化陷入停滞。我们提出了三种机制来解决这一挑战：评估器协同进化，将发现的最优策略纳入对手池；分层深度评估，用统计可靠的评估替代噪声大的少量游戏得分；以及弱点压力，动态增加最困难对手的权重以突破平台期。我们在FAMOU框架中实现了这些机制，该框架建立在与OpenEvolve和ShinkaEvolve相同的基础模型代码进化范式之上。在MCTF 2026 3v3海上夺旗任务中，FAMOU在两种骨干大语言模型下均持续优于基线，取得了最高综合得分（0.526）和最佳泛化能力（对未见对手胜率61.7%），而消融实验证实了每种机制对性能的贡献。值得注意的是，大语言模型变异过程生成了种子策略中完全不存在的战术结构——包括前向搜索和自适应拦截——证明了代码级进化能在对抗环境中产生非平凡的算法创新。FAMOU进化出的策略还在AAMAS 2026 MCTF竞赛中获得了硬件循环赛第一名和模拟赛第三名，验证了其在现实世界中的可迁移性。通过我们的进化过程优化的实现和相应的评估代码可在以下网址获取：https://github.com/1xiangliu1/FAMOU-CoEvo

Original abstract: Recent advances in LLM-driven code evolution have enabled automated discovery by iteratively generating and improving programs. However, applying these methods to adversarial multi-agent games introduces a fundamental challenge: the evaluation landscape shifts as strategies improve, causing fixed evaluators to become unreliable and evolution to stagnate. We propose three mechanisms to address this challenge: evaluator co-evolution, which incorporates discovered champions into the opponent pool; hierarchical deep evaluation, which replaces noisy few-game scores with statistically reliable assessments; and weakness pressure, which dynamically up-weights the most difficult opponents to break through plateaus. We implement these mechanisms within FAMOU, a framework built upon the same foundation-model code-evolution paradigm as OpenEvolve and ShinkaEvolve. On the MCTF 2026 3v3 maritime capture-the-flag task, FAMOU consistently outperforms both baselines under two backbone LLMs, achieving the highest combined score (0.526) and the best generalization to unseen opponents (61.7% win rate), while ablations confirm that each mechanism contributes to performance. Notably, the LLM mutation process generates tactical structures entirely absent from the seed strategies -- including lookahead search and adaptive interception -- demonstrating that code-level evolution can produce nontrivial algorithmic innovations in adversarial settings. The FAMOU-evolved strategy further achieved 1st place in the hardware round-robin and 3rd in simulation at the AAMAS 2026 MCTF Competition, validating its real-world transferability. The optimized implementation and corresponding evaluation codes developed through our evolutionary process are available at: https://github.com/1xiangliu1/FAMOU-CoEvo

</details>


### [24] [STAGE-Claw: Automated State-based Agent Benchmarking for Realistic Scenarios](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10394v1)
*Sirui Liang,Bohan Yu,Peiyu Wang,Shiguang Guo,Wenxing Hu,Pengfei Cao,Jian Zhao,Cao Liu,Ke Zeng,Xunliang Cai,Kang Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自动化agent基准测试框架，可迁移至coding agent评测

TL;DR: 提出STAGE-Claw框架，自动构建和评估真实个人代理场景，通过最终系统状态正确性衡量性能，创建40个任务并评估11个模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估基准依赖沙箱和静态任务，缺乏可扩展性，难以可靠评估个人代理。

Method: 设计STAGE-Claw框架，给定任务提示自动生成包含环境、提示、真实值和验证程序的基准任务，在真实状态环境中评估代理。

Result: 构建40个真实场景任务，评估11个前沿模型，分析任务得分、成本、工具调用可靠性及失败模式。

Conclusion: STAGE-Claw提供可扩展的基于状态的方法，用于在真实用户场景中评估代理。

中文摘要：大型语言模型越来越多地被用于驱动个人代理以处理日常应用，但评估这些代理仍然是一个挑战。现有基准仍然依赖于沙箱化的人工制品、静态任务设计和粗粒度评分，这阻碍了可扩展性，并限制了向可靠个人代理评估的进展。本文提出了STAGE-Claw，一个自动化的框架，用于在基于状态的个人计算环境中构建和评估现实的个人代理场景。给定一个任务提示，STAGE-Claw会自动创建并验证一个现实的基准任务，包括其环境、任务提示、真实值和相关验证程序。然后，代理在真实的操作环境中进行评估，其性能通过最终系统状态的正确性来衡量，而不仅仅是文本响应。使用STAGE-Claw，本文创建了一个包含40个具有挑战性的真实场景代理任务的基准，评估了11个前沿模型，并分析了它们的任务得分、成本、工具调用可靠性和常见失败模式。总的来说，STAGE-Claw提供了一种可扩展的、基于状态的方式来评估在真实用户场景中的代理。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly used to power personal agents for everyday applications, but evaluating these agents remains a challenge. Existing benchmarks still rely on sandboxed artifacts, static task design, and coarse scoring, which hinder scalability and limit progress toward reliable personal-agent evaluation. This paper introduces STAGE-Claw, an automated framework for building and evaluating realistic personal-agent scenarios in state-based personal-computing environments. Given a task hint, STAGE-Claw automatically creates and validates a realistic benchmark task with its environment, task prompts, ground truth, and related verification programs. Agents are then evaluated in realistic operating environments, where performance is measured by the correctness of the final system state rather than only the textual response. Using STAGE-Claw, this paper creates a benchmark with 40 challenging real scenario agent tasks, evaluates 11 frontier models, and analyzes their task scores, costs, tool-call reliability, and common failure patterns. Overall, STAGE-Claw offers a scalable, state-based way to evaluate agents in realistic user scenarios.

</details>


### [25] [Learning Splitting Heuristics for Parallel String Solvers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20656v1)
*Chenhao Gao,Peisen Yao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种数据驱动的方法来自动生成字符串求解器的分裂启发式，通过将分裂原子选择建模为学习任务，并在两个求解器上实现，证明其优于手动设计的启发式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 字符串约束求解器面临不可判定问题和复杂约束，并行求解方法“立方与征服”需要高质量的分裂启发式，但手动设计费时且次优。

Method: 将分裂原子的选择作为学习任务，利用输入公式和求解器执行动态数据的特征，在Z3seq和Z3str4求解器中实现数据驱动的启发式生成。

Result: 学习到的启发式在求解的公式数量和平均求解时间上均优于手动设计的启发式。

Conclusion: 数据驱动的方法能有效自动生成更好的分裂启发式，提高字符串求解器的性能。

中文摘要：字符串约束求解器对于推理字符串操作程序至关重要。然而，许多实际的字符串约束是不可判定的，现实世界的应用常常提出复杂的约束，挑战当前的求解器。多核架构的兴起为并行求解提供了机会。一种关键的并行求解方法是“立方与征服”（cube-and-conquer），其中分裂启发式的质量对于有效划分搜索空间至关重要。不幸的是，手动设计启发式是劳动密集型的，且手工设计的启发式往往是次优的。本文介绍了一种数据驱动的方法来自动生成分裂启发式。我们将选择分裂原子的问题构建为学习任务，使用来自输入公式和求解器执行的动态数据的特征。我们在两个流行的字符串求解器Z3seq和Z3str4中实现了这种方法，证明了学习到的启发式在求解的公式数量和平均求解时间上优于手动设计的启发式。

Original abstract: String constraint solvers are crucial for reasoning about string-manipulating programs. However, many practical string constraints are undecidable, and real-world applications often present complex constraints that challenge current solvers. The rise of multi-core architectures offers an opportunity for parallel solving. A key parallel solving method is \emph{cube-and-conquer}, in which the quality of splitting heuristics is critical to effectively dividing the search space. Unfortunately, manually designing the heuristics is labor-intensive, and handcrafted heuristics are often sub-optimal. This paper introduces a data-driven approach to automatically generating splitting heuristics. We frame the problem of selecting a splitting atom as a learning task, using features from input formulas and dynamic data from solver execution. We implement this approach in two popular string solvers, Z3seq and Z3str4, demonstrating that the learned heuristics outperform manually designed ones in the number of solved formulas and the average solving time.

### [26] [Trace2Policy: From Expert Behavior Traces to Self-Evolving Decision Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10457v1)
*Junli Zha,Jinbo Wang,Chao Zhou,Xiang Song*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: EISR迭代规则优化框架从专家轨迹中自进化决策agent，可迁移到coding agent的自我改进。

TL;DR: Trace2Policy通过迭代错误分析恢复和优化专家决策规则，将规则编译为确定性Python后显著优于LLM提示，在物流审计部署中准确率达79.6%，且Auto-EISR变体以低成本实现跨领域迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合规敏感决策任务中，专家隐性规则难以系统化，现有LLM方法性能受限于模型能力，而规则质量被证明是更关键的性能杠杆。

Method: 提出Trace2Policy及其核心机制EISR，通过迭代错误聚类（缺失/错误/冲突）、针对性补丁和回归门限优化人类可读规则，并支持编译为确定性Python或作为LLM提示；Auto-EISR利用LLM自动化补丁生成。

Result: 在五个LLM上，八轮EISR将规则提升至79.6%（编译Python），部署中优于纯LLM基线（72.7%）；执行形式导致9.8pp差异；Auto-EISR以每轮$5-10成本复制优化，并成功迁移至LegalBench等四个基准。

Conclusion: 在偏斜基率合规任务中，规则质量是主导性能杠杆；EISR通过迭代优化显著提升规则准确性，编译执行形式优于LLM提示，且自动化变体Auto-EISR经济有效、可迁移。

中文摘要：企业专家隐性应用的决策规则——在审计、合规和合同审查中——可以通过迭代错误分析系统地恢复和改进。我们提出Trace2Policy，其核心机制EISR（错误驱动迭代技能优化）将人类可读的规则文档作为优化目标：每一轮在验证集上执行规则，按根本原因将错误聚类为缺失、错误或冲突类型，应用针对性补丁，并仅提交通过回归门限的补丁。对于这类合规敏感、偏斜基率的决策任务，我们确定规则质量——而非模型能力——是主导性能杠杆：在五个LLM上，一次性蒸馏在已部署的测试集上接近约70%，而八轮EISR将相同规则提升到79.6%（编译为确定性Python，推理时零LLM调用）。执行形式放大了增益：在生产中，相同的EISR优化内容作为编译Python运行比作为LLM提示高出9.8个百分点，这是一个在22天部署过程中共同成熟的形态与工程组合。在一家大型物流承运商（3349个审计案例）部署22天后，编译管道优于其替代的纯LLM基线（72.7%）；在这些校准的偏斜基率工作负载上，重新启用LLM回退会单调降低准确率。一个LLM驱动的变体Auto-EISR以每轮5-10美元的成本（相对于约70专家小时）重现这种优化，并迁移到四个公开基准，涵盖法律推理（LegalBench）和流程挖掘决策（BPIC 2012），无需重新工程。

Original abstract: Decision rules that enterprise experts apply tacitly -- in auditing, compliance, and contract review -- can be systematically recovered and improved through iterative error analysis. We present \textbf{Trace2Policy}, whose core mechanism -- \textbf{EISR} (\textbf{E}rror-driven \textbf{I}terative \textbf{S}kill \textbf{R}efinement) -- maintains a human-readable rule document as its optimization target: each round executes the rules on a validation set, clusters errors by root cause into MISSING, WRONG, or CONFLICT types, applies targeted patches, and commits only those that pass a regression gate. \textbf{For this class of compliance-sensitive, skewed-base-rate decision tasks, we identify rule quality -- not model capability -- as the dominant performance lever}: across five LLMs, one-shot distillation plateaus near $\sim$70\% on the deployed pool, while eight EISR rounds lift the same rules to 79.6\% when compiled into deterministic Python -- zero LLM calls at inference. \textbf{Execution form compounds the gain: in production, the same EISR-refined content runs 9.8~pp higher as compiled Python than as an LLM prompt, a form-and-engineering bundle the 22-day deployment matured together.} Deployed for 22 days at a major logistics carrier (3,349 audit cases), the compiled pipeline outperforms the pure-LLM baseline it replaced (72.7\%); on these calibrated, skewed-base-rate workloads, re-enabling LLM fallback monotonically degrades accuracy. An LLM-driven variant, \textbf{Auto-EISR}, reproduces this refinement at \$5--\$10 per cycle versus $\sim$70 expert-hours, and transfers to four public benchmarks spanning legal reasoning (LegalBench) and process-mining decisions (BPIC 2012) without re-engineering.

### [27] [A complementary study on PlanGPT: Evaluation with defined Performance Metrics and comparison with a planner](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10489v1)

Result: PlanGPT的性能不比贪婪搜索策略更好。

中文摘要：自动化规划是人工智能（AI）的一个子领域，其主要目标是生成一系列动作，称为计划，帮助我们从初始状态达到目标状态。规划问题由一组对象、一个初始状态和一个期望的目标状态定义。目标是计算一个计划，使我们能从初始状态到达目标状态。生成计划的程序称为规划器。在本文中，我们对去年发布的最先进的LLM（称为PlanGPT）进行了一项补充性研究。我们重新进行了一些实验，以验证使用LLM进行规划是否相关且值得。我们还检查了PlanGPT官方论文中关于计划覆盖的结果是否正确，并且我们对PlanGPT的性能进行了更全面的研究：在我们的论文中，使用两个指标评估PlanGPT的性能：计划成本和计划生成时间。将PlanGPT的结果与相同计划下的传统规划器结果进行比较。我们发现PlanGPT并不比贪婪搜索策略更好。

Original abstract: Automated Planning is a subfield of Artificial Intelligence (AI) where the main objective is generating a sequence of actions, known as a plan, that helps us reach a goal state from an initial state. A planning problem is defined by a set of objects, an initial state and a desired goal state. The objective is to compute a plan that'll lead us from the inital state to the goal state. Programs that generate plans are called planners.
  In this paper, we did a complementary study to the state-of-the-art LLM called PlanGPT which was released last year. We redid some experiments to verify whether planning with LLMs is \textbf{pertinent} and \textbf{worthwhile}. We also check whether the results obtained in the official PlanGPT paper for plan coverage were correct, and we also performed a more comprehensive study on PlanGPT's performance: in our paper PlanGPT's performance was evaluated using two metrics: Plan Cost and Plan Generation Time. The results of planGPT were compared to those produced by a traditional planner for the same plans and same metrics. We discovered that PlanGPT is no better than a Greedy search strategy.
