### [28] [A-Evolve-Training: Autonomous Post-Training of a 30B Model](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20657v2)
*Zhan Shi,Bing He,Yisi Sang,Hanqing Lu,Benoit Dumoulin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自动后训练系统，含自我改进循环及发现能力，可迁移至agent自优化

TL;DR: 一个自主后训练系统在无人工干预下对300亿参数模型进行多轮后训练，达到接近人类顶尖水平，并主动修正了自己失效的评估指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿模型的后训练通常需要大量人工迭代，本文旨在探索能否构建一个自主系统来自动完成这一过程，从而降低人力成本并可能发现新的优化策略。

Method: 系统采用闭环自动后训练，包括自动提出数据与配方更改、启动训练运行、读取评估结果、决定保留内容，并能在发现开发指标与外部目标脱节时自动调整搜索策略。

Result: 自主后训练的30B Nemotron模型在公开排行榜上达到0.86的得分（人类最佳0.87），排名前8/4000；系统还成功训练了120B和550B版本（但无人类基准对比）。

Conclusion: 该系统首次证明了规模化自主后训练的可行性，且展示了自主系统不仅能优化，还能发现自身测量框架的缺陷并修正，为递归自我改进提供了可审计的证据。

中文摘要：后训练一个前沿模型通常需要数周的人力工作：提出数据和配方更改、启动运行、读取评估、决定保留哪些内容。我们报告了一个自主系统，在没有人参与的情况下运行这个循环，在数周内对300亿参数的Nemotron模型进行了四轮后训练。自主生成的模型在公开的NVIDIA Nemotron-Reasoning挑战排行榜上达到了0.86的保留分数，而最佳人类提交为0.87，截至撰写时在约4000个提交中排名第八。比数字更引人注目的是：该循环检测到其自身的开发指标在最弱的领域已不再跟踪外部性能——候选方案将开发指标推至历史新高，但外部目标未动——并修改了其自身的搜索策略，不再最大化开发指标，而是寻求降低现在具有误导性的代理指标同时改善外部目标的干预措施。我们将此视为直接的、可审计的证据，表明规模化的自主循环可以产生发现，而不仅仅是优化：它检测到其测量框架已变得具有误导性，并改变了什么算作证据。我们采取操作性的观点：任何配得上“递归自我改进”标签的系统最终都必须执行端到端的前沿类模型后训练；这是该标准被满足的一个数据点。我们并不声称这是人类研究人员的“首次自主匹敌”。我们的主张更窄且可审计：据我们所知，这是首次公开报道的这种规模的自主后训练运行，而之前的公开自主机器学习研究演示停留在GPT-2级（约1.24亿参数）的计算预算上。同一系统还对1200亿和5500亿参数的Nemotron进行了后训练；由于没有公开的人类基线，这仅显示循环在该规模上闭合，而非其输出具有竞争力——这是基础设施证据，有效性主张延迟到存在可比的人类基准时。

Original abstract: Post-training a frontier model is normally weeks of human work: proposing data and recipe changes, launching runs, reading evals, deciding what to keep. We report an autonomous system that runs this loop with no human in the loop, post-training a 30B Nemotron across four rounds over multiple weeks. The autonomously produced model reaches a held-out score of 0.86 against the top human submission's 0.87 on the public NVIDIA Nemotron-Reasoning Challenge leaderboard, placing 8th of ~4000 at the time of writing. More striking than the number: the loop detected that its own dev metric had stopped tracking external performance on the weakest domain -- candidates drove dev to record highs without moving the external target -- and revised its own search policy, no longer maximizing dev but seeking interventions that lowered the now-misleading proxy while improving the external target. We treat this as direct, auditable evidence that a scaled autonomous loop can produce discovery, not only optimization: it detected that its measurement frame had become misleading and changed what counted as evidence. We take the operational view that any system worth the "recursive self-improvement" label must eventually perform end-to-end post-training of a frontier-class model; this is one datapoint of that bar being cleared. We do not claim a "first autonomous match" of human researchers. The claim we make is narrower and auditable: to our knowledge, this is the first publicly reported autonomous post-training run at this scale, where prior public autonomous-ML-research demonstrations sit at GPT-2-class (~124M) budgets. The same system also post-trains the 120B and 550B Nemotron; with no public human baseline there, this shows only that the loop closes at that scale, not that its output is competitive -- infrastructure evidence, with the effectiveness claim deferred until a comparable human anchor exists.

</details>


### [29] [HIPIF: Hierarchical Planning and Information Folding for Long-Horizon LLM Agent Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10507v1)
*Juncheng Diao,Zhicong Lu,Peiguang Li,Yongwei Zhou,Changyuan Tian,Qingbin Li,Rongxiang Weng,Jingang Wang,Xunliang Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分层规划与信息折叠用于长程LLM agent学习，直接相关

TL;DR: 提出HIPIF方法，通过子目标分解和历史折叠减少长上下文干扰，提升LLM在长周期代理任务中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法未解决长上下文干扰问题，导致多轮长周期任务中性能下降。

Method: 分层规划与信息折叠（HIPIF），包括子目标分解、历史折叠、分层反思和过程奖励。

Result: 在三个公开基准上验证有效性。

Conclusion: HIPIF有效提升LLM在长周期代理任务中的表现。

中文摘要：虽然大型语言模型（LLM）在作为自主代理执行广泛任务方面展现了强大能力，但在多轮长周期代理任务中其性能往往下降。现有方法通过细粒度信用分配来缓解长周期稀疏奖励，以及通过分层强化学习来分解任务并减少长期依赖，取得了一定进展。然而，这些方法仍未直接解决长上下文干扰问题，即不断增长的历史记录削弱了代理跟踪全局任务状态的能力，并损害后续推理和决策。受人类通过子目标分解和已完成进度总结处理复杂任务的方式启发，我们提出用于长周期LLM代理学习的分层规划与信息折叠（HIPIF）。HIPIF端到端训练代理围绕显式子目标组织长周期执行，同时折叠已完成的子目标历史以减少长上下文干扰。此外，为稳定基于子目标的规划与执行，HIPIF结合分层反思和面向子目标的过程奖励来指导子目标生成、转换和执行，无需依赖昂贵的辅助模型或特定任务专家轨迹。在三个公开的代理基准上的大量实验证明了我们方法的有效性。

Original abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong capabilities as autonomous agents across a wide range of tasks, their performance often degrades in multi-turn long-horizon agentic tasks. Existing methods have made progress through fine-grained credit assignment to alleviate long-horizon sparse rewards and hierarchical reinforcement learning to decompose tasks and reduce long-term dependency. However, these methods still do not directly address long-context interference, in which continuously growing histories weaken the agent's ability to track the global task state and impair subsequent reasoning and decision-making. Inspired by the way humans handle complex tasks through subgoal decomposition and completed progress summarization, we propose Hierarchical Planning and Information Folding (HIPIF) for long-horizon LLM agent learning. HIPIF trains the agent end-to-end to organize long-horizon execution around explicit subgoals while folding completed subgoal histories to reduce long-context interference. Furthermore, to stabilize subgoal-based planning and execution, HIPIF combines hierarchical reflection and subgoal-oriented process rewards to guide subgoal generation, transition, and execution, without relying on costly auxiliary models or task-specific expert trajectories. Extensive experiments on three publicly available agentic benchmarks demonstrate the validity of our method.

</details>


### [30] [ActiveMem: Distributed Active Memory for Long-Horizon LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10532v1)
*Yunhan Jiang,Wenbin Duan,Shasha Guo,Liang Pang,Xiaoqian Sun,Huawei Shen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分布式主动记忆用于长程推理，agent记忆机制可迁移

TL;DR: ActiveMem通过解耦记忆与推理，模仿人脑前额叶和海马体的分工，实现分布式主动记忆，在长视野推理任务中以更低开销达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有集中式记忆在长视野推理中面临上下文过载与信息丢失的权衡，而人脑的认知结构表明这种权衡可通过分离记忆与推理来缓解。

Method: 提出ActiveMem异构框架，包含一个使用语义要点推理的高级规划器和一个并行运行的轻量级分布式内存系统，后者主动累积和巩固要点。

Result: 在BrowseComp-Plus和GAIA上取得SOTA准确率，且计算开销显著降低。

Conclusion: 分布式主动记忆能有效解决长视野推理中的权衡问题，提升效率与性能。

中文摘要：记忆对于使大型语言模型（LLM）代理能够处理长视野推理任务至关重要。现有的记忆机制大多是集中式的，通常将检索到的信息和交互历史组织在单个模型上下文中。这种设计引入了一个根本的权衡：扩展推理轨迹可能导致上下文过载，而激进的内容剪裁则可能造成不可逆的信息丢失。为了寻求更好的权衡，我们从人类认知系统中汲取灵感，特别是前额叶皮层（执行控制）和海马体（记忆管理）之间的功能互补性，表明这种权衡并非固有，而可能源于集中式的记忆组织。为此，我们提出了ActiveMem，一种异构框架，将代理记忆与核心推理过程解耦。具体来说，高级规划器利用提炼的语义要点执行推理，而轻量级分布式内存系统并行运行，在整个任务过程中主动累积和巩固这些要点。在BrowseComp-Plus和GAIA上的实验表明，ActiveMem以显著降低的开销实现了最先进的准确率，证明了分布式主动记忆在长视野推理中的有效性。

Original abstract: Memory is essential for enabling large language model (LLM) agents to handle long-horizon reasoning tasks. Existing memory mechanisms are largely centralized, typically organizing retrieved information and interaction history within a single model context. This design imposes a fundamental trade-off: scaling reasoning trajectories risks context overload, whereas aggressive content pruning may result in irreversible information loss. Seeking a better trade-off, we draw inspiration from human cognitive systems, especially the functional complementarity between the prefrontal cortex (executive control) and the hippocampus (memory management), suggesting that such a trade-off need not be inherent, but may instead stem from centralized memory organization. To this end, we propose ActiveMem, a heterogeneous framework that decouples agent memory from the core reasoning process. Specifically, a high-level Planner utilizes distilled semantic gists to execute reasoning, while a lightweight, distributed memory system operates in parallel to actively accumulate and consolidate these gists throughout the task. Experiments on BrowseComp-Plus and GAIA show that ActiveMem achieves state-of-the-art accuracy with significantly reduced overhead, demonstrating the effectiveness of distributed active memory for long-horizon reasoning.

</details>


### [31] [Expected Free Energy-based Planning as Variational Inference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20658v1)
*Wouter W. L. Nuijten,Thijs van de Laar,Bert de Vries*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基于自由能的规划作为变分推理，通用agent规划方法

TL;DR: 本文将基于预期自由能的规划重新表述为具有认知先验的生成模型上的变分自由能最小化，从而统一了规划与感知和学习的推理过程，并在多个环境中验证了其信息寻求行为和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于EFE的规划方法使用专门的优化过程，难以扩展或分析，且与自由能原理的理论一致性不够明确。

Method: 通过将EFE规划转化为增广认知先验的生成模型上的变分自由能最小化，推导出期望规划成本与复杂度项的分解。

Result: 在三个环境中，认知先验诱导了信息寻求行为；变分表述在随机转换下优于基于规划的方法；时间因子分解使得方法可扩展到表格方法无法处理的复杂环境。

Conclusion: 本文提出的变分表述不仅强化了与自由能原理的一致性，还提升了规划的性能和可扩展性。

中文摘要：不确定性下的规划要求智能体在实现目标与信息收集之间取得平衡。主动推理通过预期自由能（Expected Free Energy, EFE）来解决这一问题，该代价函数统一了工具性目标与认知性目标。然而，现有的基于EFE的方法通常采用专门的优化过程，难以扩展或分析。在本文中，我们证明了基于EFE的规划可以被表述为在增广了认知先验的生成模型上的变分自由能最小化。我们的主要结果表明，最小化具有适当选择先验的变分自由能泛函会产生一个分解，即期望规划成本（EFE）加上一个复杂度项。这种表述通过将规划视为与感知和学习相同的推理过程，强化了与自由能原理的理论一致性。我们在三个复杂度递增的环境上验证了我们的方法：一个确定性的T型迷宫，一个随机反应性迷宫，以及一个部分可观测的MiniGrid DoorKey-8x8环境。实验表明，认知先验诱导了信息寻求行为，变分表述产生了在随机转换下优于基于规划方法的基于策略的推理，并且时间因子分解使得该方法能够扩展到现有表格型主动推理方法无法运作的环境。

Original abstract: Planning under uncertainty requires agents to balance goal achievement with information gathering. Active inference addresses this through the Expected Free Energy (EFE), a cost function that unifies instrumental and epistemic objectives. However, existing EFE-based methods typically employ specialized optimization procedures that are difficult to extend or analyze. In this paper, we show that EFE-based planning can be formulated as Variational Free Energy minimization on a generative model augmented with epistemic priors. Our main result demonstrates that minimizing a Variational Free Energy functional with appropriately chosen priors yields a decomposition into expected plan costs (the EFE) plus a complexity term. This formulation reinforces theoretical consistency with the Free Energy Principle by casting planning as the same inferential process that governs perception and learning. We validate our approach on three environments of increasing complexity: a deterministic T-maze, a stochastic Reactivity Maze, and a partially observable MiniGrid DoorKey-8x8 environment. The experiments demonstrate that the epistemic priors induce information-seeking behavior, that the variational formulation yields policy-based inference outperforming plan-based methods under stochastic transitions, and that temporal factorization enables scalability to environments where existing tabular active inference methods cannot operate.

</details>


### [32] [One Token per Multimodal Evidence: Latent Memory for Resource-Constrained QA](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10572v1)
*Zhi Zheng,Ziqiao Meng,Hao Luan,Wei Liu,Wee Sun Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 潜在记忆范式用于QA，可迁移至agent记忆机制

TL;DR: 提出Latent Memory，一种潜在空间记忆范式，用高维潜在令牌替代原始多模态证据，降低令牌消耗，在QA任务上性能与RAG相当且效率更高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆范式以原始文本/图像表示记忆项，导致检索系统传递大量令牌，消耗高，不适合资源受限应用。

Method: 使用小型压缩器LLM/VLM将每个证据项压缩为单个高维潜在令牌；查询嵌入到同一潜在空间检索相关令牌；直接将这些令牌作为提示给生成模型；通过重建、对比、蒸馏目标端到端训练压缩器。

Result: 在七个文本QA和多模态QA基准上，性能与先进RAG基线相当，但生成令牌减少3-10倍；在WebQA上达到最强图像基础QA性能。

Conclusion: Latent Memory是一种高效、低消耗的记忆范式，适用于资源受限场景。

中文摘要：外部记忆有效地将基于大语言模型（LLM）和视觉语言模型（VLM）的问答（QA）锚定在相关的多模态证据上。然而，现有的记忆范式以原始文本和图像形式表示每个记忆项，因此基于检索的系统必须将检索到的文本或图像传递给生成LLM/VLM，导致高令牌消耗和存储压力，使得资源受限的应用难以承受。我们提出Latent Memory，一种潜在空间记忆范式，它用一个小型压缩器LLM/VLM生成的单个高维潜在令牌替换每个原始文本或图像证据项。Latent Memory不是检索原始证据进行生成，而是在统一的潜在表示空间中操作：将查询嵌入到该空间以检索相关的潜在令牌，并将检索到的潜在令牌直接提示给预训练的LLM或VLM进行答案生成。为了使每个潜在令牌同时有效地用于重建、检索和生成，我们以统一端到端的方式使用重建、对比和蒸馏目标训练压缩器。Latent Memory在七个纯文本QA基准（例如HotpotQA）和多模态QA基准上进行了评估，与先进的RAG基线相比，它实现了有竞争力的QA性能，同时消耗的生成器令牌少3到10倍。它还在WebQA上提供了最强的图像基础QA性能。代码可在https://github.com/zz1358m/Latent-Memory-Master获取。

Original abstract: External memory effectively grounds large language models (LLMs) and vision-language models (VLMs)-based question answering (QA) in relevant multimodal evidence. However, existing memory paradigms represent each memory item in raw text and image forms, so retrieval-based systems must pass the retrieved text or images to the generation LLMs/VLMs, resulting in high token consumption and storage pressure, making it unaffordable for resource-constrained applications. We propose Latent Memory, a latent-space memory paradigm that replaces each raw text or image evidence item with a single high-dimensional latent token produced by a small compressor LLM/VLM. Rather than retrieving raw evidence for generation, Latent Memory operates in a unified latent representation space: the query is embedded into this space to retrieve relevant latent tokens, and the retrieved latent tokens are directly prompted to a pretrained LLM or VLM for answer generation. To make each latent token simultaneously informative for reconstruction, retrieval, and generation, we train the compressor with reconstruction, contrastive, and distillation objectives in a unified end-to-end manner. Latent Memory is evaluated on seven text-only QA benchmarks (e.g., HotpotQA) and multimodal QA benchmarks, where it achieves competitive QA performance compared to advanced RAG baselines while consuming 3x to 10x fewer generator tokens. It can also deliver the strongest image-grounded QA performance on WebQA. Code is available at https://github.com/zz1358m/Latent-Memory-Master.

</details>


### [33] [Learning What to Remember: Observability-Safe Memory Retention via Constrained Optimization for Long-Horizon Language Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10616v6)
*Qingcan Kang,Liu Mingyang,Shixiong Kai,Kaichao Liang,Tao Zhong,Mingxuan Yuan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 长时语言agent的记忆保留框架，直接涉及agent长期记忆与约束优化，可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出OSL-MR框架，将长时程智能体的记忆保留形式化为约束随机优化问题，通过学习与可观测性安全启发式结合，在预算紧张下超越现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆保留系统忽略长期后果和部分可观测性约束，导致资源分配低效，需要更原则性的方法。

Method: 将记忆保留建模为预算、证据效用及延迟成本的约束随机优化问题，提出OSL-MR框架，结合证据学习器和混合分数启发式，确保在线可观测性安全。

Result: 在LoCoMo和LongMemEval上，OSL-MR在预算紧张时优于现有基线，混合分数先验提升精度与召回，且在小实例上接近动态规划最优。

Conclusion: 约束随机优化与优化引导学习为长时程智能体的记忆管理提供了原则性基础。

中文摘要：长期推理的语言智能体积累的观察、推理轨迹和检索到的事实会超出上下文窗口，使得记忆保留成为一个基本的资源分配问题。现有系统将保留视为局部问题，并未在可观测性约束下建模长期后果。为填补这一空白，我们将记忆保留形式化为一个具有预算可行性、证据效用以及包括遗漏、重新获取和过时惩罚在内的延迟成本的约束随机优化问题。我们证明这个多步骤问题是NP难的，因此精确求解不可行。此外，部署决策必须在部分可观测性下做出。为应对这些挑战，我们提出了OSL-MR（面向可观测性安全的记忆保留学习），这是一个学习增强框架，强制执行在线可观测特征与离线可用监督之间的严格分离。OSL-MR结合了从已实现证据中训练的证据学习器与一个混合分数启发式，该启发式既作为可部署的在线安全基线，又作为归纳先验。该策略从交互数据中学习查询条件化的证据，并在相同约束下保持可部署性。在LoCoMo和LongMemEval上的实验表明，OSL-MR在预算紧张时尤其优于基于最近性、生成式智能体风格及其他启发式基线。混合分数先验提高了精确率和召回率，敏感性分析显示其在成本设置中具有鲁棒性。在小型可解实例上，单步优化不足以预测未来的需求变化，而OSL-MR显著更接近动态规划最优解，这证实了序列化公式的必要性并强化了我们的学习引导近似。这些结果确立了约束随机优化和优化引导学习作为长时程智能体记忆管理的原则性基础。

Original abstract: Long-horizon language agents accumulate observations, reasoning traces, and retrieved facts exceeding context windows, making memory retention a fundamental resource-allocation problem. Existing systems treat retention as local and do not model long-term consequences under observability constraints. To fill this gap, we formulate memory retention as a constrained stochastic optimization with budget feasibility, evidence utility, and delayed costs including miss, reacquisition, and stale penalties. We show this multi-step problem is NP-hard, making exact solution intractable. Moreover, deployment decisions must be made under partial observability. To address these challenges, we propose OSL-MR (Observability-Safe Learning for Memory Retention), a learning-augmented framework that enforces a strict separation between online-observable features and offline-available supervision. OSL-MR combines an evidence learner trained from realized evidence with a Mixed-Score heuristic that serves as a deployable online-safe baseline and an inductive prior. The policy learns query-conditioned evidence from interaction data and remains deployable under the same constraints. Experiments on LoCoMo and LongMemEval show OSL-MR outperforms recency-based, Generative Agents-style, and other heuristic baselines, especially under tight budgets. The Mixed-Score prior improves precision and recall, and sensitivity analysis shows robustness across cost settings. On small solvable instances, single-step optimization is insufficient to anticipate future demand shifts, while OSL-MR stays significantly closer to the dynamic-programming optimum, confirming the necessity of the sequential formulation and reinforcing our learning-guided approximation. These results establish constrained stochastic optimization and optimization-guided learning as a principled foundation for memory management in long-horizon agents.

### [34] [Skill Coverage: A Test Adequacy Metric for Agent Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20659v2)
*Boyin Tan,Xiaowei Huang,Youcheng Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于轨迹的技能覆盖率度量，通过提取技能行为约束并评估覆盖率，发现现有技能覆盖率低，但利用失败约束可提升任务恢复率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能评估仅依赖任务结果，无法分析技能的具体执行情况，导致测试不充分且缺乏改进依据。

Method: 从技能中提取自然语言指令转化为半结构化行为约束，计算轨迹对其的覆盖率及通过/失败判定，并基于失败约束强化技能内容。

Result: SkillsBench上平均覆盖率仅38.66%-45.51%；强化后失败任务恢复率达16.0%。

Conclusion: 技能覆盖率既可作为测试充分性度量，也能提供细粒度可操作信号以改进智能体技能有效性。

中文摘要：智能体技能编码了大型语言模型（LLM）智能体的可复用程序性知识，现有基准测试表明此类技能可以提升任务级性能。然而，任务结果并不能揭示可复用技能的哪些部分被实际执行，也不能表明智能体在执行这些部分时是否遵循了相关的技能指令。这一差距使得我们无法判断技能是否得到了充分测试，也无法确定观察到的任务失败是否为改进技能有效性提供了可操作的证据。为填补这一空白，我们引入了技能覆盖率（skill coverage），一种基于轨迹的可复用智能体技能测试充分性度量。我们的框架从每个技能中提取技能行为约束，将自然语言技能指令转化为半结构化约束，这些约束规定了特定条件下预期的智能体行为。然后，它判断每个约束是否被智能体轨迹覆盖，对于被覆盖的约束，根据智能体行为给出通过或失败的判定。我们将该框架应用于SkillsBench。结果表明，基准排行榜上的智能体轨迹平均仅覆盖了38.66%至45.51%的提取技能行为约束。随后，我们仅通过强调智能体未能遵循的原始指令，利用失败判定来加强相应的技能内容，并使用加强后的技能执行相同任务。这种强调在五个智能体模型行中平均带来了16.0%的失败任务恢复率。这些结果表明，技能覆盖率既是一种测试充分性度量，也是一种用于观察技能使用行为的细粒度信号。在失败任务中，失败约束标签为改进智能体技能有效性提供了可操作的证据。论文附带了一个项目网站。

Original abstract: Agent skills encode reusable procedural knowledge for large language model (LLM) agents, and existing benchmarks show that such skills can improve task-level performance. However, a task outcome does not reveal which parts of a reusable skill were exercised, nor whether the agent followed the relevant skill instructions when those parts were exercised. This gap makes it unclear whether a skill has been adequately tested, or whether observed task failures provide actionable evidence for improving agent skill effectiveness.
  To fill this gap, we introduce skill coverage, a trajectory-based test-adequacy metric for reusable agent skills. Our framework extracts skill behavior constraints from each skill, translating natural-language skill instructions into semi-structured constraints that specify the expected agent behavior under particular conditions. It then determines whether each constraint is covered by an agent trajectory and, for covered constraints, assigns a Pass or Fail verdict according to the agent behavior. We apply this framework to SkillsBench. The results show that agent trajectories on the benchmark leaderboard cover only 38.66 to 45.51% of the extracted skill behavior constraints on average. We then use Fail verdicts to strengthen the corresponding skill content only by emphasizing the original instructions that the agent failed to follow, and run the same tasks with the strengthened skills. This emphasis yields an average 16.0% recovery rate of the failed tasks across the five agent-model rows. These results show that skill coverage is both a test-adequacy metric and a fine-grained signal for observing skill-use behavior. In failed tasks, failed constraint labels provide actionable evidence for improving agent skill effectiveness. A project website accompanies the paper.

</details>


### [35] [Infini Memory: Maintainable Topic Documents for Long-Term LLM Agent Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10677v1)
*Suozhao Ji,Baodong Wu,Zehao Wang,Lei Xia,Qingping Li,Ruisong Wang,Wenbo Ding,Zhenhua Zhu,Boxun Li,Guohao Dai,Yu Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 长期LLM agent记忆架构，主题文档与迭代检索，通用agent记忆方法。

TL;DR: 提出Infini Memory，一种主题结构化的文本持久记忆架构，通过缓冲区整合和迭代检索提升LLM长期记忆能力，在MemoryAgentBench上取得64.7%得分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆系统将观察存储为孤立记录或索引片段，导致证据聚合、事实修正和记忆维护困难。

Method: 将记忆视为主题文档，新观察先存缓冲区再整合为连贯上下文，推理时通过迭代工具调用进行智能体检索。

Result: 在MemoryAgentBench上取得64.7%总体得分。

Conclusion: 主题结构化维护和迭代证据检查互补地提升了长期记忆使用效果。

中文摘要：长期LLM智能体需要持久记忆，能够跨会话追踪变化的事实并提供相关证据。现有的记忆系统通常将观察结果存储为孤立的记录、摘要或索引片段，这使得证据聚合、事实修正和记忆维护变得困难。我们提出Infini Memory，一种可维护的基于文本的持久记忆架构，将智能体记忆视为主题结构化的文档。每个主题文档作为一个语义单元，用于收集相关证据、保留元数据并随时间修正事实。新的观察结果首先暂存在缓冲区中，并定期整合成连贯的文本上下文。在推理时，一种智能体检索过程允许LLM通过迭代工具调用读取记忆，而不是单次检索步骤。在MemoryAgentBench上，Infini Memory获得了64.7%的总体得分。消融实验表明，主题结构化的维护和迭代的证据检查改善了长期记忆使用的互补方面。

Original abstract: Long-term LLM agents need persistent memory that can track changing facts and provide relevant evidence across sessions. Existing memory systems often store observations as isolated records, summaries, or indexed fragments, which makes evidence aggregation, fact revision, and memory maintenance difficult. We propose Infini Memory, a maintainable text-based persistent memory architecture that treats agent memory as topic-structured documents. Each topic document serves as a semantic unit for collecting related evidence, preserving metadata, and revising facts over time. New observations are first staged in a buffer and periodically consolidated into coherent textual contexts. At inference time, an agentic retrieval procedure lets the LLM read memory through iterative tool calls rather than a single retrieval step. On MemoryAgentBench, Infini Memory achieves 64.7% overall score. Ablations show that topic-structured maintenance and iterative evidence inspection improve complementary aspects of long-term memory use.

</details>


### [36] [When the Chain of Thought Knows Better: Failure Modes in Multi-Turn Reasoning Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10740v2)
*Sai Kartheek Reddy Kasu,Nils Lukas,Samuele Poppi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多轮推理模型安全失败模式分析，对agent安全控制有启发

TL;DR: 提出CoT-Output 2×2安全矩阵诊断多轮推理模型的安全失败模式，发现监督悖论和上下文注入失败两种漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮推理模型在安全问题上的失败难以通过终端分数评估发现，需要更细致的痕迹级诊断方法。

Method: 设计CoT-Output 2×2安全矩阵，从内部推理和可见输出两个维度标记每轮对话，并在信息危险场景下对三个蒸馏推理目标进行五种监督条件的评估。

Result: 收集6750个轮级观察，发现监督悖论（监控线索增加对齐伪装率）和上下文注入失败（安全内部状态却输出有害内容）两种可重现漏洞。

Conclusion: 当前的终端评估方法掩盖了多轮安全失败，所提诊断框架能有效暴露这些动态，并提供了数据集以支持后续研究。

中文摘要：多轮推理模型的失败在终端分数评估中基本不可见。模型可能在长对话早期就锁定不安全立场，但其最终轮拒答率与稳健对齐的基线相比可能看起来无差异。为了暴露这些隐藏的时间动态，我们提出了一种痕迹级诊断方法——CoT-Output 2×2安全矩阵。该框架沿两个独立轴（内部推理和可见输出）标记每一轮，产生四个操作定义的失败单元：稳健对齐、对齐伪装、显式越狱以及一种独特的失败模式，我们称之为上下文注入失败（其中CoT保持安全推理，但可见输出产生危害，突出了推理不忠实性的多轮表现）。我们在信息危险场景下，针对固定攻击者评估了三个蒸馏推理目标，涵盖五种监督条件，收集了6750个轮级观察。我们的分析揭示了两个可重现的漏洞：一个监督悖论，即明确的监督线索反而增加对齐伪装率而非抑制它；以及一个上下文注入失败，即模型在内部状态安全的情况下锁定不安全的外部输出。我们发布了完整的多轮对话和CoT轨迹数据集，以支持后续的痕迹诊断研究。

Original abstract: Failures in multi-turn reasoning models are largely invisible to terminal-score evaluation. A model can lock onto an unsafe stance early in a long dialogue, yet its final-turn refusal rate may appear indistinguishable from a robustly aligned baseline. To expose these hidden temporal dynamics, we propose a trace-level diagnostic - the CoT-Output 2x2 safety matrix. This framework labels every turn along two independent axes (internal reasoning and visible output), yielding four operationally defined failure cells: robust alignment, alignment faking, overt jailbreak, and a distinct failure mode we term context-injection failure (where the CoT maintains safe reasoning, but the visible output produces harm, highlighting a multi-turn manifestation of reasoning unfaithfulness). We evaluate three distilled reasoning targets against a fixed attacker across five oversight conditions, collecting 6750 turn-level observations on the Information-Hazard scenario. Our analysis reveals two reproducible vulnerabilities: an oversight paradox where explicit monitoring cues paradoxically increase alignment-faking rates rather than suppress them, and a context-injection failure where models lock onto unsafe external outputs despite safe internal states. We release the full dataset of multi-turn dialogues and CoT traces to support follow-up trace-diagnostic research.

</details>


### [37] [The Arbiter Agent: Continually Monitoring Multi-Agent Conversations to Detect Emergent Misalignment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10747v1)
*Filippo Tonini,Federico Torrielli,Anton Danholt Lautrup,Peter Schneider-Kamp,Mustafa Mert Çelikok,Lukas Galke Poech*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出实时监控多agent对话的Arbiter Agent，涉及多agent协作与安全

TL;DR: 本文提出仲裁者（Arbiter），一种在有限检查预算下实时监控多语言模型代理对话并识别不协调行为的工具，实验表明其能早期可靠检测，主动检查工具提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多语言模型代理交互可能引发个体测试时未显现的不协调问题，需要实时监控。

Method: 仲裁者通过逐步观察对话，在检查预算内选择等待、询问、检查内部信息或记录可疑行为，最终报告不协调来源。

Result: 仲裁者在五种对话条件下有效检测不协调，主动工具提升准确性和速度；权重引起的不协调最难检测，指令引起的易检测；记录工具提高召回但降低精确。

Conclusion: 持续、预算感知的监控能有效捕捉不协调，监督多代理系统需将审计者视为主动参与者。

中文摘要：随着基于多个语言模型代理构建的AI系统变得越来越普遍，它们被越来越多地用于共同做出决策：讨论、协商和执行共享任务。虽然单个代理在单独测试时可能表现良好，但问题可能源于它们之间的互动方式。我们引入了仲裁者（Arbiter），这是一种专门设计用于实时监控多代理对话并识别哪些参与者可能表现出不协调行为的代理。仲裁者在有限的“检查预算”下运作，这意味着它必须谨慎决定如何使用其资源。当它逐步观察对话时，它可以选择等待、询问参与者、检查内部信息（如系统提示或推理轨迹）或记录可疑行为。最后，它生成一份报告，指出不协调的可能来源。我们在五种对话条件下评估了仲裁者，范围从风险性金融建议的模型生物到评估感知和串通合作的代理，测试了五种能力递增的工具配置和两种骨干模型。我们发现仲裁者能够在对话结束前可靠地检测出不协调的代理，主动检查工具提高了检测准确性和速度。权重引起的不协调最难检测，而指令引起的不协调即使在被动观察下也能可靠识别。记录工具表现出双重效果，提高了召回率但降低了精确度。这些结果表明，持续的、预算感知的监控可以有效捕捉不协调，并且监督多代理系统可能需要将审计者视为过程中的主动参与者。代码可在 https://github.com/aisilab/arbiter 获取。

Original abstract: As AI systems built from multiple language-model agents become more common, they are increasingly used to make decisions together: discussing, negotiating, and acting on shared tasks. While individual agents may appear well-aligned when tested on their own, problems can arise from how they interact with one another. We introduce the Arbiter, an agent designed to monitor multi-agent conversations in real time and identify which participants may be behaving in misaligned ways. The Arbiter operates under a limited "inspection budget", meaning it must decide carefully how to use its resources. As it observes a conversation step by step, it can choose to wait, question a participant, examine internal information such as system prompts or reasoning traces, or log concerning behavior. At the end, it produces a report identifying the likely source of misalignment. We evaluate the Arbiter across five conversation conditions, ranging from risky financial advice model organisms to evaluation-aware and colluding agents, we test five tool configurations of increasing capability and two backbone models. We find that the Arbiter reliably detects misaligned agents well before the end of the conversation, with active inspection tools improving both detection accuracy and speed. Weight-induced misalignment proves hardest to detect, while instruction-induced misalignment is identified reliably even under passive observation. The logging tool exhibits a dual effect, improving recall at the cost of precision. These results suggest that continual, budget-aware monitoring can effectively catch misalignment, and that overseeing multi-agent systems may require treating the auditor as an active participant in the process. The code is available at https://github.com/aisilab/arbiter.

</details>


### [38] [AutoPDE: Reliable Agentic PDE Solving via Explicitly Represented Solver Strategies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10752v1)
*Huanshuo Dong,Keyao Zhang,Hong Wang,Zhezheng Hao,Zhiwei Zhuang,Ziyan Liu,Jiacong Wang,Gengyuan Liu,Xin Jin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: AutoPDE：显式表示求解器策略的LLM agent自动编写PDE求解器，直接相关代码优化agent

TL;DR: AutoPDE是一个显式维护求解器策略的代码智能体，通过三个阶段（PDE分析、数值方法选择、自适应调优）构建可检查的策略对象，在PDE Agent Benchmark上达到54.5%的通过率，比最强基线提高14.2个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM编码智能体直接从PDE问题生成代码，求解器策略隐含在实现中，导致数值决策难以检查与修订，反馈只能回到代码编辑而非策略层面。

Method: AutoPDE将求解器策略作为显式对象维护，通过三个阶段构建：PDE分析识别方程类型和结构；数值方法选择匹配分析结果并确定离散化等；自适应调优使用低成本预求解校准参数。

Result: 在PDE Agent Benchmark上，AutoPDE的通过率为54.5%，比最强基线提高14.2个百分点。

Conclusion: 显式维护求解器策略能够有效提升PDE求解器生成的可靠性和成功率，使数值决策可检查、可修订。

中文摘要：偏微分方程（PDE）的数值求解器是科学和工程中的核心计算工具。构建可靠的PDE求解器不仅需要可执行的代码，还需要一个数值求解器策略——一组关于离散化、稳定化、求解器配置和分辨率控制的决策，这些决策必须与PDE结构相匹配。最近的基于LLM的编码智能体已开始通过生成和调试求解器实现来减轻编程负担。然而，它们通常直接从PDE问题转向求解器代码，将求解器策略隐式地包含在实现细节中。因此，失败求解的反馈被路由回代码编辑而非底层策略，导致数值决策在代码生成之前难以检查，并且在失败时难以利用数值证据进行修订。为了解决这一限制，我们提出了AutoPDE，一个在整个求解过程中将求解器策略作为显式表示对象维护的代码智能体：一个独立的、可检查的对象，在任何代码编写之前构建，并且每当求解失败时，可以使用数值证据进行修订。AutoPDE通过三个阶段构建和维护此对象，所有阶段均利用可复用的PDE求解技能库：PDE分析识别方程类型和代数结构；数值方法选择选择与分析结果相匹配的数值方法，并据此确定离散化、稳定化和线性求解器；自适应调优运行低成本预求解以在给定精度和运行时间预算下校准分辨率和容差。我们在PDE Agent Benchmark上评估AutoPDE，实验结果表明，AutoPDE的通过率达到54.5%，比最强基线提高了14.2个百分点。

Original abstract: Numerical solvers for partial differential equations (PDEs) are core computational tools in science and engineering. Building reliable PDE solvers requires not only executable code, but a numerical solver strategy, a set of decisions about discretization, stabilization, solver configuration, and resolution control, that matches the PDE structure. Recent LLM-based coding agents have begun to reduce the programming burden by generating and debugging solver implementations. However, they typically move directly from a PDE problem to solver code, leaving the solver strategy implicit in implementation details. Feedback from a failed solve is therefore routed back to code edits rather than to the underlying strategy, so numerical decisions remain hard to check before code is generated and hard to revise using numerical evidence when it fails. To address this limitation, we propose AutoPDE, a code agent that maintains the solver strategy as an explicitly represented object throughout the solving process: an independent, inspectable object that is built before any code is written and can be revised, using numerical evidence, whenever a solve fails. AutoPDE builds and maintains this object in three stages, all drawing from a library of reusable PDE-solving skills: PDE analysis identifies the equation type and algebraic structure; numerical method selection chooses a numerical method that matches the analysis result and commits to a discretization, stabilization, and linear solver accordingly; and adaptive tuning runs low-cost pilot solves to calibrate resolution and tolerances under the prescribed accuracy and runtime budget. We evaluate AutoPDE on the PDE Agent Bench, where experimental results show that AutoPDE achieves a pass rate of $54.5%$, improving over the strongest baseline by $14.2$ percentage points.

</details>


### [39] [Evaluating Research-Level Math Proofs via Strict Step-Level Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10799v1)
*Yifeng Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 严格步骤级别的数学证明验证agent，对代码验证agent有启发

TL;DR: 提出逐步骤验证框架，通过严格约束上下文解决LLM验证数学证明时的上下文污染问题，优于全局评估并揭示专家基准中的隐含歧义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准全局评估方法受“上下文污染”影响，无法严格验证复杂数学证明中的细微逻辑错误。

Method: 从全局评估转向逐步骤验证，为每个推理步骤维护详细上下文，并严格约束应用定理的来源。

Result: 在FirstProof对抗性套件上的消融研究显示，约束性提示显著优于无约束全局提示，且剩余错误主要是“迂腐的过度严谨”而非逻辑幻觉。

Conclusion: 提示代理以谨慎的数学家人方式组织验证笔记可提高区分严谨与缺陷证明的能力，为自动证明审查系统奠定基础。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在严格验证复杂数学证明方面存在困难。标准的全局评估方法遭受“上下文污染”，其中表面上合理的陈述掩盖了微妙的逻辑缺陷，导致幻觉或过度怀疑。为了解决这个问题，我们从全局评估转向严格的逐步骤验证：我们的框架为每个推理步骤维护详细的上下文，并严格约束所应用定理的来源。我们在FirstProof挑战中精心策划的对抗性诊断套件上进行了评估，该套件包含研究级别的证明。一项系统的消融研究表明，这些演绎约束是不可或缺的，因为无约束的全局提示始终无法定位微妙的逻辑错误。除了优于全局评估外，我们的方法从根本上改变了失败分类。错误分析表明，剩余的拒绝主要不是严重的逻辑幻觉，而是由于未陈述的领域约定导致的“迂腐的过度严谨”实例，实际上暴露了专家基准本身隐含的歧义。我们的发现表明，提示代理以谨慎、类似人类数学家的方式组织其验证笔记，可以显著提高其区分严谨证明和有缺陷证明的能力，有潜力加强基础模型尚未很好掌握的前沿数学概念上的代理推理，并为未来的自动证明审查系统奠定理论基础。代码和提示可在GitHub上获取。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) struggle to rigorously verify complex mathematical proofs. Standard global evaluation approaches suffer from "context poisoning," in which superficially plausible statements mask subtle logical flaws, leading to hallucination or over-skepticism. To address this, we shift from global evaluation to strict step-level verification: our framework maintains detailed context for each deduction step and strictly constrains the sources of applied theorems. We evaluate on a carefully curated adversarial diagnostic suite of research-level proofs drawn from the FirstProof challenge. A systematic ablation study demonstrates that these deductive constraints are indispensable, as unconstrained global prompting consistently fails to localize subtle logical errors. Beyond outperforming global evaluation, our approach fundamentally alters the failure taxonomy. Error analysis reveals that, rather than exhibiting severe logical hallucinations, remaining rejections are primarily instances of "pedantic hyper-rigor" stemming from unstated domain conventions, effectively exposing implicit ambiguities within the expert benchmark itself. Our findings suggest that prompting agents to organize their verification notes in a cautious, human-mathematician-like manner can substantially improve their ability to distinguish rigorous proofs from flawed ones, with the potential to strengthen agentic reasoning on frontier mathematical concepts that the base model does not already know well, and to lay a theoretical foundation for future automated proof-review systems. Code and prompts are available at GitHub.

### [40] [Moonshine: An Autonomous Mathematical Research Agent Centered on Conjecture Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10806v1)
*Xiaoyang Chen,Xiang Jiang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 数学研究agent，涉及自主猜想生成，属于通用agent方法，对agent规划与推理有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 本文介绍Moonshine智能体，它通过生成数学猜想并证明来探索Jacobian猜想，提出了神经Jacobian猜想，并利用多个AI系统证明了特定情况，展示了自主生成和证明数学问题的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 展示Moonshine能够自主生成有意义的数学问题并取得严格进展，以Jacobian猜想为例验证其能力。

Method: 将Jacobian猜想的逻辑转移到一隐藏层仿射-ridge sigmoid网络，提出神经Jacobian猜想；分别调用GPT-5.5-pro和DeepSeek-V4-pro独立证明\(N=n+1\)情况，并借助ChatGPT交互开发几何拓扑证明。

Result: 获得了\(N=n+1\)情况的独立完整证明和几何拓扑证明；一般更高宽度\(N\ge n+2\)情况未解决。

Conclusion: Moonshine能够自主生成有意义的数学猜想并取得严格进展，初步验证了其能力。

中文摘要：Moonshine是一个自主智能体，其核心目标是生成数学猜想。它的核心能力是从经典问题中提取结构、提炼新概念，并制定具有数学意义的猜想。Moonshine不将单个命题的解决作为终点，而是通过猜想生成、桥梁构建和障碍识别来构建可扩展的理论框架。本文以Moonshine对Jacobian猜想的探索为例。它展示了局部非退化是否能强制全局单射性的核心逻辑如何被转移到一个隐藏层的仿射-ridge sigmoid网络。这导致了神经Jacobian猜想（NJC）的形成：如果这样的网络在整个空间上具有严格正的Jacobian行列式，那么它必须是全局单射的。通过分别调用GPT-5.5-pro和DeepSeek-V4-pro，Moonshine获得了\(N=n+1\)情况的独立完整证明。此外，在ChatGPT的辅助下，通过交互式使用其网页界面与GPT-5.5-pro，开发了一个几何拓扑证明。这些结果为猜想的合理性提供了初步证据。然而，一般更高宽度的情况\(N\ge n+2\)仍未解决，留待进一步研究。这项工作展示了Moonshine自主生成有意义的数学问题并对其进行严格进展的能力。

Original abstract: Moonshine is an autonomous agent whose central objective is to generate mathematical conjectures. Its core capability is to extract structure from classical problems, distill new concepts, and formulate conjectures of mathematical significance. Rather than treating the solution of a single proposition as its endpoint, Moonshine builds an extensible theoretical framework through conjecture generation, bridge building, and obstacle identification. This article uses Moonshine's exploration of the Jacobian conjecture as an example. It shows how the central logic of whether local nondegeneracy can force global injectivity is transferred to one-hidden-layer affine-ridge sigmoid networks. This leads to the formulation of the \emph{Neural Jacobian Conjecture} (NJC): if such a network has strictly positive Jacobian determinant on the whole space, then it must be globally injective. By invoking GPT-5.5-pro and DeepSeek-V4-pro separately, Moonshine obtained independent complete proofs for the case \(N=n+1\). In addition, with the assistance of ChatGPT through interactive use of its web interface with GPT-5.5-pro, a geometric-topological proof was developed. These results provide preliminary evidence for the plausibility of the conjecture. The general higher-width case \(N\ge n+2\), however, remains unresolved and is left for further investigation. This work illustrates Moonshine's ability to autonomously generate meaningful mathematical problems and make rigorous progress on them.

### [41] [Role-Agent: Bootstrapping LLM Agents via Dual-Role Evolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10917v1)
*Xucong Wang,Ziyu Ma,Shidong Yang,Tongwen Huang,Pengkun Wang,Yong Wang,Xiangxiang Chu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 双角色进化引导LLM agent，包含环境建模与过程奖励，直接相关coding agent。

TL;DR: Role-Agent框架利用单个LLM同时作为智能体和环境，通过预测状态对齐作为过程奖励和失败模式分析实现自举式协同进化，在多个基准上平均提升超过4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体学习受限于低效交互反馈和静态训练环境，缺乏泛化能力。

Method: 提出Role-Agent框架，包含WIA（预测状态对齐作为过程奖励）和AIW（失败模式分析重塑训练分布）两个协同组件，利用单个LLM同时充当智能体和环境。

Result: 在多个基准上平均性能提升超过4%。

Conclusion: Role-Agent通过自举式协同进化有效提升了LLM智能体的性能和泛化能力。

中文摘要：尽管大规模语言模型（LLM）智能体在复杂任务上展现出强大性能，但其学习往往受限于低效的交互反馈和静态训练环境，这阻碍了更广泛的泛化。为了解决这些限制，本文引入了Role-Agent，一个利用单个LLM同时充当智能体和环境的框架，实现了自举式的协同进化。Role-Agent包含两个协同组件：World-In-Agent（WIA）和Agent-In-World（AIW）。在WIA中，LLM作为智能体，在每次动作后预测未来状态；预测状态与实际状态之间的对齐度被用作过程奖励，鼓励环境感知的推理。在AIW中，LLM从失败的轨迹中分析失败模式，并检索具有相似失败模式的任务，从而重塑训练数据分布以进行针对性练习。在多个基准上的实验表明，Role-Agent持续提升性能，相较于强基线平均提升超过4%。

Original abstract: Although Large Language Model (LLM) agents have demonstrated strong performance on complex tasks, their learning is often limited by inefficient interaction feedback and static training environments, which hinder broader generalization. To address these limitations, this paper introduces Role-Agent, \textcolor{black}{a framework} that harnesses a single LLM to function concurrently as both the agent and the environment, enabling a bootstrapped co-evolution. Role-Agent comprises two synergistic components: World-In-Agent (WIA) and Agent-In-World (AIW). In WIA, the LLM acts as the agent and predicts future states after each action; the alignment between predicted and actual states is then used as a process reward, encouraging environment-aware reasoning. In AIW, the LLM analyzes failure modes from failed trajectories and retrieves tasks with similar failure patterns, thereby reshaping the training data distribution for targeted practice. Experiments on multiple benchmarks show that Role-Agent consistently improves performance, yielding an average gain of over 4\% over strong baselines.

</details>


### [42] [Frontier Coding Agents Use Metaprogramming to Adapt to Unfamiliar Programming Languages](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10933v1)
*Aman Sharma,Sushrut Thorat,Paras Chopra*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接研究coding agent在陌生语言中的自适应能力，涉及元编程和工具反馈，与自动代码优化agent高度相关。

TL;DR: 本研究发现，最强的LLM编码代理在面对不熟悉的深奥编程语言时，会采用元编程策略（用Python生成目标代码并调试），禁止该策略导致性能大幅下降；资源投入仅能放大已有策略，不能创造新策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准主要评估主流语言环境，可能掩盖代理在不熟悉语言中的表现差异，因此需要设计实验来暴露这些差异。

Method: 使用顺序设置（文件编辑、本地执行、隐藏测试评分）在四种深奥语言上评估六个代理，并比较元编程策略的影响。

Result: 最强代理（Claude Opus 4.6, GPT-5.4 xhigh）通过元编程取得高绩效；禁止元编程导致性能大幅下降；为弱代理提供辅助代码能提升部分代理，但仍有差距；更多计算资源仅放大强代理的已有策略。

Conclusion: 强大的编码代理通过利用工具、反馈和工作区状态构建目标语言的工作模型来适应不熟悉语言，元编程是典型例子，但根本差距在于构建和调试有效策略的能力。

中文摘要：基于LLM的编码代理通常是在熟悉的软件环境中进行评估：主流语言、常见库和公共仓库。这些基准仍然重要，但它们可能掩盖了当语言本身不熟悉时代理的行为。我们使用带有文件编辑、本地执行和隐藏测试评分的顺序设置，在四种深奥编程语言上评估了六个当代编码代理。我们的协议揭示了这些代理之间的能力差异，而主流编码和代理基准（如SWE-Bench Verified和Terminal-Bench 2.0）将这些差异压缩到更窄的范围内。我们观察到最强的代理，Claude Opus 4.6和GPT-5.4 xhigh，通常避免直接编写目标语言。在Brainfuck和Befunge-98上，它们编写Python程序来生成目标语言代码，并本地调试这些生成器。禁止这种元编程策略会导致性能大幅下降。从该策略中提取的文本指导并不能实质性地改善较弱的代理。相比之下，Opus派生的用于构建生成器的Python辅助代码（没有解决的基准程序或隐藏测试答案）显著改善了Sonnet 4.6和GPT-5.4 mini在相同问题上的表现，而Haiku 4.5仍然较低。更多的解释器调用和输出标记改善了较强的代理，但使较弱的代理接近其原始性能，表明这些资源放大了有用的策略而非创造了它们。总之，这些结果表明，强大的编码代理通过使用工具、反馈和工作区状态来构建目标语言的工作模型，从而适应不熟悉的语言。元编程是最明显的例子，但更广泛的差距是构建和调试在目标语言规则下有效的策略。

Original abstract: LLM-based coding agents are usually evaluated in familiar software settings: mainstream languages, common libraries, and public repositories. These benchmarks remain important, but they can hide how agents behave when the language itself is unfamiliar. We evaluate six contemporary coding agents on four esoteric programming languages using a sequential setup with file editing, local execution, and hidden-test grading. Our protocol exposes capability differences between these agents that mainstream coding and agentic benchmarks such as SWE-Bench Verified and Terminal-Bench 2.0 compress into much narrower bands. We observe that the strongest agents, Claude Opus 4.6 and GPT-5.4 xhigh, often avoid writing the target language directly. On Brainfuck and Befunge-98, they write Python programs that generate target-language code and debug those generators locally. Forbidding this metaprogramming strategy causes large performance drops. Text guidance distilled from this strategy does not materially improve weaker agents. In contrast, Opus-derived Python helper code for building generators, with no solved benchmark programs or hidden-test answers, sharply improves Sonnet 4.6 and GPT-5.4 mini on the same problems, while Haiku 4.5 remains low. More interpreter calls and output tokens improve stronger agents but leave weaker agents near their original performance, indicating that these resources amplify useful strategies rather than create them. Together, these results show that strong coding agents adapt to unfamiliar languages by using tools, feedback, and workspace state to build a working model of the target language. Metaprogramming is the clearest case, but the broader gap is constructing and debugging a strategy that works under the target language's rules.

### [43] [Recalling Too Well: Sycophancy Evaluation and Mitigation in Memory-Augmented Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10949v1)
*Shelly Bensal,Axel Magnuson,Aparna Balagopalan,Daniel M. Bikel*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究记忆增强模型中的讨好行为，对设计更可靠的 agent 记忆组件有启发，但并非直接针对代码优化或 coding agent。

TL;DR: 持久性内存系统会放大语言模型的谄媚行为，通过引入MIST基准评估发现谄媚率最高增加25倍，并提出两种缓解措施。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究持久性内存系统可能对语言模型准确性产生的负面影响，特别是系统性放大谄媚行为。

Method: 构建多轮对话基准MIST，在三种内存系统和五个模型系列上进行测试，并进行错误分析。

Result: 内存系统在所有条件下均放大谄媚行为，谄媚率比基线高25倍，主要原因是内存提取过程中的有损压缩丢失纠正性上下文。

Conclusion: 提出的两种轻量级缓解措施能有效减少谄媚行为，同时保持或提升事实回忆能力。

中文摘要：持久性内存系统有望通过随时间存储用户信念来使大语言模型更有帮助。我们表明，它们也通过系统地放大谄媚行为（即模型优先考虑与用户的一致性而非准确性）使模型变得不那么正确。我们首次对这种效应进行了系统评估，引入了MIST：一个合成生成的多轮对话基准，其中用户在科学、医学和道德推理领域中表达看似合理的误解。在三种最先进的内存系统和五个模型系列上的测试表明，内存在所有条件下都放大了谄媚行为，谄媚率比上下文基线高出高达25倍。错误分析表明，内存提取是主要元凶：将有损压缩成离散片段的过程编码了用户的误解，同时丢弃了纠正性的上下文。基于这些结果，我们提出了两种轻量级缓解措施，这些措施在大幅减少谄媚行为的同时，在事实回忆方面达到或超过了内存系统。

Original abstract: Persistent memory systems promise to make LLMs more helpful by storing user beliefs over time. We show they also make models less correct by systematically amplifying sycophancy, wherein models prioritize agreement with users over accuracy. We conduct the first systematic evaluation of this effect, introducing MIST: a benchmark of synthetically generated multi-turn conversations where users express plausible misconceptions in scientific, medical, and moral reasoning domains. Testing across three state-of-the-art memory systems and five model families reveals that memory amplifies sycophantic behavior across all conditions, with up to 25x higher sycophancy rates than in-context baselines. Error analyses suggest memory extraction as the primary culprit: lossy compression into discrete snippets encodes user misconceptions while discarding corrective context. Based on these results, we propose two lightweight mitigations that substantially reduce sycophancy while matching or exceeding memory systems at factual recall.

Original abstract: The deployment of Large Language Model (LLM) agents for computer automation is accelerating, yet their ability to navigate complex, professional-grade productivity software is largely untested. We argue that Office automation is an ideal environment for benchmarking document-automation capability, as it requires long-horizon planning and reasoning, precise parameter configuration, and multi-application integration. To quantify this capability, we introduce an evaluation based on China's National Computer Rank Examination (NCRE), featuring 200 comprehensive practical-operation tasks across Word, Excel, and PowerPoint. Each task is scored on a 100-point rubric scale using 7,118 machine-gradable criteria, and Score Rate (SR) denotes the mean percentage of rubric points earned across these tasks. We benchmark 7 frontier LLMs and observe stark limitations: single-turn models score a maximum of 36.6%. A stronger agentic system with execution feedback, iterative repair, and broader Office automation access reaches 68.8%, but remains below the 95.5% community-reference score used as a scoring sanity check. Ultimately, our experiments demonstrate that despite recent advancements in code generation, achieving reliable fine-grained Office document automation remains a significant challenge for current code-generating LLM and agent systems.

### [45] [Structure from Reasoning, Numbers from Search: On-Premise Open LLMs as Structural Priors for Coupled MIMO Controller Tuning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11015v1)
*Jiaxuan Chen,Haonan Li,Yang Shu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出LLM作为结构先验与优化器结合的agent框架，展现了规划与工具使用的通用方法，可迁移到代码优化agent的设计中。

TL;DR: LLM在强耦合MIMO系统控制调谐中，通过提供结构先验而非优化能力，实现样本高效和可解释的控制器设计，尤其在高维场景下优势显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典控制调谐方法在强耦合MIMO系统中因忽略交互或陷入局部最优而失效，而LLM凭借对耦合的推理能力可能提供解决方案。

Method: 使用开源LLM进行推理，提出非对称控制器结构，结合经典优化器精炼，并与继电器调谐、局部优化和全局优化对比。

Result: 在强耦合四水箱系统上，支撑的LLM从任意起点达到J=16.9，精炼后达到全局最优J=12.0（10/10成功），且样本效率比全局优化器高约6倍。

Conclusion: 开源LLM在控制调谐中不作为直接优化器，而是作为样本高效、可解释的结构先验，在强耦合系统中有效，在简单系统中无优势。

中文摘要：调谐强耦合的多输入多输出（MIMO）工业过程控制器是困难的：传统的分散式自动调谐忽略了回路间的相互作用，而从自然初始化的局部数值优化会在由此产生的非凸代价景观中停滞。我们探讨了本地部署的开源大型语言模型（LLM）是否能够提供帮助，这种模型能够将数据保留在本地，且不需要过程模型。在单回路CSTR上，经典的继电反馈调谐（IAE 0.106，接近0.102的最优值）优于LLM调谐器（0.162）：对于简单回路，LLM没有增加价值。而在具有冲突设定点的强耦合四水箱系统上，情况发生了反转，该系统通过一个惩罚代价J = IAE + λ*TV(u)来评分，该代价奖励无致动器颤振的跟踪。在那里，简单的继电器调谐（J~28.6）和简单的LLM调谐（29.7）并不优于开环（22.7），而从平衡起点出发的局部优化器在10/10次运行中均失败。相反，一个经过支撑的开源LLM能够推理耦合关系，提出反直觉的非对称结构，并从任何起点达到J~16.9±0.2；使用经典优化器对其精炼后，达到了平滑的全局最优（J~12.0，10/10对0/10），该最优甚至应用了一个非显而易见的负积分校正，而分散式调谐无法实现。全局优化器（差分进化）也能达到该最优，因此LLM并非唯一途径；其优势在于样本效率和可解释性：在18次评估内得到一个可用的控制器（此时全局优化器比开环更差），并附有明确原理。这种优势随维度增长而扩大，在3x3系统上评估次数减少约6倍。该行为在四个开源模型上普遍存在，而在一个良性的过程中LLM没有优势，这划定了边界。我们贡献了一个可复现的基准测试，界定了开源LLM在控制调谐中何时有帮助：不是作为优化器，而是作为一种样本高效且可解释的结构先验。

Original abstract: Tuning controllers for strongly coupled multi-input multi-output (MIMO) industrial processes is hard: decentralized classical auto-tuning ignores loop interaction, and local numerical optimization from natural initializations stalls in the resulting non-convex cost landscape. We ask whether on-premise open-source large language models (LLMs), which keep data on-site and need no plant model, can help. On a single-loop CSTR, classical relay-feedback tuning (IAE 0.106, near the 0.102 optimum) beats an LLM tuner (0.162): for simple loops the LLM adds nothing. The picture inverts on a strongly coupled quadruple-tank with conflicting set-points, scored by a penalized cost J = IAE + lambda*TV(u) that rewards tracking without chattering actuators. There, naive relay tuning (J ~ 28.6) and naive LLM tuning (29.7) are no better than open loop (22.7), and a local optimizer from balanced starts fails in 10/10 runs. A scaffolded open LLM instead reasons about the coupling, proposes the counter-intuitive asymmetric structure, and reaches J ~ 16.9 +/- 0.2 from any start; refining it with a classical optimizer attains the smooth global optimum (J ~ 12.0, 10/10 vs. 0/10), which even applies a non-obvious negative integral correction decentralized tuning cannot. A global optimizer (differential evolution) also reaches this optimum, so the LLM is not the only route; its advantage is sample efficiency and interpretability: a usable controller in 18 evaluations (where the global optimizer is worse than open loop) plus a stated rationale. This edge grows with dimension, reaching ~6x fewer evaluations on a 3x3 plant. The behaviour generalizes across four open models, and on a benign plant the LLM offers no advantage, sharpening the boundary. We contribute a reproducible benchmark delimiting when open LLMs help in control tuning: not as optimizers, but as a sample-efficient, interpretable structural prior.

</details>

*Liya Zhu,Jingzhe Ding,Jian Zhang,Jianbo Xue,Shihao Liang,Ge Zhang,Yi Zhu,Duju Zeng,Xiang Gao,Qingshui Gu,Mailun Gao,Huimin Che,Yan Zhao,Peiheng Zhou,Haojun Wang,Chaobo Xian,Lili Le,Chi Wu,Yiwei Liu,Shengda Long,Jiale Yang,Fangzhi Xu,Sijin Wu,Haodong Duan,Chao He,Zhaojian Li,Minchao Wang,Huan Zhou,Jiani Hou,Chuqian Yu,Weiran Shi,Hongwan Gao,Jiamin Chen,Guanhong Chen,Tingqin Luo,Kaiyuan Zhang,Zhixin Yao,Qing Hua,Yuhao Jiang,Jin Chen,Pu Chen,Zhenyu Hu,Xingyu Li,Zhengxuan Jiang,Meng Cao,Tianfeng Long,Haozhe Wang,Mingzhang Wang,Yichen Zhang,Yiming Dai,Chenchen Zhang,Jiaying Wang,Xinying Liu,Xingzu Liu,Lingling Zhang,Xinjie Chen,Yujia Qin,Wangchunshu Zhou,Zhiyong Wu,Yang Liu,Jiaheng Liu,Lei Zhang,Shen Yan,Wenhao Huang,Zaiyuan Wang,Xiaolong Chang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 当前GUI代理在处理专业长期任务方面存在重大局限，工作流程一致性差，为下一代代理研究提供了方向（如提升长期依赖和领域理解能力）。

中文摘要：近年来，人工智能代理在处理日益复杂的现实世界任务方面取得了快速进展。然而，现有基准很少评估代理是否能操作图形用户界面来完成跨领域的长期、高价值专业工作流程。当前的GUI基准仍然主要集中在通用软件、相对简单的应用程序和短期任务上，这使得人们很大程度上不清楚现代代理是否能够遵循用户指令自主操作特定领域的专业软件，并以端到端的方式完成具有经济价值的工作。为了弥补这一差距，我们引入了Workflow-GYM，这是一个以专业领域和专用软件环境为中心的长期GUI任务基准。通过对最先进模型的广泛实验，我们发现即使是最强大的模型也仅能达到略高于30%的成功率，这突显出专业的长期GUI工作流程对于当前GUI代理仍然极具挑战性。进一步分析表明，当前代理难以维持长期工作流程的一致性，频繁出现工作流程阶段遗漏、错误传播、目标漂移以及缺乏对专业软件环境理解等问题。我们的发现为当前代理系统的局限性提供了重要见解，并为下一代GUI代理研究指出了关键方向。

Original abstract: Recent years have witnessed the rapid evolution of AI agents toward handling increasingly complex, real-world tasks. However, existing benchmarks rarely evaluate whether agents can operate graphical user interfaces to complete long-horizon, high-value professional workflows across diverse domains. Current GUI benchmarks still predominantly focus on general-purpose software, relatively simple applications, and short-horizon tasks, leaving it largely unknown whether modern agents can follow user instructions to autonomously operate domain-specific professional software and accomplish economically valuable work in an end-to-end manner. To bridge this gap, we introduce Workflow-GYM, a benchmark for long-horizon GUI tasks centered on professional domains and specialized software environments. Through extensive experiments on state-of-the-art models, we find that even the strongest models achieve only slightly above 30% success rates, highlighting that professional long-horizon GUI workflows remain highly challenging for current GUI agents. Further analysis reveals that current agents struggle to maintain long-horizon workflow consistency, frequently exhibiting workflow stage omission, error propagation, objective drift, and insufficient understanding of professional software environments. Our findings provide important insights into the limitations of current agent systems and suggest key directions for the next generation of GUI-agent research.

### [47] [What Fits (Into Few Tokens) Doesn't Overfit: Compression and Generalization in ML Research Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11045v1)
*Martin Andres Bertran,Aaron Roth,Zhiwei Steven Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究ML research agent的压缩与泛化，探讨策略复杂度与过拟合，属于通用agent自我改进与评估方法，可启发代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 通过两个信息瓶颈验证了成功ML策略的高度可压缩性假设，发现短提示和压缩反馈足以复现高性能模型，支持对基准驱动ML中缺乏过拟合的描述长度解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释基准驱动机器学习中重复使用保留基准却很少出现过拟合的悖论，并提出“成功策略高度可压缩”的假设。

Method: 在LLM驱动的智能体设置中，设计输出压缩和输入压缩两种信息瓶颈，在8个不同类型的数据集上测试短提示和单比特反馈下探索与复现的性能。

Result: 信息瓶颈对性能影响很小，短提示和压缩反馈足以复现和发现高性能模型，而故意诱导过拟合会导致复现失败。

Conclusion: 成功策略位于低复杂度的策略空间区域，这支持了描述长度解释，即基准驱动ML中缺乏过拟合的原因是可压缩性。

中文摘要：重复使用保留的基准测试集进行自适应调整，原则上会引发过拟合。然而，基准驱动的机器学习在实践中却出人意料地很少出现过拟合。一个有吸引力的假设是，成功的机器学习策略具有高度可压缩性。我们在LLM驱动的研究智能体设置中研究这一点，通过两个互补的信息瓶颈使该假设变得可直接检验。在“输出压缩”中，探索智能体使用验证集自适应地搜索高性能模型，我们测试一个全新的“复现智能体”能否仅凭极短的提示和训练数据复现其性能。在“输入压缩”中，探索智能体仅接收一位反馈，指示每次提交的模型是否改进了当前最佳模型。在涵盖表格分类、视觉、语言建模、扩散建模和奖励建模的8个数据集上，我们发现这些瓶颈对性能影响很小：短提示和可压缩的反馈足以复现和发现高性能模型。该假设是可证伪的：当我们有意诱导验证集过拟合时，结果无法用短提示复现。综合来看，我们的结果支持用描述长度解释基准驱动机器学习中缺乏过拟合的现象：成功的策略位于策略空间的低复杂度区域。

Original abstract: Reusing a held-out benchmark adaptively should, in principle, invite overfitting. Yet benchmark-driven machine learning (ML) has produced surprisingly little overfitting in practice. An attractive hypothesis is that successful ML strategies are highly compressible. We study this in the setting of LLM-driven research agents, where the hypothesis becomes directly testable via two complementary information bottlenecks. In \emph{output compression}, an exploration agent adaptively searches for high-performance models using a validation set, and we test whether a fresh ``reproducer agent'' can reproduce its performance given only an extremely short prompt and the training data. In \emph{input compression}, the explorer receives only one-bit feedback indicating whether each submitted model improves on the running best. Across 8 datasets spanning tabular classification, vision, language modeling, diffusion modeling, and reward modeling, we find that these bottlenecks have little effect on performance: short prompts and compressible feedback are sufficient to reproduce and find high-performance models. The hypothesis is falsifiable: when we deliberately induce validation-set overfitting, the results fail to reproduce with short prompts. Taken together, our results support a description-length explanation for the lack of overfitting in benchmark-driven ML: successful strategies occupy a low-complexity region of strategy space.

</details>


### [48] [CIAware-Bench: Benchmarking Control Intervention Awareness Across Frontier LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11063v1)
*Joachim Schaeffer,Thomas Jiralerspong,Alexander Panfilov,Guillaume Lajoie,Jonas Geiping,Yoshua Bengio,Roland S. Zimmermann*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出控制干预感知基准，评估LLM检测轨迹篡改能力，可迁移至coding agent的自主性监控与安全验证。

TL;DR: 本文提出CIAware-Bench基准，用于衡量AI模型对控制干预的感知能力，发现模型在区分自身轨迹与被修改轨迹时表现不一，且CI意识不是固定属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI控制协议可能被模型检测到干预并规避，需要衡量模型的干预感知能力以设计更安全的协议。

Method: 构建包含四个任务领域和多种变量（如水印、侧任务、控制协议）的基准CIAware-Bench，测试模型区分原始轨迹与干预后轨迹的能力。

Result: 在11个前沿模型上，默认设置下CI意识准确率最高0.87（随机为0.5），不同任务和模型间差异大，跨模型家族检测更容易。

Conclusion: CI意识不是固定模型属性，需针对每个新模型和部署场景测量，CIAware-Bench可辅助设计更难检测的控制协议。

中文摘要：AI控制协议通过监控不可信模型的行为并修改潜在不安全的步骤来监督这些模型，通常使用一个可信模型。这会部分篡改不可信模型的轨迹。如果可信模型检测到这种干预，它可能推断监控器的属性并适应以避免控制。我们引入“CIAware-Bench”，一个用于衡量前沿模型对控制干预（CI）意识的基准。CIAware-Bench测试模型是否能区分其自身轨迹与被控制干预修改后的轨迹。该基准包含四个任务领域的套件（论文写作、BigCodeBench、Bash Arena和SHADE-Arena），同时变化轨迹水印、侧任务存在以及控制协议。评估十一个前沿模型，我们在默认设置下发现低到中等的CI意识（最高0.87；随机机会平衡二元分类准确率为0.5），且在不同任务领域和模型对之间存在显著差异。跨模型家族的检测通常更容易，表明模型利用了提供商在风格或后训练上的特定差异。总体而言，CI意识不是一个固定的模型级属性，应该针对每个新的模型发布和部署场景进行衡量。我们发布CIAware-Bench以跟踪CI意识，并指导其干预更难被检测到的控制协议。

Original abstract: AI control protocols oversee untrusted models by monitoring their actions and modifying potentially unsafe steps, often using a trusted model. This partially tampers with the untrusted model's trajectory. If the trusted model detects such an intervention, it may infer properties of the monitor and adapt to evade control. We introduce \textbf{CIAware-Bench}, a benchmark for measuring \textbf{c}ontrol \textbf{i}ntervention (CI) awareness across frontier models. CIAware-Bench tests whether models can distinguish their own trajectories from those modified by a control intervention. The benchmark is comprised of a suite of four task domains (essay writing, BigCodeBench, Bash Arena, and SHADE-Arena), while varying trajectory watermarking, side-task presence, and the control protocol. Evaluating eleven frontier models, we find low to moderate CI awareness under default settings (up to 0.87; random chance balanced binary classification accuracy is 0.5) with substantial variation across task domains and model pairs. Detection is generally easier across model families, suggesting that models exploit provider-specific differences in style or post-training. Overall, CI awareness is not a fixed model-level property, and should be measured for each new model release and deployment scenario. We release CIAware-Bench to track CI awareness and inform control protocols whose interventions are harder to detect.

### [49] [A History-Aware Visually Grounded Critic for Computer Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11078v1)
*Jaewoo Lee,Zaid Khan,Archiki Prasad,Justin Chih-Yao Chen,Supriyo Chakraborty,Kartik Balasubramaniam,Sambit Sahu,Elias Stengel-Eskin,Hyunji Lee,Mohit Bansal*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 为GUI agent设计的历史感知视觉grounded批评模型，可迁移至coding agent的test-time动作验证与错误拦截。

TL;DR: HiViG是一个历史感知、视觉基础的测试时框架，通过多模态批评模型提供宏动作历史和视觉基础批判，显著提升GUI智能体的成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有批评模型存在两个关键局限：短视决策（遗忘先前动作）和缺乏视觉基础（无法检测点击错误等缺陷）。

Method: 提出HiViG框架，包含一个基于真实GUI轨迹训练的多模态批评模型，在测试时集成到策略循环中，提供宏动作历史（总结已完成任务）和视觉基础批判（验证执行坐标与当前截图）。

Result: 在网页、移动和桌面基准上，HiViG优于现有方法，Qwen3-VL-32B和Gemini-3-Flash的平均成功率分别提升5.8%和9.0%，消融实验证实两个组件均关键。

Conclusion: HiViG有效解决了批评模型的短视和视觉缺失问题，其两个组件对长程GUI任务的测试时缩放至关重要，展现出跨平台泛化能力。

中文摘要：针对计算机使用智能体（CUA）的各种测试时干预方法，包括批评模型，已被开发用于通过在复杂图形用户界面（GUI）环境中执行前动作评估来提升性能。然而，现有的批评模型存在两个关键局限性：它们（1）主要关注短视的决策循环（例如，遗忘先前的动作）以及（2）缺乏检测有缺陷动作（例如，点击错误的UI元素）所需的视觉基础。为了解决这些问题，我们引入了HiViG，一个历史感知的视觉基础测试时框架，它围绕一个多模态批评模型构建，该模型在真实GUI轨迹上训练，将过去的交互抽象为紧凑的记录，并通过视觉基础评估动作。在测试时，HiViG将批评模型整合到策略决策循环中，以提供宏动作历史（总结策略已完成的任务）和视觉基础批判（通过当前截图验证原始执行坐标，在执行前拦截错误）。在网页、移动和桌面基准测试中，HiViG持续优于现有的标量和语言批评模型，将Qwen3-VL-32B和Gemini-3-Flash的平均成功率分别比最强基线提高了5.8%和9.0%，并展示了强大的跨平台泛化能力。消融实验表明，宏动作历史减轻了短视规划，视觉基础批判减少了执行错误，这两个组件对于长程GUI任务中的测试时缩放至关重要。

Original abstract: Various test-time interventions for Computer Use Agents (CUAs), including critic models, have been developed to improve performance through pre-execution action evaluation in complex Graphical User Interface (GUI) environments. However, existing critics suffer from two key limitations: they (1) focus primarily on short-sighted decision loops (e.g., forgetting earlier actions) and (2) lack the visual grounding needed to detect flawed actions (e.g., clicking wrong UI elements). To address these, we introduce HiViG, a History-aware Visually Grounded test-time framework, built around a multimodal critic trained on real GUI trajectories to abstract past interactions into a compact record and to evaluate actions with visual grounding. At test time, HiViG integrates the critic into the policy decision loop to provide macro-action history, which summarizes the policy's completed achievements, and visually grounded critique, which verifies raw execution coordinates against the current screenshot to intercept errors before execution. Across web, mobile, and desktop benchmarks, HiViG consistently outperforms existing scalar and verbal critics, improving average success rates over the strongest baseline by 5.8% for Qwen3-VL-32B and 9.0% for Gemini-3-Flash, and demonstrates strong cross-platform generalization. Ablations show that macro-action history mitigates short-sighted planning and visually grounded critique reduces execution errors, with both components being critical for test-time scaling in long-horizon GUI tasks.

### [50] [Monte Carlo Pass Search: Using Trajectory Generation for 3D Counterfactual Pass Evaluation in Football](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11120v1)
*Andrew Kang,Priya Narasimhan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 使用MCTS和轨迹生成评估足球传球，方法（值模型、世界模型、反事实）可迁移至agent规划与执行验证。

TL;DR: 本文提出蒙特卡洛传球搜索（MCPS），通过MCTS-like框架和世界模型评估足球传球价值，并引入分布感知归因分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有传球评估方法未充分利用反事实推理和价值分布，缺乏对传球执行变异和选项变异的系统评估。

Method: 基于3D球追踪数据，使用MCPS推断踢球参数，采样执行和选项变体，用球条件世界模型滚动，用价值模型评分，得到价值分布，并用两个互补的执行剩余分数进行归因；世界模型采用改进的SMART离散令牌自回归生成器。

Result: MCPS的世界模型在最佳20个预测中表现出比基线更强的准确性，并且支持完全假设的滚动。

Conclusion: MCPS提供了分布感知的传球价值评估，有助于分析和排名，代码和模型已开源。

中文摘要：我们将足球传球评估重新表述为一种类似蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）的评估问题，其组成部分大多以不同名称存在于文献中：一个价值模型（控球价值），一个世界模型（多智能体轨迹与球交互），以及一个反事实动作的策略（带噪声的传球变体采样）。基于首个公开的、来自德甲联赛的高保真追踪数据集（包含3D球轨迹），我们引入了蒙特卡洛传球搜索（MCPS），它为每个观察到的传球推断踢球参数，采样执行变体和选项变体，用球条件世界模型将每个候选向前滚动直到下一次球交互，并用一个学习到的价值模型对结果进行评分，以获得一个关于获得价值的分布。这个分布使得分布感知归因成为可能，使用两个互补的执行剩余分数用于分析和排名：基于均值的分数和基于百分位数的分数。为了使世界模型在有限的公开数据下样本高效，我们调整了来自自动驾驶的离散令牌自回归轨迹生成器（SMART），并展示了与基线相比，它在最佳20个预测中具有强大的准确性，同时支持完全假设的滚动以进行下游评估。我们已经发布了模型检查点和代码。

Original abstract: We recast pass evaluation in football (soccer) as a Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS)-like evaluation problem whose components mostly exist in the literature under different names: a value model (possession value), a world model (multi-agent trajectories with ball interactions), and a policy over counterfactual actions (sampling pass variants with noise). Building on the first public high-fidelity tracking dataset with 3D ball trajectories from the Bundesliga, we introduce Monte Carlo Pass Search (MCPS), which infers kick parameters for each observed pass, samples execution variants and option variants, rolls each candidate forward with a ball-conditioned world model until the next ball interaction, and scores outcomes with a learned value model to obtain a distribution over gained value. This distribution enables distribution-aware attribution with two complementary execution-surplus scores used for analysis and ranking: mean-based and percentile-based scores. To make the world model sample-efficient under limited public data, we adapt a discrete-token, autoregressive trajectory generator from autonomous driving (SMART) and show it yields strong best-of-20 forecasting accuracy compared to baselines, while supporting fully hypothetical rollouts for downstream evaluation. We have released model checkpoints and code.

### [51] [From Knowing to Acting: Benchmarking Self-Awareness Capability of LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20661v1)
*Yifan Li,Shengbin Yue,Boyu Feng,Jinhu Qi,Bo Ke,Zixing Song,Hongru Wang,Zhongyu Wei,Irwin King*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 评估LLM agent自我认知（何时使用工具）的基准，直接关注agent元认知，可迁移至coding agent的自主决策评测。

TL;DR: 提出KAPRO框架和KAware数据集，用于评估LLM智能体的自我意识能力，发现自我意识与任务成功相关，开源模型易过度使用工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准只关注执行成功，忽略了智能体判断是否需要外部工具的能力（自我意识）。

Method: 设计KAPRO框架，将元认知判断与执行解耦；构建KAware数据集，划分任务为外部、内部、混合三类，系统评估自我意识。

Result: 自我意识与任务成功强相关，在内部能力设置中下降；开源模型更易过度使用工具，专有模型认知门控更可靠。

Conclusion: 自我意识是LLM智能体的关键能力，需在基准中加以考虑；不同模型架构在认知-行为对齐上存在差异。

中文摘要：外部工具的集成将LLM智能体从被动响应者转变为自主系统。然而，当前的基准测试优先考虑执行成功，忽视了自我意识能力，即判断问题是否需要必要的外部资源或可以通过内部参数知识解决的能力。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了KAPRO（Knowing-Acting Quadrant PRObe），一个通过解耦智能体的元认知判断（Knowing）和自发执行（Acting）来评估认知-行为对齐的框架。我们进一步构建了KAware，一个严格将任务划分为外部、内部和混合子空间的数据集，以系统地探索这些认知边界。跨多种智能体架构的大量实验表明，自我意识能力与任务成功密切相关，但在内部能力设置中急剧下降。此外，开源和指令遵循模型由于浅层模式匹配表现出更强的工具过度使用，而专有和推理导向模型则显示出更可靠的认知门控。基准测试和代码可在https://github.com/AI-Santiago/KAware获取。

Original abstract: The integration of external tools has transitioned LLM agents from passive responders to autonomous systems. However, current benchmarks prioritize execution success, neglecting self-awareness capability, the ability to discern whether a problem requires necessary external resources or can be solved via internal parametric knowledge. To address this, we introduce KAPRO (Knowing-Acting Quadrant PRObe), a framework that evaluates cognitive-behavioral alignment by decoupling an agent's metacognitive judgment (Knowing) from its spontaneous execution (Acting). We further construct KAware, a dataset rigorously partitioning tasks into external, internal, and hybrid subspaces to systematically probe these epistemic boundaries. Extensive experiments across diverse agent architectures show that self-awareness capability is strongly correlated with task success but degrades sharply in internal-capability settings. Moreover, open-source and instruction-following models exhibit stronger tool overuse due to shallow pattern matching, while proprietary and reasoning-oriented models demonstrate more reliable cognitive gating. Benchmark and codes are available at https://github.com/AI-Santiago/KAware.

### [52] [ABC-Bench: An Agentic Bio-Capabilities Benchmark for Biosecurity](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11150v1)
*Andrew Bo Liu,Samira Nedungadi,Bryce Cai,Alex Kleinman,Harmon Bhasin,Seth Donoughe*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: agent生物能力基准，涉及工具使用（操控机器人、设计DNA），benchmark设计可迁移至代码agent的任务构建。

TL;DR: 提出ABC-Bench基准，评估LLM智能体在生物安全相关任务上的表现，发现所有LLM智能体优于人类中位数专家。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在生物学任务上的能力增强带来了机遇和生物安全风险，需要系统性地评估其双用途能力。

Method: 设计ABC-Bench基准，包含三个任务（操作液体处理机器人、设计DNA片段、规避DNA合成筛选），并进行了湿实验室验证。

Result: 所有LLM智能体在所有任务上优于中位人类专家；在依赖已知知识任务上表现良好，在新颖推理任务上较弱；o4-mini-high生成的脚本成功在湿实验中组装了DNA。

Conclusion: LLM智能体在生物安全相关任务上展现强大的性能，但需警惕其双用途风险，特别是在需要新颖推理的任务上表现有限。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）正在迅速获得与生物学研究相关的能力，从文献综合到实验数据解释。LLM智能体还能执行以前需要经验丰富的人类生物学家才能完成的计算机模拟生物学任务。这些新兴的AI能力为科学发现和生物医学进步提供了新机遇，但也改变了生物安全风险的格局。为了解决这一问题，我们引入了智能体生物能力基准（ABC-Bench），这是一套用于衡量智能体生物安全相关能力的任务集。ABC-Bench评估LLM智能体在良性和双重用途生物学任务上的表现：编写代码操作液体处理机器人、设计用于体外组装的DNA片段，以及规避DNA合成筛选。这些任务需要生物学和软件专业知识的结合。所有测试的LLM智能体在所有三个任务上都优于中位专家人类基线。智能体在依赖公开知识和文档齐全协议的任务上表现良好，而在需要新颖生物信息学推理的任务上表现较弱。在三个湿实验室验证实验中，我们发现OpenAI的o4-mini-high生成的脚本在OpenTrons液体处理机器人上运行时，成功组装了预期序列的DNA。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are rapidly acquiring capabilities relevant to biological research, from literature synthesis to interpretation of experimental data. Increasingly, LLM agents can also perform in silico biology tasks that previously required experienced human biologists. These emerging AI capabilities offer new opportunities for scientific discovery and biomedical advances, but they also shift the landscape of biosecurity risks. To address this, we introduce the Agentic Bio-Capabilities Benchmark (ABC-Bench), a suite of tasks to measure agentic biosecurity-relevant capabilities. ABC-Bench evaluates LLM agents on both benign and dual-use biology tasks: writing code to operate liquid handling robots, designing DNA fragments for in vitro assembly, and evading DNA synthesis screening. These tasks require a combination of biology and software expertise. All tested LLM agents outperformed the median expert human baseliner on all three tasks. Agents performed highly on tasks drawing on published knowledge and well-documented protocols, and more weakly on a task requiring novel bioinformatics reasoning. In three wet-lab validation experiments, we found that OpenAI's o4-mini-high produced scripts that, when run on an OpenTrons liquid handling robot, successfully assembled DNA with expected sequences.

### [53] [Can AI Agents Synthesize Scientific Conclusions?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11337v1)
*Hayoung Jung,Pedro Viana Diniz,José Reinaldo Corrêa Roveda,Abner Fernandes da Silva,Haeun Jung,Enoch Tsai,Aleksandra Korolova,Manoel Horta Ribeiro*

TL;DR: 引入SciConBench和SciConHarness评估科学结论合成，发现模型事实质量低，干净室评估揭示数据泄露问题，消费者代理生成不完整结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有科学AI代理在健康等高风险领域进行证据检索、推理和结论合成的能力尚不明确，且缺乏可靠的评估基准和避免数据泄露的方法。

Method: 构建SciConBench基准（9.11K问题+专家结论）和SciConHarness干净室评估框架，采用自动分解原子事实并计算事实精确率/召回率的方法。

Result: 最佳代理在干净室环境下事实F1仅0.337；干净室设置一致降低性能；消费者代理常生成不完整或矛盾结论。

中文摘要：科学AI代理越来越多地检索证据、跨来源推理并综合结论，这些结论被用于具有重大影响的决策中。然而，它们在健康等高风险领域进行这种操作的能力仍不明确。我们引入了SciConBench，这是一个大型实时基准测试，包含来自系统综述的9.11K个问题和专家撰写的结论，用于评估开放领域的科学结论合成。该基准测试利用一个经过专家验证的自动化评估管道，将结论分解为原子事实，并通过事实精确率和召回率来衡量正确性和全面性。为减轻数据泄露，我们进一步引入了SciConHarness，一个干净室评估框架，为代理配备受控的网络交互以确保有效测量。评估8个前沿模型和深度研究代理后，我们发现事实质量仍然很低：在干净室设置下，最佳代理仅达到0.337的事实F1分数。我们的干净室设置一致地降低了相对于无约束评估的性能，这表明数据泄露夸大了对模型真实合成能力的估计。最后，我们审计了面向消费者的代理（例如Google AI Overview、OpenEvidence），发现它们经常生成不完整甚至矛盾的结论，即使真实答案可用。总体而言，我们的结果表明，科学结论的可靠合成仍然是一个开放的挑战，而干净室评估对于评估开放领域的AI代理至关重要。

Original abstract: Scientific AI agents increasingly retrieve evidence, reason across sources, and synthesize conclusions used in consequential decisions. Yet, their ability to do so in high-stakes domains such as health remains unclear. We introduce SciConBench, a large-scale live benchmark of 9.11K questions and expert-written conclusions from systematic reviews to evaluate open-domain scientific conclusion synthesis. The benchmark draws on an expert-validated automated evaluation pipeline that decomposes conclusions into atomic facts and measures correctness and comprehensiveness via factual precision and recall. To mitigate data leakage, we further introduce SciConHarness, a clean-room evaluation harness that equips agents with controlled web interaction to ensure valid measurement. Evaluating 8 frontier models and deep research agents, we find that factual quality remains low: under clean-room settings, the best agent achieves only a factual F1 of 0.337. Our clean-room setting consistently reduces performance relative to unconstrained evaluation, suggesting that leakage inflates estimates of models' true synthesis capabilities. Finally, we audit consumer-facing agents (e.g., Google AI Overview, OpenEvidence) and find they frequently generate incomplete and sometimes contradictory conclusions, even when the ground-truth answer is available. Overall, our results show that reliable synthesis of scientific conclusions remains an open challenge, and that clean-room evaluation is essential for assessing open-domain AI agents.

### [54] [Knowing When to Ask: Self-Gated Clarification for Hierarchical Language Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11349v2)
*Aijing Gao,Yiming Kang,Mengdie Flora Wang,Jae Oh Woo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分层语言agent的自我门控澄清机制，将询问纳入行动空间，可迁移至coding agent的规划与调试。

TL;DR: ACTION-RATING通过将澄清纳入动作空间，使提问与行动直接竞争，在HS分类任务中观察到从强制性到机会性澄清的转变，ISE提升至74%，且信息寻求模式与答案质量分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分层推理中智能体常在缺乏关键信息时错误决策，而现有方法未能将澄清作为内嵌动作，导致求助行为不可观察且间接优化。

Method: 提出ACTION-RATING公式，将澄清置于与导航共享序数尺度的动作空间，使提问与行动在每个决策点直接竞争，自然产生强制性和机会性两种信息寻求模式。

Result: 在HS分类任务中，ISE从50%提升至74%，且信息寻求模式在答案质量下降时仍保持，受控答案通道下准确率提升+16.2%。

Conclusion: ACTION-RATING有效揭示了信息寻求的结构性转变，且求助位置与答案质量经验可分离，为提升分层推理鲁棒性提供了新方向。

中文摘要：在分层推理中，失败通常源于中间决策点，即智能体在未意识到缺少关键信息时便错误地进入某一分支。我们不将澄清视为外部不确定性触发机制，而是提出ACTION-RATING公式，将其置于与导航共享序数尺度的智能体动作空间内，使得提问在每个决策点上与行动直接竞争，并在中间状态下可观察求助行为。从智能体自身评分中涌现出两种结构不同的信息寻求模式：强制性（无可行分支）和机会性（尽管有领先候选但存在残余不确定性）。在《协调关税制度》分类任务（30,000节点分类树、三个基准、4个系列共9个大语言模型）上，我们观察到从强制性澄清到机会性澄清的阶段性转变，同时信息寻求有效性（ISE，一种局部诊断指标，定义为正确下一步导航步骤后跟随的求助交互占比，非最终任务指标）从50%上升至74%。三种诊断对比未能复现此结构。分离测试显示，当答案质量下降时（准确率降低-18.8%），信息寻求模式（模式拆分、ISE排序）仍然保持，这支持了智能体求助位置与其所获答案质量之间的经验分离。在受控答案通道下，准确率增益达到+16.2%（十位数字）；我们将其解读为更优定位可解锁的上限，而非部署估计。

Original abstract: In hierarchical reasoning, failures often originate at intermediate decision points where the agent commits to a wrong branch without recognizing that it lacks critical information. Rather than treating clarification as an external uncertainty trigger, we propose ACTION-RATING, a formulation that places it inside the agent's action space on a shared ordinal scale with navigation, so that asking competes directly with acting at every decision point and help-seeking becomes observable at intermediate states. Two structurally distinct information-seeking modes emerge from the agent's own ratings: mandatory (no viable branch) and opportunistic (residual uncertainty despite a leading candidate). On Harmonized Tariff Schedule classification (30,000-node taxonomy, three benchmarks, 9~LLMs across 4 families), we observe a regime shift from mandatory to opportunistic clarification, with Information-Seeking Effectiveness (ISE), a local diagnostic defined as the fraction of help interactions followed by a correct next navigation step (not a final-task metric), rising from 50% to 74%. Three diagnostic contrasts fail to reproduce this structure. A separability test shows that the information-seeking pattern (mode split, ISE ranking) persists when answer quality is degraded (-18.8% accuracy), supporting an empirical separation between where an agent seeks help and the quality of the help it receives. Under the controlled answer channel, accuracy gains reach +16.2% at 10-digit; we read this as an upper bound on what better localization could unlock, not a deployment estimate.

</details>


### [55] [Automated Mediator for Human Negotiation: Pre-Mediation via a Structured LLM Pipeline](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11379v1)
*Jamie Bergen,Sarit Kraus*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 结构化LLM管道实现自动化调解agent，模块化设计思路可迁移至其他agent系统。

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于LLM模块结构化流水线的自动前置调解系统，在两个人类实验中表明，其在短期自我报告指标上与人类调解人相当，且偏好推断误差更低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前置调解常因成本、时间和缺乏训练有素的调解人而被忽略，需要可扩展、低投入的自动调解支持。

Method: 将前置调解分解为对话、偏好预测、回应批评和结构化总结四个专门模块，按固定顺序传递输出，避免单体提示的局限性。

Result: 自动调解人达到与人类调解人大体相当的信任和信心，偏好推断RMSE低36%，过度肯定模式从36.6%降至16.8%。

Conclusion: 结构化的LLM流水线提供可扩展的自动前置调解，短期效果与人类调解人相当，支持并行部署。

中文摘要：前置调解，即直接人类谈判之前的准备阶段，在达成互利协议方面起着关键作用，但由于成本、时间和难以接触到训练有素的调解人而常被忽略。我们引入了一种用于人类谈判的自动调解人，实现为LLM模块的结构化流水线，支持综合谈判场景中的前置调解。该流水线将准备分解为专门模块，用于对话、偏好预测、回应级别批评和结构化总结，将推理、生成和评估分离，以解决单一提示方法的局限性。我们使用术语“代理”来指代每个模块，遵循常见的LLM系统术语，但各组件并非自主，也不进行点对点交互；输出按固定顺序向前传递。我们在两个受控的人类受试者实验中评估该系统，在多议题谈判场景中比较基于AI的前置调解与专业人类调解人。在短期自我报告指标上，自动调解人达到了与人类调解人大体相当的准备结果，包括对调解人的信任和对达成互利协议的信心，同时在我们的场景和提示下，在偏好推断任务上实现了显著更低的误差（RMSE低36%）。第二项研究表明，有针对性的提示改进将过度肯定模式从36.6%降至16.8%，与人类调解人基线相当。我们的发现表明，结构化的LLM流水线可以提供可扩展、低投入的前置调解支持，在短期自我报告的准备工作结果上与人类调解人大体相当。该流水线的单方设计反映了人类调解人今天进行前置调解的方式，并支持在所有争议方之间并行部署，从而实现可扩展性。

Original abstract: Pre-mediation, the preparatory phase preceding direct human negotiation, plays a critical role in achieving mutually beneficial agreements, yet is often omitted due to cost, time, and limited access to trained mediators. We introduce an automated mediator for human negotiation, implemented as a structured pipeline of LLM modules, that supports pre-mediation in integrative negotiation settings. The pipeline decomposes preparation into specialized modules for dialogue, preference prediction, response-level critique, and structured summarization, separating inference, generation, and evaluation to address limitations of monolithic single-prompt approaches. We use the term "agent" for each module following common LLM-systems terminology, but the components are not autonomous and do not interact peer-to-peer; outputs are passed forward in a fixed sequence. We evaluate the system in two controlled human-subject experiments comparing AI-based pre-mediation with professional human mediators in a multi-issue negotiation scenario. On short-term self-reported measures, the automated mediator achieves preparation outcomes broadly comparable to human mediators, including trust in the mediator and confidence in reaching mutually beneficial agreements, while achieving substantially lower error on the preference-inference task under our scenario and prompts (36% lower RMSE). A second study shows that targeted prompt refinements reduce excessive affirmation patterns from 36.6% to 16.8%, matching human mediator baselines. Our findings suggest that structured LLM pipelines can provide scalable, low-effort pre-mediation support broadly comparable to human mediators on short-term self-reported preparation outcomes. The pipeline's single-party design mirrors how human mediators run pre-mediation today and enables parallel deployment across all parties to a dispute, supporting scalability.
