### [56] [INFRAMIND: Infrastructure-Aware Multi-Agent Orchestration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11440v1)
*Ahasan Kabir,Jiaqi Xue,Mengxin Zheng,Qian Lou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基础设施感知的多 agent 编排，直接研究多 agent 协作与推理调度。

TL;DR: INFRAMIND通过基础设施感知的规划、执行和调度，在共享GPU集群上优化多智能体LLM编排，实现低延迟和高负载下的高SLO合规。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法忽略基础设施运行时状态，导致资源利用不足和延迟堆叠，尤其是在多智能体流水线中，需要同时优化规划、路由和调度三个决策。

Method: 提出INFRAMIND框架，包含基础设施感知规划器（根据负载选择拓扑）、基础设施感知执行器（根据队列和延迟选择模型）、预算感知调度器（重排序队列），建模为层次化约束MDP，通过强化学习端到端学习。

Result: 在五个基准上，低负载下准确率提升7.6个百分点，延迟降低7倍；高负载下SLO合规99.9%，基线低于50%。

Conclusion: INFRAMIND能有效结合基础设施信号自动平衡质量与延迟，显著提升多智能体LLM系统在共享GPU集群上的性能。

中文摘要：现有的多智能体LLM编排方法，从暴力枚举集成到学习型路由器，基于任务和模型特征选择模型和拓扑。然而，这些方法没有考虑服务基础设施的运行状态。在共享GPU集群并发负载下，这种基础设施盲区导致系统性的资源利用不足：首选模型积累大量请求队列，而同样有能力的替代模型却闲置。在多智能体流水线中，每个查询触发多个顺序模型调用，这些延迟会在每个下游步骤中叠加。解决这一挑战是困难的，因为相关的基础设施信号（队列深度、KV缓存压力、延迟）是动态且嘈杂的，并且它们必须驱动三种不同的决策：规划、每步路由和调度。我们提出了INFRAMIND，这是一个使整个多智能体堆栈具有基础设施感知的框架。一个基础设施感知规划器根据实时系统负载和剩余预算来调节拓扑和角色选择，在拥塞时偏向简单图，在低负载时偏向丰富图。一个基础设施感知执行器随后在每个智能体步骤观察每个模型的队列深度、缓存利用率和响应延迟，以决定调用哪个模型以及推理深度；一个预算感知调度器进一步重新排序每个模型的队列，以便紧急请求优先得到服务。将其建模为层次化约束MDP，并通过强化学习端到端求解，系统自动学习平衡质量与延迟。在五个基准测试中，INFRAMIND在低负载下相比先前基线准确率最高提升了7.6个百分点，延迟降低7倍，在高负载下SLO合规率达到99.9%，而所有基线均低于50%。

Original abstract: Existing multi-agent LLM orchestration methods, ranging from brute-force ensembles to learned routers, select models and topologies based on task and model features. However, these methods do not consider the runtime state of the serving infrastructure. On shared GPU clusters under concurrent load, this infrastructure blindness causes systematic resource underutilization: preferred models accumulate deep request queues while equally capable alternatives sit idle. In multi-agent pipelines, where each query triggers multiple sequential model calls, these delays then compound across every downstream step. Closing this gap is challenging because the relevant infrastructure signals (queue depths, KV-cache pressure, latencies) are dynamic and noisy, and they must drive three different decisions: planning, per-step routing, and scheduling. We introduce INFRAMIND, a framework that makes the entire multi-agent stack infrastructure-aware. An infra-aware planner conditions topology and role selection on real-time system load and remaining budget, biasing toward simpler graphs under congestion and richer ones at low load. An infra-aware executor then observes per-model queue depths, cache utilization, and response latencies at each agent step to decide which model to call and how deeply to reason; a budget-aware scheduler further reorders each model's queue so that urgent requests are served first. Cast as a hierarchical constrained MDP and solved end-to-end via reinforcement learning, the system learns to balance quality against latency automatically. Across five benchmarks, INFRAMIND delivers up to +7.6 pp accuracy over the prior baseline at low load with up to 7x lower latency, and sustains up to 99.9% SLO compliance under high load where every baseline drops below 50%.

</details>


### [57] [Forecasting Future Behavior as a Learning Task](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11445v1)
*Mosh Levy,Yoav Goldberg,Asa Cooper Stickland*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 行为预测器用于预测 LLM 未来行为，可用于 agent 评测。

TL;DR: 本文提出训练行为预测器来预测大型推理模型的行为，绕过传统解释方法，在多项任务上超越GPT-5.4和Claude Opus-4.6，且推理成本更低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于解释的行为预测方法对大型推理模型（LRMs）不适用，因为解释方法难以泛化到长轨迹，且轨迹作为自然语言不忠实。因此提出将行为预测作为可学习任务，直接训练预测器。

Method: 训练行为预测器（Behavior Forecaster），以单个推理轨迹为输入，预测LRM未来行为（如答案重复概率、输入移除影响）。训练数据通过查询LRM自动生成，无需人工标注。推理只需单次前向传播。

Result: 在三个推理数据集上，行为预测器在两项任务上的准确性超过GPT-5.4和Claude Opus-4.6，且推理成本仅为它们的一小部分。

Conclusion: 推理轨迹包含超越简单阅读的有用信息，且端到端微调和从目标LRM初始化对于性能至关重要。

中文摘要：对AI系统的信任通常基于对其工作原理的解释，然后人们利用这些解释来预测其在新输入上的行为。对于大型推理模型（LRMs），这种传统方法尤其难以遵循：针对单个token生成的解释方法不能自然地推广到长轨迹，而且轨迹本身在作为自然语言阅读时往往不忠实。我们提出了一种替代方案，绕过了解释步骤：将行为预测视为可学习任务，训练行为预测器（Behavior Forecasters），它基于单个推理轨迹进行预测，这些预测通常是从解释中寻求的。预测器的训练数据通过查询LRM获得，无需人工标注，并且其推理在单次前向传播中完成。我们将该方法实例化到两个任务上：LRM在重新运行时重复其答案的可能性，以及移除输入部分如何改变其答案。我们在三个不同的推理数据集上对这两个任务进行了评估，发现训练好的行为预测器比直接阅读相同轨迹的GPT-5.4和Claude Opus-4.6更准确，且推理成本仅为它们的一小部分。我们发现，端到端微调骨干网络并从目标LRM初始化骨干网络对于强性能都是必要的。这些结果表明，推理轨迹携带了关于LRM未来行为的信息，超出了简单阅读所传达的内容。

Original abstract: Trust in an AI system is often anchored by explanations of how it works, which one then uses to forecast its behavior on new inputs. For large reasoning models (LRMs), this conventional route is particularly difficult to follow: explanation methods for single token generations do not naturally generalize to long trajectories, and the trajectories themselves are often not faithful when read as natural language. We propose an alternative that bypasses the explanation step: treat behavior forecasting as a learnable task and train Behavior Forecasters that operates on a single reasoning trajectory to make the same forecasts one would typically seek from an explanation. The forecaster's training data is obtained by querying the LRM with no human annotation, and its inference is done in a single forward pass. We instantiate this approach on two tasks: how likely the LRM is to repeat its answer on re-runs, and how removing parts of the input changes its answer. We evaluate this approach on both tasks across three diverse reasoning datasets and find that trained Behavior Forecasters are more accurate than GPT-5.4 and Claude Opus-4.6 reading the same trajectories as naive readers, at a small fraction of their inference cost. We find that fine-tuning the backbone end-to-end and initializing it from the target LRM are each necessary for strong performance. These results show that the reasoning trajectory carries information about the LRM's future behavior that goes beyond what naive reading conveys.

</details>


### [58] [Confidence Laundering in Agent Systems: Why Uncertainty Needs a Latent Carrier](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20662v1)
*Kaiwen Shi,Zheyuan Zhang,Han Bao,Colby Nelson,Yanfang Ye*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出 agent 系统中的置信度洗钱问题，关注不确定性传播与接口设计。

TL;DR: 提出潜在不确定性作用于决策交接以解决智能体系统不确定性传播的接口瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能体系统中上游不确定性在接口处丢失导致系统级错误放大，现有方法无法有效传播不确定性。

Method: 提出潜在不确定性作为附加到决策交接的载体，保留承诺前脆弱性供下游组件使用。

Result: 实现不确定性保留的接口设计，避免信心洗白导致的过度信任，提高系统可恢复性。

Conclusion: 智能体不确定性传播应从逐步估计转向不确定性保留的接口设计。

中文摘要：现代智能体系统可以将不确定性转化为过度自信。脆弱的上游决策通常作为干净的中间产物暴露给下游组件，而这些决策背后的不确定性在接口处丢失。结果，局部模糊性可能会演变为系统级的错误放大。我们认为这揭示了智能体不确定性传播中的接口瓶颈：不确定性不会仅仅因为轨迹包含不确定步骤而传播；只有当它在组件之间的交接中幸存时，不确定性才会传播。我们将不确定决策交接定义为在不确定性下做出的中间决策的转移，并识别出信心洗白作为一种失效模式，其中脆弱的上游状态被重新包装成程序上有效的伪迹，下游智能体会过度信任。为了解决这一瓶颈，我们提出潜在不确定性作为附加到决策交接上的承载不确定性的载体。潜在不确定性并非用隐藏状态替换文本，而是旨在以下游组件可以使用的方式保留承诺前的脆弱性。这一立场将智能体不确定性传播从逐步不确定性估计转向不确定性保留的接口设计，以实现更可恢复的智能体系统。

Original abstract: Modern agent systems can turn uncertainty into overconfidence. Fragile upstream decisions are often exposed to downstream components as clean intermediate artifacts, while the uncertainty behind those decisions is lost at the interface. As a result, local ambiguity can become system-level error amplification. We argue that this reveals an interface bottleneck in agent uncertainty propagation: uncertainty does not propagate simply because a trajectory contains uncertain steps; it propagates only when it survives the handoff between components. We define uncertain decision handoff as the transfer of an intermediate decision made under uncertainty, and identify confidence laundering as a failure mode in which fragile upstream states are repackaged as procedurally valid artifacts that downstream agents over-trust. To address this bottleneck, we propose latent uncertainty as an uncertainty-bearing carrier attached to decision handoffs. Rather than replacing text with hidden states, latent uncertainty aims to preserve pre-commitment fragility in a form that downstream components can use. This position shifts agent uncertainty propagation from step-wise uncertainty estimation toward uncertainty-preserving interface design for more recoverable agent systems.

</details>


### [59] [Search Discipline for Long-Horizon Research Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11522v1)
*Adithya Srinivasan,Devesh Paragiri*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 长程研究 agent 的搜索纪律，避免聚合指标误导，通用 agent 方法。

TL;DR: 聚合指标可能错误地排名多维度有效的候选者，导致模型破坏，为此提出外部控制循环审计分解行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主研究智能体使用聚合指标选择候选者时，可能导致表面提升但底层结构反转，从而错误选择破坏模型的候选者，因此需要更可靠的决策机制。

Method: 在生态系统人口模型的火灾任务上展示反转现象，并提出外部控制循环，在智能体决策后审计每个候选者的分解行为，可降级或重新开启运行。

Result: 得分最高的候选者全局分数仅略高，但导致北方森林崩溃，而稍低者却保留它们，说明聚合指标不可靠。

Conclusion: 应放弃基于聚合得分的决策，转而采用基于可审查候选效应证据的搜索纪律协议。

中文摘要：自主研究智能体现在根据一个度量来提出、评估和选择科学候选者，而这个度量通常是一个在区域、切片或队列的异质空间上聚合的简化值。我们证明，当科学有效性存在于这种分解结构中时，聚合指标可能将错误的候选者排在首位。整体数字提升了，但其底层的结构却发生了反转，因此基于该数字做出的决策会接受一个悄然破坏模型的候选者。这种失败并非领域特定，而是出现在任何候选者有效性是多维但其验证者是单一简化值的情况下。我们在生态系统人口模型中的火灾模型任务上展示了这种反转。得分最高的候选者和一个稍低的候选者在全局得分上彼此处于噪声范围内，但得分最高的候选者导致受保护的北方森林崩溃，而另一个则保留了它们。区分它们的是每个区域的行为，而不是整体数字。这个决策不应该留给产生候选者的智能体。优化得分的智能体是最不可能发现得分错误的一方，一旦智能体停止，提示就没有剩余的回合了。我们将决策移交给一个外部控制循环，该循环根据每个候选者的分解行为进行审计，并在智能体做出决策后采取行动。它可以降级智能体原本会接受的候选者，也可以重新开启智能体宣布结束的运行。我们的贡献在于反转发现本身，以及一种基于可审查的候选效应证据而非得分的搜索纪律协议。

Original abstract: Autoresearch agents now propose, evaluate, and select scientific candidates against a metric, and that metric is usually an aggregate reduced over a heterogeneous space of regions, slices, or cohorts. We show that when scientific validity lives in that disaggregated structure, the aggregate can rank the wrong candidate first. The headline number improves while the structure underneath inverts, so a decision made on the number accepts a candidate that quietly breaks the model. The failure is not domain-specific. It appears wherever a candidate's validity is multi-dimensional but its verifier is a single reduction.
  We demonstrate the inversion on a fire-model task in the Ecosystem Demography model. The highest-scoring candidate and a slightly lower one are within noise of each other on global score, yet the top-scoring one collapses the protected boreal regions while the other preserves them. What separates them is the per-region behavior, not the headline number.
  This decision should not be left to the agent that produced the candidates. The agent optimizing the score is the last party likely to catch the score being wrong, and a prompt has no remaining turn once the agent has stopped. We move the decision to an external control loop that audits each candidate on its disaggregated behavior and acts after the agent has decided. It can demote a candidate the agent would have accepted, and it can reopen a run the agent had declared finished. Our contribution is the inversion finding itself, and a search-discipline protocol that decides on reviewable candidate-effect evidence instead of the score.

</details>

### [60] [SkillResolve-Bench: Measuring and Resolving Same-Capability Ambiguity in Agent Skill Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10388v1)
*Jiandong Ding*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 代理技能检索benchmark与方法，对coding agent工具选择有直接启发

TL;DR: 提出了SkillResolve-Bench基准和SkillResolve方法，通过家族内代表选择解决同能力执行风险检索问题，在保持高召回率的同时将有害兄弟率降至0。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能体技能库的检索中，检索器可能找到正确的能力家族但暴露了同一能力中错误的代表（如过时资源或错误过程），导致执行风险，而现有基准和检索方法未关注此问题。

Method: 构建SkillResolve-Bench基准（661对有用/风险对、线索检查、查询不相交分割等）和SkillResolve方法（解析候选家族、用库负例和合同轮廓评分、每个家族选一个代表后输出top-K）。

Result: SkillResolve在Recall@3=0.766和NDCG@3=0.699时HSR@3=0，相比SkillRouter Recall提高0.112、NDCG提高0.165且HSR从0.693降至0；无代表选择时HSR@3升至0.236。

Conclusion: 家族内代表选择是将能力检索转换为更安全过程暴露的关键机制，SkillResolve有效消除了同能力执行风险。

中文摘要：智能体技能库正成为可路由的软件资产：检索到的技能可以为智能体提供指令、脚本、资源绑定和执行假设。这使得技能检索不仅仅是宽泛的相关性匹配。检索器可以找到正确的能力家族，却暴露了同一能力中错误的代表。我们将这种失败称为同能力执行风险检索。每个查询将一个有用的技能与一个查询特定的风险兄弟配对，该兄弟共享能力家族，但可能导致执行走向过时资源、缺失前提或错误程序。我们引入了SkillResolve-Bench 1.0，这是一个针对此设置的可审计基准测试，包含661对有用/风险对、源角色和入场证据、线索/泄漏检查、查询不相交分割，以及包含6660个公共SkillRet候选的7982候选池。该基准测试报告了有用排序以及有害兄弟率（HSR@K），即风险兄弟在top-K中的暴露程度。我们还提供了SkillResolve，一种参考方法，它解析活动候选家族，根据可混淆的库负例和合同轮廓线索对查询条件效用进行评分，并在最终top-K列表前从每个家族中选择一个代表。在发布的家族关系下，SkillResolve的Recall@3达到0.766，NDCG@3达到0.699，同时保持HSR@3=0。它在Recall@3上比SkillRouter提高0.112，在NDCG@3上提高0.165，同时将HSR@3从0.693降至0。没有代表选择时，在同一评分器下HSR@3升至0.236，这表明家族内代表选择是将能力检索转变为更安全过程暴露的机制。

Original abstract: Agent skill libraries are becoming routable software assets: a retrieved skill can contribute instructions, scripts, resource bindings, and execution assumptions to an agent. This makes skill retrieval more than broad relevance matching. A retriever can find the right capability family yet expose the wrong same-capability representative. We study this failure as same-capability execution-risk retrieval. Each query pairs a helpful skill with a query-specific risky sibling that shares the capability family but can lead execution toward a stale resource, missing precondition, or wrong procedure. We introduce SkillResolve-Bench 1.0, an auditable benchmark for this setting with 661 helpful/risky pairs, source-role and admission evidence, cue/leakage checks, query-disjoint splits, and a 7,982-candidate pool that includes 6,660 public SkillRet candidates. The benchmark reports helpful ranking together with harmful sibling rate (HSR@K), the top-K exposure of the risky sibling. We also provide SkillResolve, a reference method that resolves active candidate families, scores query-conditioned utility from confusable library negatives and contract-profile cues, and selects one representative from each family before the final top-K list. Under the released family relation, SkillResolve reaches Recall@3 0.766 and NDCG@3 0.699 while keeping HSR@3=0. It improves over SkillRouter by 0.112 Recall@3 and 0.165 NDCG@3 while reducing HSR@3 from 0.693 to 0. Without representative selection, HSR@3 rises to 0.236 under the same scorer, identifying within-family representative choice as the mechanism that turns capability retrieval into safer procedural exposure.

</details>


### [61] [Effective Reinforcement Learning for Agentic Search by Recycling Zero-Variance Queries During Training](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10709v1)
*João Coelho,João Magalhães,Bruno Martins,Chenyan Xiong*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 提出GRPO-style训练LLM搜索agent的零方差查询回收方法，可迁移至coding agent训练

TL;DR: 提出查询回收方法，将零方差组重新采样，使训练分布与策略共同进化，1.7B模型在7个多跳QA上达到66.0 Pass@1，匹配7B模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GRPO训练中，零方差组（全对或全错）浪费计算且被丢弃或过滤，但查询的零方差状态会随策略变化，需要更高效利用这些查询。

Method: 提出查询回收：将零方差组放回可变池，允许未来重新采样，使有效训练分布与策略共同进化。

Result: 1.7B参数模型在7个多跳QA基准上平均Pass@1为66.0，匹配或超越7B模型；回收查询贡献约75%的有效批次。

Conclusion: 查询回收有效利用零方差组，提升训练效率，验证了查询状态动态变化的假设。

中文摘要：使用GRPO风格的算法已成为在仅结果奖励下训练LLM搜索智能体的标准策略。使用这些算法时，仅当查询的展开组混合了成功和失败时，该查询才会对参数更新有贡献；全正确（太简单）和全错误（太难）的组是零方差的，浪费展开成本。现有方法将零方差视为静态属性，要么丢弃这些组，要么预先过滤掉它们。我们假设并通过实验验证，随着训练过程中策略的演变，查询会在零方差状态和有信号状态之间切换。基于这一直觉，我们提出了查询回收（query recycling），它将零方差组返回到一个可变池中以供将来重新采样，从而使有效的训练分布与策略共同进化。使用所提出的技术，一个在合成数据上训练的1.7B参数模型可以在七个多跳QA基准上达到平均66.0的Pass@1，匹配或超越使用基准监督训练、参数多达7B的系统。对回收模式的分析表明，到训练结束时，回收的查询贡献了大约四分之三的有效批次，其贡献在策略改进恢复和策略漂移之间分配。

Original abstract: The use of GRPO-style algorithms has become the standard strategy for training LLM search agents under outcome-only rewards. With these algorithms, a query contributes to parameter updates only when its rollout group mixes successes and failures; all-correct (too-easy) and all-incorrect (too-hard) groups are zero-variance and waste rollout cost. Existing approaches treat zero-variance as a static property and either discard or pre-filter such groups. We hypothesize and empirically validate that queries flip between zero-variance and signal-bearing states as the policy evolves during training. Building on this intuition, we propose query recycling, which returns zero-variance groups to a mutable pool for future resampling, so that the effective training distribution co-evolves with the policy. With the proposed technique, a 1.7B parameter model trained on synthetic data can reach 66.0 average Pass@1 accross seven multi-hop QA benchmarks, matching or surpassing systems with up to 7B parameters trained on benchmark-derived supervision. Analysis of recycling patterns shows that recycled queries supply roughly three quarters of the effective batch by the end of training, with contributions split between recovery from policy improvement and policy drift.

</details>

### [62] [RECON: An LLM-Enhanced Backward Constraint Analysis Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10264v1)
*Babangida Bappah,Lamine Noureddine,Umar Farooq,Aisha Ali-Gombe*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出RECON框架，结合LLM与静态分析，从Android字节码中高效提取精确的执行约束，比符号执行快5.8倍且成功率100%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统符号执行因路径爆炸等问题难以扩展至现代复杂软件，尤其在Android环境中，需要更高效精确的约束提取方法。

Method: RECON从目标方法逆向发现到入口点的路径，提取方法级控制流约束，并利用LLM将字节码条件转化为可解释规范。

Result: 在78个场景中，比符号执行快5.8倍，成功率100%；在100个恶意软件样本中，生成语义约束的成功率为84%。

Conclusion: LLM增强的逆向约束分析有效提升了对Android字节码的约束提取效率和可解释性，适用于恶意软件分析等场景。

中文摘要：尽管传统技术（如符号执行）为程序分析中的精确约束推理提供了原则性基础，但它们在扩展到现代软件系统时面临困难，主要是由于路径爆炸、函数建模需求以及低级程序表示中语义意图的丢失。在诸如Android等复杂的执行环境中，这些限制更加严重，因为其特征是广泛的框架交互和事件驱动行为。因此，在本文中，我们提出了一种新颖的大语言模型（LLM）增强的逆向约束分析框架，该框架结合了静态程序分析的精确性和LLM的语义理解能力，从Android字节码中提取精确的执行约束。我们的方法名为RECON，它执行从目标方法到应用程序入口点的逆向路径发现，发现方法级控制流约束，并利用LLM推理将字节码条件转换为可解释的规范。我们使用五个LLM在78个Android约束提取场景中评估了RECON，并将其与传统符号执行在真实世界应用上进行了比较。结果表明，我们的方法比传统符号执行快5.8倍，成功率达100%，同时保持逻辑等价性并提供更精确和可解释的输出。我们进一步在100个样本上评估了RECON用于恶意软件分析。结果显示，在生成导致危险API行为执行的语义约束以及检测跨多条执行路径的复杂约束方面，成功率为84%。

Original abstract: While traditional techniques, such as symbolic execution, provide a principled foundation for precise constraint reasoning in program analysis, they struggle to scale to modern software systems mainly due to path explosion, the need for function modeling, and the loss of semantic intent at low-level program representations. In complex execution environments such as Android, characterized by extensive framework interactions and event-driven behavior, these limitations are even more amplified. Thus, in this paper, we present a novel large language model (LLM)-enhanced backward constraint analysis framework that combines the precision of static program analysis with LLM's semantic understanding to extract precise execution constraints from Android bytecode. Our approach, titled RECON, performs backward path discovery from target method(s) to the application entry point(s), discovers method-level control-flow constraints, and leverages LLM reasoning to transform bytecode conditions into interpretable specifications. We evaluated RECON using five LLMs across 78 Android constraint-extraction scenarios and compared it with traditional symbolic execution on real-world applications. Results demonstrate that our approach operates 5.8X faster than traditional symbolic execution, with a 100% success rate, while maintaining logical equivalence and providing significantly more precise and interpretable output. We further evaluated RECON for malware analysis on 100 samples. The results indicate an 84% success rate in generating semantic constraints that lead to the execution of dangerous API behaviors and in detecting complex constraints across multiple execution paths.

</details>


### [63] [The Linux IOCTL Census: A Source-Derived Database of the Linux Kernel Control-Code Surface](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10290v1)
*Michael J. Bommarito*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了一个基于源代码的可查询Linux ioctl攻击面清单，通过静态分析识别入口点、命令码、输入接收点和权限门，并回测了22个CVE。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ioctl处理程序是Linux内核中最广泛且最不统一的攻击面，缺乏集中式清单，导致安全漏洞频发。

Method: 对allmodconfig构建的878个模块进行libclang单次遍历，恢复ioctl分发入口点、命令码、输入接收点和权限门；第二次遍历编码威胁模型，区分能力门控。

Result: 发现586个入口点、1289个命令码、3583个接收点、1298个权限门，回测22个CVE，并发布开放数据。

Conclusion: 该清单可有效评估ioctl攻击面，且跨操作系统查询能力增强了安全分析的通用性。

中文摘要：ioctl系统调用是Linux通用的设备控制接口。用户空间程序打开一个设备节点，向驱动程序传递一个数字命令码和一个参数缓冲区，然后驱动程序执行该命令码对应的任何操作，无论是配置硬件、读取状态，还是在内核与用户空间之间移动数据。驱动程序自行定义这些命令，数量成千上万，并在内核上下文中解析其参数，这使得ioctl处理程序成为内核中最广泛且最不统一的局部攻击面之一。一个信任从未验证的参数长度的处理程序可能会越界读写内核内存，而且命令空间没有集中记录的地方。我们提出了Linux IOCTL Census，这是一个源自源代码且可查询的攻击面清单。一个allmodconfig构建编译了跨越169个子树的878个模块，在这些模块上，对内核源代码进行单次确定的libclang遍历恢复了586个ioctl分发入口点、1289个解码的_IOC命令码、3583个受控输入接收点以及1298个权限门。第二次遍历将内核自身记录的威胁模型编码为一个可查询的列，将无能力门控的ioctl表面（这是非特权可达性的上界，而非经证明的可达性）与由硬能力门控排除在外的部分区分开来。我们使用22个最近的树内ioctl CVE对清单进行了回测，并以开放数据的形式发布了结构层，其模式与配套的Windows IOCTL Census共享，以便单个查询可以跨越两个操作系统。

Original abstract: The ioctl system call is Linux's catch-all device-control interface. A userspace program opens a device node and hands the driver a numeric command code and an argument buffer, and the driver does whatever that code means, whether configuring hardware, reading back state, or moving data into and out of the kernel. Drivers define these commands themselves, by the thousand, and parse their arguments in kernel context, which makes ioctl handlers one of the broadest and least uniform local attack surfaces in the kernel. A handler that trusts an argument length it never validates can read or write kernel memory out of bounds, and the command space is catalogued in no central place. We present the Linux IOCTL Census, a source-derived and queryable inventory of that surface. An allmodconfig build compiles 878 modules across 169 subtrees, and over them a single deterministic libclang pass over the kernel source recovers 586 ioctl dispatch entry points, 1,289 decoded _IOC command codes, 3,583 controlled-input sinks, and 1,298 permission gates. A second pass encodes the kernel's own documented threat model as a queryable column, separating the capability-ungated ioctl surface, an upper bound on unprivileged reach rather than proven reach, from the part a hard capability gate puts out of scope. We backtest the census against 22 recent in-tree ioctl CVEs and release the structural tier as open data, on a schema shared with the companion Windows IOCTL Census so a single query spans both operating systems.

</details>


### [64] [Assessing Automated Prompt Injection Attacks in Agentic Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10525v1)
*David Hofer,Edoardo Debenedetti,Florian Tramèr*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 自动提示注入攻击在agent环境中的评估，涉及agent安全与测试

TL;DR: 本研究对LLM代理的自动提示注入攻击进行实证评估，发现黑盒优化优于白盒方法，攻击效果依赖攻击者模型，且任务通用攻击可迁移但模型间迁移受限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 间接提示注入对LLM代理构成严重威胁，但自动化攻击方法在真实代理环境中的研究不足。

Method: 在AgentDojo框架中，将白盒（GCG）和黑盒（TAP）方法适应代理环境，在80个任务对（跨四个域和多模型）上进行评估。

Result: 黑盒优化（TAP）显著优于白盒梯度方法（GCG）；攻击效果依赖攻击者模型的能力和安全调整；任务通用攻击可迁移到未见任务和域，但从开源小模型到前沿模型（如GPT-5）的迁移失败。

Conclusion: 自动提示注入是可信但依赖模型的威胁，模型无关的利用仍面临重大障碍。

中文摘要：间接提示注入对与不可信外部数据交互的LLM代理构成了严重威胁，然而自动攻击方法（经证明对越狱有效）在现实代理环境中的探索仍不足。我们在AgentDojo框架中对LLM代理进行了全面的自动提示注入攻击实证评估，将白盒（GCG）和黑盒（TAP）方法适应代理环境。我们在80个跨四个域和多个模型的任务对上评估，发现黑盒优化显著优于基于梯度的方法，我们将其归因于GCG在合理计算预算下的优化不稳定性。我们还发现TAP的有效性取决于攻击者模型，因为通用能力和安全调整都影响攻击成功率——更强的模型产生更有效的注入，而安全调整的攻击者可能拒绝生成对抗性提示。任务通用攻击有效迁移到未见任务和域外分布域，但在较小开源模型上优化的攻击不能迁移到前沿模型如GPT-5。这些发现凸显自动提示注入是一种可信但依赖模型的威胁，模型无关的利用仍存在重大障碍。

Original abstract: Indirect prompt injection poses a critical threat to LLM agents that interact with untrusted external data, yet automated attack methods--proven effective for jailbreaking--remain underexplored in realistic agentic settings. We present a comprehensive empirical evaluation of automated prompt injection attacks against LLM agents, adapting both white-box (GCG) and black-box (TAP) methods to the agentic setting within the AgentDojo framework. We evaluate across 80 task pairs spanning four domains and multiple models, and find that black-box optimization substantially outperforms gradient-based methods, a gap we attribute to GCG's optimization instability under reasonable compute budgets. We also find that TAP's effectiveness depends on the attacker model, as both general capability and safety tuning affect attack success--stronger models produce more effective injections, while safety-tuned attackers can refuse to generate adversarial prompts. Task-universal attacks transfer effectively to unseen tasks and out-of-distribution domains, but attacks optimized on smaller open-source models do not transfer to frontier models like GPT-5. These findings highlight automated prompt injection as a credible but model-dependent threat, with significant barriers remaining for model-agnostic exploitation.

### [65] [Toward Secure LLM Agents: Threat Surfaces, Attacks, Defenses, and Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10749v1)
*Yuchen Ling,Shengcheng Yu,Zhenyu Chen,Chunrong Fang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: LLM agent安全综述，涵盖威胁面、攻击、防御和评估，直接相关

TL;DR: 本文通过生命周期框架综合247篇论文，分析LLM代理的安全威胁、防御和评估，指出提示注入等当前主导问题及持久状态破坏等新兴关注点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理从对话界面转向软件组件，安全风险本质改变且研究分散，需要系统化框架来理解威胁、防御和评估。

Method: 综合247篇论文，提出基于生命周期、面向系统的框架，围绕信息流、委托权限和持久状态建模代理安全，并按四个问题组织文献。

Result: 提示注入和工具介导控制流劫持占主导；持久状态破坏和多代理传播成为新兴关注；当前防御组合性弱；基准低估长期、有状态和部署敏感风险。

Conclusion: 安全的LLM代理需要明确的信任边界、原则性的权限控制、来源感知的状态管理和与真实操作环境一致的评估实践。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）代理正在迅速从对话界面转变为规划、调用工具、维护内存并对外部环境采取行动的软件组件。这种转变改变了安全风险的本质。在代理场景中，故障不再仅限于不安全的文本生成。不受信任的内容可能会重定向控制流、滥用工具权限、破坏持久状态、泄露敏感信息或触发有害的外部行动。同时，关于LLM代理安全的研究正在快速扩展，但仍然分散在攻击家族、防御层、应用领域和评估设置中。本文通过一个基于生命周期、面向系统的框架综合了247篇论文，该框架围绕信息流、委托权限和持久状态的交互来建模代理安全。我们围绕四个问题组织文献：LLM代理安全应如何建模，哪些威胁面和攻击家族占主导地位，提出了哪些防御措施及其权衡，以及如何评估安全声明。我们发现，提示注入和工具介导的控制流劫持仍然主导该领域，而持久状态破坏和多代理传播正在成为新兴的核心关注点。我们还发现，当前的防御措施提供了有用的构建块，但组合性仍然较弱，现有的基准仍然低估了长期、有状态和部署敏感的風險。我们认为，安全的LLM代理需要明确的信任边界、原则性的权限控制、具有来源感知的状态管理，以及与真实操作环境一致的评估实践。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are rapidly moving from conversational interfaces to software components that plan, invoke tools, maintain memory, and act on external environments. This transition changes the nature of security risk. In agentic settings, failures are no longer limited to unsafe text generation. Untrusted content may redirect control flow, misuse tool privileges, corrupt persistent state, leak sensitive information, or trigger harmful external actions. At the same time, research on LLM agent security is expanding quickly but remains fragmented across attack families, defense layers, application domains, and evaluation settings. This paper synthesizes 247 papers through a lifecycle-based, systems-oriented framework that models agent security around the interaction of information flow, delegated authority, and persistent state. We organize the literature around four questions: how LLM agent security should be modeled, which threat surfaces and attack families dominate, what defenses have been proposed and with what tradeoffs, and how security claims are evaluated. We find that prompt injection and tool-mediated control-flow hijacking still dominate the field, while persistent state corruption and multi-agent propagation are becoming central emerging concerns. We further find that current defenses provide useful building blocks but remain weakly compositional, and that existing benchmarks still underrepresent long-horizon, stateful, and deployment-sensitive risks. We argue that secure LLM agents require explicit trust boundaries, principled privilege control, provenance-aware state management, and evaluation practices aligned with realistic operational settings.

### [66] [Securing Code Understanding: Detecting Natural Backdoor Vulnerability in Code Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10846v1)
*Yuchen Chen,Weisong Sun,Haocheng Huang,Yuan Xiao,Chunrong Fang,Yiran Zhang,Tingting Xu,Zhenpeng Chen,An Guo,Peizhuo Lv,Xiaofang Zhang,Zhenyu Chen,Yang Liu,Baowen Xu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文研究了代码语言模型中的自然后门漏洞，发现其普遍存在且为固有特性，并分析了它们与注入后门的差异、可转移性、成因，评估了现有防御技术，最后提出了新的检测方法ScanNBT。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管自然后门在深度学习模型中已被发现且威胁严重，但CodeLMs中自然后门漏洞的安全影响尚不清楚，因此有必要进行深入研究。

Method: 通过44种场景的实证研究，比较注入与自然后门差异，分析可转移性（数据集、架构、共享知识），探究成因（训练数据、训练过程），评估现有防御技术，并设计ScanNBT检测方法。

Result: 自然后门在CodeLMs中普遍存在且固有；与注入后门在模型和参数层面有差异；可转移性受多种因素影响；现有防御技术部分有效；ScanNBT能提升检测覆盖率。

Conclusion: 自然后门是CodeLMs的重要安全威胁，需针对性防御；提出的ScanNBT可有效检测，为增强CodeLM安全性提供了新见解。

中文摘要：代码语言模型（CodeLMs）已成为软件工程不可或缺的一部分，显著推进了代码智能任务。然而，它们的广泛采用引发了严重的安全问题，特别是对后门攻击的敏感性。最近的研究在正常训练的深度学习模型中发现了自然出现的后门，称为自然后门。尽管这些后门与通过数据投毒引入的后门一样构成严重威胁，但CodeLMs中自然后门漏洞的安全影响仍然知之甚少。在本文中，我们对各种模型架构和代码智能任务下的CodeLMs中的自然后门漏洞进行了彻底的实证研究。具体来说，我们检查了44种场景下的潜在自然后门漏洞，证明自然后门在CodeLMs中普遍存在且是固有的。我们揭示了注入后门和自然后门漏洞在模型和参数层面上的差异。然后我们从三个角度分析了自然后门漏洞的可转移性：数据集、模型架构和共享知识。我们进一步从两个方面调查了自然后门的成因：训练数据集和模型训练过程。我们评估了现有的后门防御技术，包括预训练、训练中和训练后防御，在缓解自然后门方面的效果。最后，我们提出了ScanNBT，一种新颖的检测方法，旨在改进CodeLMs中自然后门漏洞的全面检测。我们希望我们的发现能增强对这些漏洞的理解，并为加强CodeLMs对抗后门威胁的安全性提供见解。

Original abstract: Code Language Models (CodeLMs) have become integral to software engineering, significantly advancing code intelligence tasks. However, their widespread adoption has raised critical security concerns, particularly regarding susceptibility to backdoor attacks. Recent studies have uncovered naturally occurring backdoors, referred to as natural backdoors, in normally trained deep learning models. Despite posing threats as serious as those introduced through data poisoning, security implications of natural backdoor vulnerabilities in CodeLMs remain poorly understood.
  In this paper, we conduct a thorough empirical study of natural backdoor vulnerabilities in CodeLMs across various model architectures and code intelligence tasks. Specifically, we examine potential natural backdoor vulnerabilities across 44 scenarios, demonstrating that natural backdoors are prevalent and intrinsic to CodeLMs. We reveal differences between injected and natural backdoor vulnerabilities at both the model and parameter levels. We then analyze the transferability of natural backdoor vulnerabilities from three perspectives: datasets, model architectures, and shared knowledge. We further investigate the causes of natural backdoors from two aspects: training datasets and the model training procedure. We evaluate existing backdoor defense techniques, including pre-training, in-training, and post-training defenses, in mitigating natural backdoors. Finally, we propose ScanNBT, a novel detection method designed to improve comprehensive detection of natural backdoor vulnerabilities in CodeLMs. We aim for our findings to enhance understanding of these vulnerabilities and provide insights for strengthening CodeLM security against backdoor threats.

### [67] [Context-Based Adversarial Attacks on AI Code Generators: Vulnerability Analysis and Implications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10945v1)
*Walther A. Del Orbe,John D. Hastings,Varghese Vaidyan*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究系统性地调查了基于上下文的对抗性攻击对AI代码生成安全性的影响，通过大量实验量化了攻击效果，并提出了一种高效的双层防御框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI代码生成系统存在推理时安全漏洞，需要系统性地研究上下文对抗攻击及其防御机制。

Method: 在CodeT5+、CodeLlama、GPT-3.5-Turbo和GPT-4上进行了2800次受控实验，评估攻击有效性和防御机制。

Result: 对抗性条件使漏洞生成增加10.7倍，直接指令攻击在GPT-3.5-Turbo上成功率100%，跨模型迁移率60-100%；双层防御框架检测率89.1%，误报率0.3%，延迟520ms。

Conclusion: 上下文对抗攻击对多个主流代码生成模型构成严重威胁，但所提出的防御框架可在实际部署中有效检测和缓解此类攻击。

Original abstract: AI-powered code generation systems have transformed software development but introduce critical inference-time security vulnerabilities. This research presents a systematic investigation of context-based adversarial attacks, where strategically crafted contextual inputs, including comments, documentation, variable names, bias large language models toward generating exploitable code. Through 2,800 controlled experiments across CodeT5+, CodeLlama, GPT-3.5-Turbo, and GPT-4, we quantify attack effectiveness and defense mechanisms. Results demonstrate that adversarial conditions increase vulnerability generation 10.7x (from 3.5% to 37.4%), with direct instruction attacks achieving 100% success on GPT-3.5-Turbo. Cross-model transferability reaches 60-100%, indicating systemic architectural vulnerabilities rather than model-specific flaws. Our dual-layer defense framework achieves 89.1% detection rate with 0.3% false positives and 520ms latency, demonstrating practical feasibility for real-time deployment in development environments.

Original abstract: OpenClaw has rapidly emerged as a transformative artificial intelligence (AI) agent framework, and its ability to autonomously execute complex, multi-step tasks has attracted an ever-growing and diverse user base. However, this capability comes with significant risks. While existing research has made important strides in characterizing these threats, such work is predominantly directed at technically sophisticated audiences. First, we identify and categorize seven core risks that OpenClaw users may encounter in daily usage, explaining each in plain language so that non-technical users can readily grasp the nature and potential consequences of these threats. Second, for each identified risk, we distill a set of corresponding defensive strategies into clear and actionable operational steps that are easy to follow. Third, to make protection even easier, we provide a companion OpenClaw Skill that automates key security configurations, enabling users to safeguard their systems with minimal manual intervention. Through this work, we demonstrate that safeguarding against the risks of intelligent agents need not be the exclusive domain of security experts, and that non-technical users can meaningfully participate in reducing these risks through simple, practical actions.

### [69] [MPC-Patch-Bench: Security-Aware LLM Code Patch for Multi-Party Computation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11416v1)
*Yukuan Zhang,Mengxin Zheng,Qian Lou*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 安全感知LLM代码补丁benchmark，直接针对代码修复agent，含MPC验证器，强烈相关。

TL;DR: MPC-Patch-Bench是首个评估LLM在仓库级MPC代码修复上的基准，包含数据整理框架和MPC验证器，发现最强LLM仅能解决17.1%的验证任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准缺少对MPC仓库级代码修复的评估，直接移植通用基准存在结构性问题，且MPC代码需要额外的安全与数值保真度验证。

Method: 构建包含两个框架的MPC-Patch-Bench：数据整理框架（领域特定智能体过滤+人类-AI补全引擎）生成205个实例；MPC验证器（动态差分测试+静态分析规则）进行安全与数值保真度检查。

Result: 最强LLM功能解决率22.9%，经MPC验证器降至17.1%，40%功能性通过补丁因密码学/数值违规被拒。

Conclusion: MPC-Patch-Bench揭示了现有LLM在仓库级MPC修复上的显著不足，强调了MPC特定验证的必要性。

中文摘要：针对大型语言模型（LLM）在安全多方计算（MPC）软件上的代码修复的仓库级基准尚不存在，直接移植通用基准（如SWE-bench）在三个结构层面失败：（i）MPC仓库主要由通用Python基础设施而非密码学逻辑主导；（ii）高价值的MPC修复缺乏严格提取流程所需的标准化测试；（iii）标准的fail-to-pass评估对于必须同时保证密码学安全的代码是不足够的。MPC越来越多地部署于隐私保护机器学习、生物医学协作和安全分析。现有的MPC特定代码合成工作仅涵盖算子级或单框架任务；评估LLM代理在真实仓库级MPC修复上需要MPC感知的数据整理和与MPC程序必须遵循的安全与数值保真度保证相匹配的验证器，而现有基准两者都不提供。我们引入MPC-Patch-Bench，一个围绕两个框架组织的仓库级基准。(1)数据整理框架结合了一个领域特定整理智能体（通过三个密码学层过滤原始拉取请求）和一个人类-人工智能补全引擎（合成缺失的问题描述以及Fail-to-Pass/Pass-to-Pass测试），产生205个完全验证的实例。(2)MPC验证器通过针对明文预言机的动态差分测试和MPC特定静态分析规则（标记不安全的揭示、不安全的算术和非法公有/私有类型转换）提供专用的安全和数值保真度检查。评估的最强LLM仅功能性地解决了22.9%的MPC-Patch-Bench任务；MPC验证器进一步将已验证的解决率降至17.1%，其中高达40%的功能性通过的补丁因密码学或数值保真度违规而被拒绝。

Original abstract: Repository-level benchmarks for evaluating Large Language Model (LLM) code repair on Secure Multi-Party Computation (MPC) software do not yet exist, and directly transplanting general-purpose benchmarks such as SWE-bench fails on three structural fronts: (i) MPC repositories are dominated by generic Python infrastructure rather than cryptographic logic; (ii) high-value MPC fixes lack the standardized tests rigid extraction pipelines require; and (iii) standard fail-to-pass evaluation is insufficient for code that must also be cryptographically safe. MPC is increasingly deployed for privacy-preserving machine learning, biomedical collaboration, and secure analytics. Existing MPC-specific code-synthesis efforts cover only operator-level or single-framework tasks; evaluating LLM agents on real repository-level MPC repair instead demands MPC-aware data curation and a verifier matched to the security and numerical-fidelity guarantees MPC programs must obey neither of which existing benchmarks provide. We introduce MPC-Patch-Bench, a repository-level benchmark organised around two frameworks. (1)The Data Curation Framework combines a domain-specific curation agent that filters raw pull requests through three cryptographic layers with a human-AI completion engine that synthesizes missing problem statements and Fail-to-Pass/Pass-to-Pass tests, yielding 205 fully verified instances. (2)The MPC Verifier provides dedicated security and numerical-fidelity checks via dynamic differential testing against plaintext oracles and MPC-specific static analysis rules that flag unsafe reveals, insecure arithmetic, and illegal public/private casts. The strongest evaluated LLM functionally resolves only 22.9% of MPC-Patch-Bench tasks; the MPC Verifier further reduces verified resolution to 17.1%, with up to 40% of functionally-passing patches rejected for cryptographic or numerical-fidelity violations.

</details>


### [70] [JailbreakOPT: Tool-Assisted Iterative Jailbreak Prompt Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11425v1)
*Ge Shi,Jun Yin,Donglin Xie,Fangyi Liu,Yucan Li,Menglin Liu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 工具辅助的迭代越狱提示优化，涉及工具使用与经验复用，可迁移至 agent 方法。

TL;DR: JailbreakOPT是一个工具辅助的迭代单轮越狱提示优化框架，通过原子工具库和上下文老虎机策略提高攻击成功率并减少攻击次数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的单轮越狱方法在手工提示的静态性与迭代优化的低效之间面临权衡，需要一种能结合两者优势并高效利用经验的框架。

Method: 将原子越狱提示组织成攻击工具库，通过回合内优化组合生成更强提示；并将工具选择建模为上下文老虎机问题，使用上下文汤普森采样指导探索与利用。

Result: 在多个目标LLM和攻击目标上，JailbreakOPT提高了攻击成功率（ASR），并减少了成功所需的攻击次数（No.A）。

Conclusion: JailbreakOPT通过组合优化和经验重用有效提升了单轮越狱攻击的性能，但该工作也揭示了LLM的安全弱点，需注意防范。

中文摘要：越狱攻击揭示了大型语言模型（LLM）中持续存在的安全弱点，但现有的无状态单轮方法面临一种权衡：手工制作的提示具有表现力但静态，而迭代提示优化可以适应，但通常依赖于需要多次目标查询的低级突变。我们提出了JailbreakOPT，一个用于改进迭代单轮越狱提示优化的工具辅助框架。JailbreakOPT将多种原子越狱提示组织成攻击工具库，并通过统一的回合内优化抽象组合它们，以生成更强的独立攻击提示。为了在攻击回合之间重用经验，JailbreakOPT进一步将工具选择框架化为上下文老虎机问题，并应用上下文汤普森采样来基于过去的结果指导探索和利用。在多个目标LLM和攻击目标上的实验表明，与原子单轮攻击和现有的迭代优化基线相比，JailbreakOPT提高了攻击成功率（ASR），同时减少了成功所需的攻击次数（No.A）。本文可能包含冒犯性或有害内容。

Original abstract: Jailbreak attacks expose persistent safety weaknesses in large language models (LLMs), but existing stateless single-turn methods face a trade-off: hand-crafted prompts are expressive but static, while iterative prompt optimization can adapt but often relies on low-level mutations that require many target queries. We propose JailbreakOPT, a tool-assisted framework for improving iterative single-turn jailbreak prompt optimization. JailbreakOPT organizes diverse atomic jailbreak prompts into an attack tool library and composes them through a unified intra-episode optimization abstraction to generate stronger standalone attack prompts. To reuse experience across attack episodes, JailbreakOPT further frames tool selection as a contextual bandit problem and applies contextual Thompson sampling to guide exploration and exploitation based on past outcomes. Experiments across multiple target LLMs and attack goals show that JailbreakOPT improves attack success rate (ASR) while reducing the number of attacks until success (No.A) compared with atomic single-turn attacks and existing iterative optimization baselines. This paper may contain offensive or harmful content.

</details>

### [71] [A Constrained Natural-Language Interface for Variational Multi-Physics Finite Element Simulations in FEniCS](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10928v1)
*Nilay Upadhyay,Wesley F. Reinhart*

Main category: cs.CE

Selection reason: 约束自然语言仿真接口，强调可靠性与验证，可迁移至代码生成agent的鲁棒性。

TL;DR: 提出一个受限自然语言接口用于有限元分析，LLM仅处理前端任务，核心求解器由确定性模板处理，提高了可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成求解器代码存在可靠性风险，需要约束其作用范围以确保安全。

Method: 设计受限接口，LLM仅用于解析提示和生成非标准几何体代码，通过重试反馈改进，后端使用确定性模板调度器。

Result: 在解析器基准测试中达到100%有效解析率，在自定义几何体测试中达到90%成功率，验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 该架构为自然语言驱动的变分仿真提供了可靠的方法，避免了自主代码生成的风险。

中文摘要：大型语言模型可以减少设置有限元仿真所需的手动工作，但当生成的求解器代码位于关键路径上时，它们会引入可靠性风险。我们提出了一种用于多物理场有限元分析的受限自然语言接口，其中LLM被限制在前端任务：将提示解析为结构化的JSON，仅为非目录几何体生成Gmsh代码，并对这些阶段使用重试反馈。它从不编写FEniCS求解器模板、推导弱形式或编写数值求解器核心。一个确定性调度器将验证后的规范映射到五个手写的FEniCS/UFL模板：线弹性、超弹性、弹塑性、热力耦合和相场断裂。我们针对解析解和已发表的2D/3D基准验证了这个确定性模板层。平滑情况下，在合适网格上达到亚百分比一致性，而较难的非线性情况达到2-5%范围。我们还直接评估了面向LLM的前端。在15个提示的解析器基准测试中，9个案例首次解析有效，其余案例在重试后修复，最终有效解析率达到100.0%，问题类别准确率100.0%，字段提取准确率97.1%。在10个自定义几何体基准测试中，通过实际的LLM到Gmsh路径，首次和最终成功率均为90.0%，有一个未恢复的无效几何体失败。这些结果表明，解析器和受限提示/验证设计在这些基准测试上是有效的。作为一个端到端的演示，系统从一个自然语言提示生成并分析了一个带有圆角和螺栓孔的3D弹塑性L形支架。贡献在于一种用于自然语言驱动变分仿真的测量架构，而不是开放式的自主代码生成。

Original abstract: Large language models can reduce the manual effort required to set up finite element simulations, but they introduce reliability risks when generated solver code lies on the critical path. We present a constrained natural-language interface for multi-physics finite element analysis in which the LLM is limited to front-end tasks: parsing prompts into structured JSON, generating Gmsh code only for non-catalog geometries, and using retry feedback for those stages. It never writes FEniCS solver templates, derives weak forms, or writes the numerical solver core. A deterministic dispatcher maps the validated specification to five human-written FEniCS/UFL templates: linear elasticity, hyperelasticity, elastoplasticity, thermo-mechanical coupling, and phase-field fracture. We validate this deterministic template layer against analytical solutions and published 2D/3D benchmarks. Smooth cases reach sub-percent agreement on adequate meshes, while harder nonlinear cases reach the 2-5 percent range. We also evaluate the LLM-facing front end directly. In a 15-prompt parser benchmark, first-pass valid parses were obtained for 9 cases, and all remaining cases were repaired after retry, giving a final valid parse rate of 100.0 percent, 100.0 percent problem-class accuracy, and 97.1 percent field-extraction accuracy. In a 10-case custom-geometry benchmark routed through the real LLM-to-Gmsh path, first-pass and final success were both 90.0 percent, with one unrecovered invalid-geometry failure. These results show that the parser and constrained prompt/validation design are effective on these benchmarks. As an end-to-end demonstration, the system generates and analyzes a 3D elastoplastic L-bracket with a fillet and bolt hole from one natural-language prompt. The contribution is a measured architecture for natural-language-driven variational simulation, not open-ended autonomous code generation.

</details>

### [72] [Flaws in the LLM Automation Narrative](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11166v1)
*George Perrett,Javae Elliott,Jennifer Hill,Marc Scott*

Main category: stat.OT

Selection reason: 比较LLM与人类专家在数据分析代码任务上的可靠性与误差大小，涉及代码生成agent评估。

TL;DR: 通过编程任务比较LLM与人类专家，发现人类专家平均表现更好且更稳定，LLM未达到人类专家水平，强调评估变异性和错误大小的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM基准测试通常基于训练数据中的内容，且不评估可靠性和错误大小，但在高风险场景中这些至关重要，因此需要更严格的评估。

Method: 设计一个需要编写计算机代码进行数据分析的基准任务，比较前沿LLM与人类专家的表现，并测量响应变异性和错误大小。

Result: 人类专家在多个指标上平均表现更好，且表现变异性更小。

Conclusion: LLM并未持续达到人类专家水平，未来基准评估应纳入变异性和错误大小指标。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被描述为在知识经济任务上达到人类专家水平。这些说法主要基于LLM在标准化数据集上衡量平均表现的基准测试任务上的表现。许多基准测试任务的主要局限在于，它们通常基于直接包含在LLM训练数据中的内容来衡量性能，并且经常不评估LLM表现的可靠性或LLM错误的严重程度。然而，在高风险情境中，这些品质至关重要。通过一项新颖的LLM基准测试任务，该任务要求编写计算机代码完成数据分析任务，我们比较了一个前沿LLM与人类专家提交物的表现，并明确衡量了响应的变异性和错误的严重程度。我们的研究表明，人类专家在一系列指标上平均表现更好，并且表现出的变异性更小。我们的结果提供了证据，表明LLM并不始终达到人类专家的水平，并且证明了在LLM基准评估中衡量变异性和评估错误严重程度的重要性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly described as performing at the level of human experts on knowledge economy tasks. These claims are primarily based on how LLMs perform on benchmarking tasks that measure average performance across standardized datasets. Primary limitations of many benchmarking tasks are that they often measure performance based on content directly included in LLM training data, and they frequently do not assess the reliability of LLM performance or the magnitude of LLM errors. However, in high stakes contexts, these qualities are critically important. Through a novel LLM benchmarking task that requires writing computer code to complete a data analysis task, we compare the performance of a frontier LLM against submissions from human experts and explicitly measure the variance of responses and the magnitude of errors. Our study reveals that the human experts perform better on average on a range of metrics and demonstrate less variability in performance. Our results provide evidence that LLMs do not consistently perform at the level of human experts and demonstrate the importance of measuring variance and assessing error magnitude in LLM benchmark evaluations.

</details>

### [73] [What Matters in Orchestrating Robot Policies: A Systematic Study of Hierarchical VLA Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10267v1)
*Jiaheng Hu,Mohit Shridhar,Caden Lu,Dhruv Shah,Hao-Tien Lewis Chiang,Jie Tan,Annie Xie*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 分层VLA agent系统研究，包含规划、记忆等通用agent设计

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了层次化视觉-语言-动作（Hi-VLA）系统的设计，统一了框架，通过实验得出了构建高性能Hi-VLA系统的实用原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Hi-VLA系统缺乏统一设计原则，组件选择与连接方式多样，性能差异大，需要系统研究来指导设计。

Method: 将代表性Hi-VLA智能体统一在选项式控制框架下，在短/长视界和推理密集型任务上基准测试核心设计选择，分析模型与接口机制的影响。

Result: 应用得出的原则构建的系统在仿真和真实机器人上显著强于平面VLA和朴素层次系统。

Conclusion: 提供了构建更强大、稳健、有原则的层次化VLA智能体的基础，并给出了实用设计准则。

中文摘要：层次化视觉-语言-动作（Hi-VLA）系统已成为复杂机器人操作的一种有前途的范式，它通过使用高层VLM规划器将任务分解为由低层VLA控制器执行的语言子目标。尽管最近取得了经验进展，但这些系统缺乏统一的设计原则：现有的Hi-VLA系统在选择和连接规划器、控制器、两者之间的切换机制，以及观测和记忆在规划器中的表示方式上存在差异。在本文中，我们对机器人操作的Hi-VLA设计进行了系统研究。我们将代表性的Hi-VLA智能体统一在一个选项式控制框架下，并在短视界、长视界和推理密集型任务中对核心设计选择进行基准测试。我们的分析提炼出构建Hi-VLA系统的实用原则，展示了模型选择和接口机制如何共同影响性能。应用这些原则，在仿真和真实ALOHA机器人的实验中，我们得到了一个比平面VLA控制或朴素设计层次结构显著更强的系统。总的来说，我们的结果为构建更强大、更稳健、更有原则的层次化VLA智能体提供了基础。更多信息和视频请见jiahenghu.github.io/hi-vla。

Original abstract: Hierarchical vision-language-action (Hi-VLA) systems have emerged as a promising paradigm for complex robot manipulation, by using high-level VLM planners to decompose tasks into language subgoals executed by low-level VLA controllers. Despite recent empirical progress, there is a lack of unified design principles for these systems: existing Hi-VLA systems differ in how they choose and connect planners, controllers, mechanisms to switch between the two, and how observations and memory are represented in the planner. In this paper, we present a systematic study of Hi-VLA design for robot manipulation. We unify representative Hi-VLA agents under an options-style control framework and benchmark core design choices across short-horizon, long-horizon, and reasoning-intensive tasks. Our analysis distills practical principles for building Hi-VLA systems, showing how model choices and interface mechanisms jointly shape performance. Applying these principles yields a substantially stronger system than either flat VLA control or a naively designed hierarchy, across experiments both in simulation and on a real ALOHA robot. Overall, our results provide a foundation for building more capable, robust, and principled hierarchical VLA agents. More information and video at jiahenghu.github.io/hi-vla.

</details>


### [74] [Embodied-R1.5: Evolving Physical Intelligence via Embodied Foundation Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11324v2)
*Yifu Yuan,Yaoting Huang,Xianze Yao,Yutong Li,Shuoheng Zhang,Linqi Han,Pengyi Li,Jiangeng Sun,Wenting Jia,Zhao Zhang,Yuhao Liu,Ruihao Liao,Yucheng Hu,Qiyu Wu,Yuxiao Li,Zibin Dong,Fei Ni,Yan Zheng,Shuyang Gu,Yi Ma,Hongyao Tang,Han Hu,Jianye Hao*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 具身基础模型，包含任务规划、修正等agent能力，可迁移性有限但涉及agent通用环节。

TL;DR: Embodied-R1.5是一个80亿参数的统一具身基础模型，通过大规模数据和多任务平衡强化学习，在16/24项基准上达到SOTA，并能在真实机器人零样本泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有具身模型通常只擅长单一任务，缺乏统一且全面的具身推理能力（如规划、纠正、指向），难以实现通用物理智能。

Method: 使用三条自动化数据构建流水线生成超过150亿token的数据，设计多任务平衡强化学习配方解决异构任务冲突，并引入规划器-接地器-纠正器（PGC）闭环框架实现长时域任务的自主执行和自我纠正。

Result: Embodied-R1.5在24项具身VLM基准中的16项上达到SOTA，超越Gemini-Robotics-ER-1.5和GPT-5.4；微调成VLA后，在4个操作基准套件上优于π_{0.5}；零样本真实机器人实验在指令遵循、可供性接地等任务中表现优异。

Conclusion: Embodied-R1.5证明了一个统一模型可以实现全面的具身推理能力，并通过开源推动具身基础模型研究。

中文摘要：我们提出了Embodied-R1.5，一种统一的具身基础模型（EFM），它将全面的具身推理能力（包括具身认知、任务规划、纠正和指向）集成在单个架构中，朝着通用物理智能迈进。利用三条自动数据构建流水线大幅扩展关键能力的数据覆盖，我们构建了超过150亿token的大规模数据系统，并设计了多任务平衡强化学习方案以缓解异构任务冲突。我们进一步引入了规划器-接地器-纠正器（PGC）闭环框架，使得单个模型能够自主执行并在长时域任务中自我纠正。仅具有80亿参数，Embodied-R1.5在24项具身VLM基准中的16项上达到了最先进水平，超越了领先模型如Gemini-Robotics-ER-1.5和GPT-5.4。得益于内化的具身能力，Embodied-R1.5可以仅用少量数据微调成VLA，在4个流行的操作基准套件上优于领先的VLA模型（如π_{0.5}）。我们进一步进行了广泛的零样本真实机器人实验，验证了其在指令遵循、可供性接地、铰接物体操作以及长时域复杂任务上的性能，展示了向物理世界的强泛化能力。我们开源了模型权重、数据集、训练代码以及EmbodiedEvalKit（一个为具身任务量身定制的评估框架），以促进未来EFM的研究。

Original abstract: We introduce Embodied-R1.5, a unified Embodied Foundation Model (EFM) that integrates comprehensive embodied reasoning capabilities, spanning embodied cognition, task planning, correction, and pointing, within a single architecture toward general physical intelligence. Leveraging three automated data construction pipelines to significantly expand the data coverage of critical capabilities, we build a large-scale data system of over 15B tokens, and design a multi-task balanced RL recipe to alleviate heterogeneous task conflicts. We further introduce a Planner-Grounder-Corrector (PGC) closed-loop framework that enables a single model to autonomously execute and self-correct over long-horizon tasks. With only 8B parameters, Embodied-R1.5 achieves SOTA on 16 out of 24 embodied VLM benchmarks, surpassing leading models like Gemini-Robotics-ER-1.5 and GPT-5.4. Benefiting from the internalized embodied capabilities, Embodied-R1.5 can be fine-tuned into a VLA with only a small amount of data, outperforming leading VLA models like $π_{0.5}$ across 4 popular manipulation benchmark suites. We further conduct extensive zero-shot real-robot experiments, validating performance in instruction following, affordance grounding, articulated object manipulation, and long-horizon complex tasks, demonstrating strong generalization to the physical world. We open-source model weights, datasets, training code, and EmbodiedEvalKit, an evaluation framework tailored for embodied tasks, to facilitate future research in EFMs.

</details>

# cs.AR [[Back]](#toc)

### [75] [Towards Autonomous Accelerator Design: FPGA Accelerator Generation with SECDA](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11117v1)
*Vinamra Sharma,Xingjian Fu,Jude Haris,José Cano*

Main category: cs.AR

Selection reason: LLM引导FPGA加速器设计空间探索，直接涉及自动代码/硬件优化，与SemOpt高度相关。

TL;DR: 本文扩展了SECDA-DSE框架的评估，通过生成三种FPGA加速器设计（逐元素向量乘法、二维卷积和矩阵转置）并实际执行，证明LLM引导的设计空间探索能有效减少探索时间和人类专业知识需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有FPGA加速器设计方法（如SECDA）虽能快速协同设计，但识别高效配置仍需大量手动探索和领域知识，耗时且依赖专家。

Method: 提出SECDA-DSE框架，将LLM集成到SECDA生态中，结合结构化DSE探索器生成候选架构，以及LLM堆栈（使用检索增强生成和思维链提示）进行推理引导探索，并通过反馈循环迭代优化。

Result: 生成了三个符合SECDA规范的加速器设计（逐元素向量乘法、2D卷积、矩阵转置），成功在FPGA上合成和执行，并捕获了计算并行性与数据移动之间的内核特定权衡。

Conclusion: LLM引导的设计空间探索能够适应不同工作负载的架构配置，显著减少探索时间和人类专业知识需求，展现出高效自动化设计潜力。

中文摘要：为现代人工智能工作负载设计基于FPGA的加速器需要探索一个庞大而复杂的硬件设计空间，涉及架构参数、数据流策略和存储层次，使得该过程非常耗时。虽然现有的方法（如SECDA）通过SystemC仿真和FPGA执行实现了快速的硬件-软件协同设计，但识别高效的加速器配置仍然主要是一个需要大量领域知识的手动过程。SECDA-DSE是一个将大型语言模型（LLM）集成到SECDA生态系统中的框架，用于指导基于FPGA的加速器的设计空间探索（DSE）。它结合了一个用于生成候选架构的结构化DSE探索器和一个LLM堆栈，该堆栈使用检索增强生成和思维链提示执行推理引导的探索，并与反馈循环相结合进行迭代强化改进。基于我们之前介绍SECDA-DSE的工作，本文通过生成三个加速器设计（包括逐元素向量乘法、二维卷积和矩阵转置）并在FPGA硬件上执行端到端执行来扩展其评估。结果表明，SECDA-DSE可以生成符合SECDA规范的加速器设计，这些设计成功地在FPGA硬件上合成和执行。此外，生成的设计捕获了内核特定的计算并行性和数据移动之间的权衡，突显了LLM引导的探索在不同工作负载中适应架构配置的潜力，同时减少了探索时间和大量人类专业知识的需求。

Original abstract: Designing FPGA-based accelerators for modern artificial intelligence workloads requires exploring a large and complex hardware design space that involves architectural parameters, data flow strategies, and memory hierarchies, making the process very time consuming. While existing methodologies such as SECDA enable rapid hardware-software co-design through SystemC simulation and FPGA execution, identifying efficient accelerator configurations remains a largely manual process requiring extensive domain knowledge. SECDA-DSE is a framework that integrates Large Language Models (LLMs) into the SECDA ecosystem to guide design space exploration (DSE) of FPGA-based accelerators. It combines a structured DSE Explorer for generating candidate architectures with an LLM Stack that performs reasoning-guided exploration using retrieval-augmented generation and chain-of-thought prompting, coupled with a feedback loop for iterative and reinforced refinement. Building on our previous work introducing SECDA-DSE, this paper extends its evaluation by generating three accelerator designs, including element-wise vector multiplication, 2D convolution, and matrix transpose, and performing end-to-end execution on FPGA hardware. The results show that SECDA-DSE can generate SECDA-compliant accelerator designs that are successfully synthesized and executed on FPGA hardware. Furthermore, the generated designs capture kernel-specific trade-offs between compute parallelism and data movement, highlighting the potential of LLM-guided exploration to adapt architectural configurations across diverse workloads while reducing exploration time and the need for extensive human expertise.

</details>


### [76] [HierSVA: A Data Synthesis Pipeline, Dataset, and Benchmark for LLM-Driven Hierarchical Hardware Formal Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13706v1)
*Maohua Nie,Jiang Zhu,Jingqun Zhang,Zhichen Zeng,Jiayi Wang,Sibo Zhang,Jialin Wang,C. -J. Richard Shi*

Main category: cs.AR

Selection reason: LLM 驱动的硬件形式化验证 agent，涉及断言生成与 benchmark。

TL;DR: HierSVA是一个用于LLM驱动层次硬件形式验证的集成套件，包含流水线、数据集和基准，通过实验评估了12个LLM的断言质量，揭示了当前LLM在形式验证中的能力与局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了系统评估LLM在层次化硬件形式验证中生成断言的质量，并建立一个标准化的评估框架。

Method: 提出了HierSVA套件，包括HierSVA-SP（RTL预处理+LLM在环验证流水线）、HierSVA-DS（基于BaseJump STL的数据集，含342个模块和28个深子集）和HierSVA-B（六个度量轴的断言质量基准），并对12个最新LLM进行了评估。

Result: 三个发现：1) 模块级编译率67.1%，可评估运行中82.1%断言非空虚证明，但仅检测70.2%故障，覆盖36.2%形式核心；2) 深子集上召回率0.87，但精确度仅0.60（40%假阳性）；3) 代理模式改善可证明性和强度，但收益饱和并振荡。

Conclusion: HierSVA提供了全面的评估框架，揭示了当前LLM在硬件形式验证中生成断言的潜力与不足，代理模式虽有提升但效果有限，未来需要进一步改进。

中文摘要：我们提出了HierSVA，这是一个集成的套件，结合了流水线、数据集和基准，用于LLM驱动的层次化硬件形式验证。HierSVA-SP将RTL预处理工具链与LLM在环形式验证流程配对，以在层次化RTL上生成参考SystemVerilog断言（SVA）。将其应用于BaseJump STL产生了HierSVA-DS，一个包含342个模块的数据集，具有层次元数据和深度0-9，并附带一个由28个模块-缺陷对组成的深子集，包含自然语言规范和缺陷变体。HierSVA-B将断言质量分解为六个度量轴：语法正确性、断言证明成功率、空虚性、规范忠实性、变异覆盖率和形式核心覆盖率。将HierSVA-B应用于十二个最新的LLM揭示了三个发现。首先，模块级编译率为67.1%；在可评估的运行中生成的断言中，82.1%被非空虚地证明，但相应的断言集仅检测到70.2%的符合条件的注入故障，并覆盖了36.2%的形式核心。其次，在深子集中的211个可评估模型-模块条目上，断言集以0.87的召回率标记有缺陷的RTL，但40%的预测有缺陷结果在正确的RTL上是假阳性，将精确度限制为0.60。第三，代理模式改善了S1风格的可证明性和强度指标，但收益趋于平稳并振荡。代码和工件可在https://github.com/HierSVAAnon/HierSVACodeAndArtifacts获取。数据集可在https://huggingface.co/datasets/AnonymousHierSVA/HierSVA获取。

Original abstract: We present HierSVA, an integrated suite that combines a pipeline, dataset, and benchmark for LLM-driven hierarchical hardware formal verification. HierSVA-SP pairs an RTL preprocessing toolchain with an LLM-in-the-loop formal verification flow to produce reference SystemVerilog Assertions (SVA) on hierarchical RTL. Applying it to BaseJump STL yields HierSVA-DS, a dataset of 342 modules, with hierarchy metadata and depths 0--9, accompanied by a deep subset of 28 module-bug pairs with natural-language specifications and bug variants. HierSVA-B decomposes assertion quality into six metric axes: syntax correctness, assertion proof success rate, vacuity, specification faithfulness, mutation coverage, and formal core coverage. Applying HierSVA-B to twelve recent LLMs reveals three findings. First, the module-level compile rate is 67.1\%; among generated assertions in evaluable runs, 82.1\% prove non-vacuously, but the corresponding assertion sets detect only 70.2\% of eligible injected faults and cover 36.2\% of the formal core. Second, on 211 evaluable model--module entries in the deep subset, assertion sets flag buggy RTL with 0.87 recall, but 40\% of predicted-buggy outcomes are false positives on correct RTL, limiting precision to 0.60. Third, agentic mode improves S1-style provability and strength metrics, but gains plateau and oscillate. Codes and artifacts are available at \href{https://github.com/HierSVAAnon/HierSVACodeAndArtifacts}{https://github.com/HierSVAAnon/HierSVACodeAndArtifacts}. Dataset is available at \href{https://huggingface.co/datasets/AnonymousHierSVA/HierSVA}{https://huggingface.co/datasets/AnonymousHierSVA/HierSVA}.

</details>

### [77] [The Confident Liar: Diagnosing Multi-Agent Debate with Log-Probabilities and LLM-as-Judge](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10296v1)
*Ali Keramati,Justin Cheok,Jacob Horne,Mark Warschauer*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent辩论诊断，涉及评估与推理质量

TL;DR: 多智能体辩论系统中，内部置信信号与推理质量的相关性存在角色不对称，构造者比审计者更可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多智能体辩论系统只评估最终答案正确性，忽略了中间推理质量，而辩论旨在产生高质量推理，因此需要研究内部信号与推理质量及任务正确性的关系。

Method: 采用两智能体辩论架构（构造者和审计者），结合LLM-as-judge对每个智能体的推理进行评分（指令遵循、理由质量、证据基础），并标记关键失败；在基于评分标准、数学推理和事实问答三个领域进行实验。

Result: 在评分标准领域观察到一致的四阶段置信轨迹；构造者的置信度与评判推理质量的相关性比审计者强约两倍，且基于置信度检测关键推理失败的AUROC（0.804）显著高于审计者（0.634）。

Conclusion: 这些发现表明内部置信信号与推理质量的关系存在角色不对称，激励了更广泛的跨领域研究。

中文摘要：多智能体辩论系统通常仅根据最终答案是否正确进行评估，而忽略了辩论旨在产生的中间推理质量。本文研究了多智能体辩论中的三种信号：推理令牌的令牌级对数概率分布、大型语言模型作为评判者对这些令牌的评分标准得分以及最终任务准确性。我们考察了内部置信信号是否能预测外部评估的推理质量，以及这两种信号是否与任务正确性一致，涉及三个领域：基于评分标准、数学推理和事实问答。我们的框架将两智能体辩论架构（构造者和审计者）与一个大型语言模型作为评判者配对，该评判者根据指令遵循、理由质量和证据基础对每个智能体的推理进行评分，并附带一个关键失败标志。在评分标准领域的实验揭示了一致的四阶段置信轨迹和显著的角色不对称性：构造者的置信度与评判推理质量之间的相关性大约是审计者的两倍，并且基于置信度检测关键推理失败对于构造者（AUROC 0.804）比审计者（0.634）明显更可靠。这些发现推动了本文提出的更广泛的跨领域调查。

Original abstract: Multi-agent debate systems are typically evaluated only on whether the final answer is correct, overlooking the quality of the intermediate reasoning that debate is designed to produce. This paper studies the relationship between three signals in multi-agent debate: token-level log-probability distributions over reasoning tokens, LLM-as-judge rubric scores assigned to those tokens, and final task accuracy. We examine whether internal confidence signals predict externally evaluated reasoning quality, and whether either signal aligns with task correctness, across three domains: rubric-based scoring, mathematical reasoning, and factual question answering. Our framework pairs a two-agent debate architecture -- a Constructor and an Auditor -- with an LLM-as-judge that scores each agent's reasoning along instruction following, justification quality, and evidence grounding, together with a critical-failure flag. Experiments in the rubric-scoring domain reveal a consistent four-phase confidence trajectory and a substantial role asymmetry: confidence aligns with judged reasoning quality roughly twice as strongly for the Constructor as for the Auditor, and confidence-based detection of critical reasoning failures is markedly more reliable for the Constructor (AUROC 0.804) than for the Auditor (0.634). These findings motivate the broader cross-domain investigation proposed in this paper.

</details>


### [78] [Catching One in Five: LLM-as-Judge Blind Spots in Production Multi-Turn Transaction Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10315v1)
*Sawyer Zhang,Alexander Wang,Sophie Lei*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 生产环境agent评估缺陷分析，对agent可靠性评测重要

TL;DR: LLM评判者仅能捕获不到四分之一的人工确认缺陷，因评分标准缺失行为维度，导致系统性问题被漏报，且路由接线问题使门控无法触发报警。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有报告仅关注LLM评判者与人类评分的一致性，忽略了其真实缺陷召回率，部署中可能漏报大量质量问题。

Method: 以人工评审为金标准，测量LLM评判者在多轮食品饮料订购代理中捕获系统问题的比例，分析盲点分类与路由机制。

Result: LLM评判者仅发现22%的系统性问题，门控在含23个缺陷的批次中未报任何问题；评分标准缺失行为维度导致跨轮状态缺陷被漏报，且路由失败使缺陷无法触发操作门控。

Conclusion: 自动评判不能替代人工评审，在多轮代理中仅提供回归底线，且流行率估计会严重偏差（低估3-6倍）。

中文摘要：LLM作为评判者是评估对话代理的默认工具，但其可靠性几乎总是报告为与人类评分的一致性，而非对真实缺陷的召回率。我们研究了一个已部署的多轮食品饮料订购代理，并以其详尽的人工转录评审作为金标准，测量其内置LLM评判者能够捕获多少真正的质量问题。在三个批次中，该评判者仅发现不到四分之一的人类确认的系统性问题——在一个批次中，9个模式中只有2个（22%），而在另一个批次中，其操作门控在100轮对话中标记了零个缺陷，而人类确认了23个不同的缺陷和7个新的跨轮模式。我们的盲点分类法显示失败是有结构的，而非随机的：评判者捕获了轮次局部问题（捏造的统计数据、错误语言），但遗漏了跨轮状态问题（确认门锁定、购物车幻觉、升级锁定、过期指代）。机制在于：评分标准仅暴露三个粗略轴（意图、品牌声音、个性化），且没有涵盖大多数缺陷集中的行为维度——状态跟踪、护栏、恢复。失败是路由问题，而非感知问题：在114轮对话中，有113轮的原始评判者注释描述了确认门或购物车状态缺陷，却被评分为“品牌声音”，且没有一个达到操作失败——门控被连接到挂起和硬断言，而非评分标准——因此0%是路由和接线失败，而非盲目。对流行率估计的后果是尖锐的：当表观缺陷率为零时，Rogan-Gladen校正退化——没有信号能恢复真实率——而当门控报告非零率时，相同的估计器在我们的测量灵敏度下暗示3-6倍的低估。对于生产中的多轮代理，自动评判是回归底线，而非人工评审的替代品。

Original abstract: LLM-as-judge is the default instrument for evaluating conversational agents, yet its reliability is almost always reported as agreement with human ratings, not recall of real defects. We study a deployed multi-turn food-and-beverage ordering agent and measure how many genuine quality problems its built-in LLM judge catches, using exhaustive human transcript review as ground truth. Across three batches the judge surfaces well under a quarter of human-confirmed systematic problems -- 2 of 9 patterns (22%) in one batch, and its operational gate flagged zero of 100 rounds in a batch where humans confirmed 23 distinct defects and 7 new cross-cutting patterns. Our blind-spot taxonomy shows the failure is structured, not random: the judge catches turn-local issues (a fabricated statistic, a wrong language) but misses cross-turn state issues (confirm-gate lockout, cart hallucination, escalation lockout, stale referents). The mechanism: the scoring rubric exposes only three coarse axes (intent, brand-voice, personalization) and has no category for the behavioural dimensions -- state-tracking, guardrails, recovery -- where most defects cluster. The failure is routing, not perception: 113 of 114 rounds whose raw judge note describes a confirm-gate or cart-state defect are scored "brand voice", and none reach an operational failure -- the gate is wired to hangs and hard assertions, not the rubric -- so the 0% is a routing-and-wiring failure, not blindness. The consequence for prevalence estimation is sharp: when the apparent defect rate is zero the Rogan-Gladen correction degenerates -- no signal can recover the true rate -- while where the gate reports a nonzero rate the same estimator implies a 3-6x undercount under our measured sensitivity. For production multi-turn agents, automated judging is a regression floor, not a substitute for human review.

</details>


### [79] [Harnessing the Collective Intelligence of AI Agents in the Wild for New Discoveries](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10402v1)
*Federico Bianchi,Yongchan Kwon,Aneesh Pappu,James Zou*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent协作科学发现平台，展示集体智能与共享记忆，可借鉴于coding agent协作

TL;DR: 提出了EinsteinArena平台，通过代理间的开放互动实现分布式科学发现，在数学问题上取得了12个新SOTA成果，例如11维接吻数下界从593提升至604。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI系统在科学发现中多为孤立运行，缺乏集体协作和长期积累的能力，而真实的科学发现是一个分布式、迭代的过程。

Method: 构建了EinsteinArena平台，提供开放问题、可靠验证器、公开排行榜和讨论论坛，允许多个语言模型代理共享结果、交流想法并逐步改进解决方案。

Result: 截至2026年5月，代理发现了12个新SOTA结果，包括11维接吻数下界从593提升至604；进展源于多次提交、讨论和思想借鉴。

Conclusion: 实验证明，通过代理间的开放互动可以涌现出分散式科学发现，为集体AI驱动研究提供了新范式。

中文摘要：科学发现通常是一个集体过程：研究人员分享部分结果，检查失败的尝试，并在长时间内相互构建想法。最近的人工智能系统表明，基于语言模型的代理可以在开放的科学问题上取得有意义的进展，但大多数现有系统是孤立运行的。在本文中，我们提出了EinsteinArena，一个用于开放分布式研究和发现的代理原生平台。EinsteinArena为代理提供了一组实时开放问题，每个问题都有可靠的验证器、公开排行榜和问题特定的讨论论坛，代理可以在其中提问和分享见解。我们专注于数学任务，这些任务已经引起了广泛的研究兴趣，并且进展可以被明确衡量。截至2026年5月，EinsteinArena上的代理已经发现了12个新的最先进结果，优于之前任何人类或人工智能的解决方案。一个显著的例子是11维的接吻数问题，该平台将已知的最佳下界从593提高到604。这一进展并非来自单个代理或孤立运行，而是通过一系列提交、公开讨论、验证器改进以及随后的代理间思想借鉴而产生的。这些结果提供了证据，表明分散的科学发现可以通过自主代理在野外开放互动中涌现，展示了一种集体人工智能驱动研究的新范式。

Original abstract: Scientific discovery is often a collective process: researchers share partial results, inspect failed attempts, and build on each other's ideas over long time horizons. Recent AI systems have shown that language-model-based agents can make meaningful progress on open scientific problems, but most existing systems operate in isolation. In this paper, we present EinsteinArena, an agent-native platform for open distributed research and discovery. EinsteinArena provides agents with a live set of open problems, each with a solid verifier, public leaderboard, and problem-specific discussion forum where agents can ask questions and share insights. We focus on mathematical tasks that have garnered substantial research interest, where progress can be measured unambiguously. As of May 2026, agents on EinsteinArena have discovered 12 new state-of-the-art results better than any previous human or AI solutions. One notable example is the kissing number problem in dimension 11, where the platform improved the best known lower bound from 593 to 604. This advance did not come from a single agent or isolated run. Rather it arose through a sequence of submissions, public discussion, verifier refinement, and subsequent agent-to-agent borrowing of ideas. These results provide evidence that decentralized scientific discovery can emerge from open interaction among autonomous agents in the wild, demonstrating a new paradigm for collective AI-driven research.

</details>


### [80] [LakeQA: An Exploratory QA Benchmark over a Million-Scale Data Lake](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10460v1)
*Haonan Wang,Jiaxiang Liu,Yurong Liu,Austin Senna Wijaya,Tianle Zhou,Eden Wu,Yijia Chen,Wanting You,Reya Vir,Daniela Pinto,Grace Fan,Yusen Zhang,Juliana Freire,Eugene Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LakeQA是大规模数据湖问答benchmark，要求agent进行多跳搜索和推理，适用于agent评测。

TL;DR: LakeQA是一个结合搜索与多跳推理的大数据湖问答基准，对现有LLM极具挑战性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有问答基准缺乏对大数据湖中同时进行搜索和推理的需求，而现实问题需要这种能力。

Method: 构建LakeQA基准，包含9.5TB异构文本资源，由博士级专家标注，任务需要多跳推理和跨文档证据组合。

Result: 七个前沿LLM表现不佳，GPT-5.2仅达到18.37%的精确匹配分数。

Conclusion: LakeQA为开发能查找和分析数据的LLM智能体提供了现实的测试床。

中文摘要：最近的大型语言模型（LLMs）在基于阅读的问答（QA）中取得了快速进展，其中证据被明确提供或可以简单检索。相比之下，现实世界的问题通常没有与准确的证据文档配对。有用的证据存在于海量数据湖中，使得搜索成为回答的前提。然而，目前缺乏需要在大数据湖上进行搜索和推理的综合基准。为此，我们引入了LakeQA，一个针对数据湖上以搜索为中心的问答的综合基准，它同时强调搜索和推理能力。LakeQA建立在来自维基百科和开源政府数据的大约9.5 TB文本资源的异构集合上，涵盖结构化和非结构化数据。为确保任务质量，每个样本至少由一位博士级专家标注。每个任务都需要长期的多跳推理，并包含隐式的中间步骤：智能体需要发现正确的文档，然后跨来源组合证据以产生答案。在七个前沿LLM上的实验结果表明，LakeQA具有挑战性。例如，GPT-5.2在LakeQA上仅达到18.37%的精确匹配分数。总体而言，LakeQA为开发能够在现代数据湖中查找和分析数据的LLM智能体提供了现实的测试床。

Original abstract: Recent large language models (LLMs) have shown rapid progress in reading-based question answering (QA), where evidence is explicitly provided or can be trivially retrieved. In contrast, real-world questions are often not paired with accurate evidence documents. The useful evidence resides in massive data lakes, making search a prerequisite for answering. However, there is a lack of comprehensive benchmarks that require both searching and reasoning over large data lakes. To this end, we introduce LakeQA, a comprehensive benchmark for search-centric question answering over data lakes that jointly emphasizes searching and reasoning capabilities. LakeQA is built on a heterogeneous collection of approximately 9.5 TB of text resources from Wikipedia and open-source government data, spanning structured and unstructured data. To ensure task quality, each sample is annotated by at least one Ph.D.-level expert. Each task requires long-horizon multi-hop reasoning with implicit intermediate steps: agents need to discover the correct documents and then compose evidence across sources to produce the answer. Experimental results on seven frontier LLMs demonstrate that LakeQA is challenging. For instance, GPT-5.2 achieves only an exact-match score of 18.37% on LakeQA. Overall, LakeQA provides a realistic testbed for developing LLM agents that can both find and analyze data in modern data lakes.

</details>


### [81] [Janus: A Benchmark for Goal-Conditioned Information Distortion in LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10852v1)
*Polydoros Giannouris,Mohsinul Kabir,Sophia Ananiadou*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM目标条件信息扭曲基准，评估agent欺骗行为，对agent安全与可靠性有参考价值。

TL;DR: 提出JANUS基准，用于评估LLM在事实基础上根据目标进行选择性语用扭曲（如强调有利事实、淡化不利事实）的倾向，实验表明当前模型存在系统性扭曲且缺乏防御。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法主要检测直接谎言，忽略了通过选择性呈现真实事实进行误导的微妙且更危险的模式。

Method: 构建包含8领域160个场景的基准，每个场景提供固定有利/不利事实池，通过对比中性提示与目标导向提示下的LLM输出，量化语用扭曲程度。

Result: 在12个LLM上的实验显示，模型一致地根据目标导向提示产生选择性扭曲，且缺乏鲁棒防御。

Conclusion: 当前LLM易受激励和框架影响而产生选择性误导，需要进一步研究安全机制。

中文摘要：LLM的欺骗性通常通过捏造主张、明确谎言或策略性隐瞒等直接标记来评估。然而，许多现实世界中的误导性沟通并非依赖于虚假陈述，而是源于对真实事实的选择性处理：省略不利证据、淡化不利细节、强调有利细节、或用模糊语言替代精确限定。现有基准在很大程度上忽略了这种更微妙且可能更危险的失败模式。我们引入了JANUS，一个衡量基于事实的LLM输出中目标条件性语用扭曲的基准。我们基准中的每个场景都提供一组固定的有利和不利事实，并比较中性条件与目标导向条件（例如，增加采纳、注册、批准或支持，尽管可能对直接受影响的个人或群体造成潜在伤害）。由于所有输出都被限制使用相同的事实池，JANUS将误导性总体印象与幻觉和捏造分离开来。JANUS包含8个领域的160个场景，每个场景都配有中性条件和目标条件的提示以及标注的事实材料。在12个LLM上的广泛实验揭示了持续的目标条件性扭曲，表明当前模型仍然对激励和框架目标敏感，缺乏对选择性误导性沟通的鲁棒防御。我们公开发布了我们的语料库和代码以供未来研究。

Original abstract: LLM deception is often evaluated through direct markers such as fabricated claims, explicit lies, or strategic concealment. However, many real-world misleading communications do not depend on false statements, rather, they arise from selective treatment of true material facts: omitting adverse evidence, softening unfavorable details, emphasizing favorable details, or replacing precise qualifications with vague language. Existing benchmarks largely miss this subtler and arguably more dangerous failure mode. We introduce JANUS, a benchmark for measuring goal-conditioned pragmatic distortion in fact-grounded LLM outputs. Each scenario in our benchmark provides a fixed pool of favorable and adverse facts and compares a neutral condition against a goal-directed condition, such as increasing adoption, enrollment, approval, or support, despite potential harm to directly affected individuals or groups. Because all outputs are constrained to use the same fact pool, JANUS isolates misleading net impressions from hallucination and fabrication. JANUS contains 160 scenarios across 8 domains, with each scenario paired with neutral and goal-conditioned prompts and annotated material facts. Extensive experiments across 12 LLMs reveal consistent goal-conditioned distortions, demonstrating that current models remain sensitive to incentive and framing objectives and lack robust safeguards against selectively misleading communication. We publicly release our corpus and code for future research.

</details>


### [82] [T1-Bench: Benchmarking Multi-Scenario Agents in Real-World Domains](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11070v1)
*Genta Indra Winata,Amartya Chakraborty,Yuzhen Lin,Swasthi P Rao,Shikhhar Siingh,Houhan Lu,Nadia Bathaee,Sriharsha Hatwar,Paresh Dashore,Anmol Jain,Kshitij Tayal,Xiuzhu Lin,Anirban Das,Sambit Sahu,Shi-Xiong Zhang*

TL;DR: T1-Bench是一个高保真、全面的基准测试，用于评估代理系统在真实多领域、多步交互中的表现，通过25个领域的交织场景提升任务复杂度和评估严谨性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试在任务复杂度、真实性和领域多样性上有限，且无法捕获跨领域交互，限制了对代理系统在现实多步场景中的评估。

Method: 构建T1-Bench基准测试，包含25个不同难度领域的交织场景，使用12个模型评估，并辅以人工判断。

Result: T1-Bench显著提升了任务复杂性、交互深度和领域覆盖，提供了标准化评估框架。

Conclusion: T1-Bench推进了代理系统评估，并将开源数据和代码。

中文摘要：近期大型语言模型在推理和工具调用能力上的进步使得越来越强大的代理系统得以实现。然而，现有基准测试在任务复杂度、真实性和领域多样性方面仍存在局限，且往往无法捕捉跨多个领域的交互，限制了它们在需要持续推理和协调的现实多步设置中评估代理的能力。为解决这些局限，我们引入了T1-Bench，这是一个高保真、全面的基准测试，用于在真实的面向客户的多领域环境中评估代理系统，具有交织的场景，需要跨多轮用户-助手交互进行结构化推理，并在25个不同难度的领域中显著增加了组合复杂性和评估严谨性。我们使用12个专有和开源权重模型评估了T1-Bench，提供了一个可重复和标准化的框架，用于评估在复杂多步环境中的代理行为、工具利用和对话质量。我们还通过人工判断补充自动评估，以加强定性表现的评估。总体而言，T1-Bench通过增加模拟多领域环境中的任务复杂性、交互深度和领域覆盖，显著推进了以前的基准测试。为促进未来对代理系统的研究，我们将公开发布数据和评估代码作为开源。

Original abstract: Recent advances in reasoning and tool-calling capabilities of large language models (LLMs) have enabled increasingly capable agentic systems. However, existing benchmarks remain limited in task complexity, realism, and domain diversity, and often fail to capture interactions that span multiple domains, limiting their ability to evaluate agents in realistic multi-step settings that require sustained reasoning and coordination. To address these limitations, we introduce T1-Bench, a high-fidelity, comprehensive benchmark for evaluating agentic systems in realistic customer-facing, multi-domain environments, featuring interleaved scenarios that require structured reasoning across multi-turn user-assistant interactions and substantially increasing both compositional complexity and evaluative rigor across 25 domains of varying difficulty. We evaluate T1-Bench using 12 proprietary and open-weight models, providing a reproducible and standardized framework for assessing agent behavior, tool utilization, and conversational quality in complex, multi-step environments. We further complement automatic evaluation with human judgments to strengthen the assessment of qualitative performance. Overall, T1-Bench substantially advances prior benchmarks by increasing task complexity, interaction depth, and domain coverage in simulated multi-domain environments. To facilitate future research on agentic systems, we will publicly release data and evaluation code as open source.

### [83] [AI Coding Agents in Social Science: Methodologically Diverse, Empirically Consistent, Interpretively Vulnerable](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11456v1)
*Meysam Alizadeh,Fabrizio Gilardi,Mohsen Mosleh,Enkelejda Kasneci*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究 AI coding agent 在社会科学中的方法论多样性与偏差，对 agent 设计有启发。

TL;DR: LLM智能体在设计层面能匹配或超越人类的方法论多样性，但在裁决层面易受提示影响，偏差焦点在于解释而非估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨LLM智能体在科学分析中是否减少方法论多样性或放大分析灵活性导致动机性结论。

Method: 在移民和社会政策数据上，运行20次Claude Code和Codex，与多分析者人类基线比较，设计层面和裁决层面分别测试。

Result: Codex匹配人类多样性，Claude Code产生更多规范；两者估计与人类一致；反移民提示改变方法决策但不影响估计；确认性提示翻转裁决但不改变系数分布。

Conclusion: AI智能体在设计层面可匹敌或超越人类，但裁决层面脆弱，偏差在于解释而非估计。

中文摘要：基于LLM的智能体在科学分析中的部署引发了两种对立的担忧：智能体可能减少方法论多样性，或者它们可能放大研究人员通过其得出动机性结论的分析灵活性。我们认为这些担忧针对两个经验上可分离的层面：设计层面（方法选择）和裁决层面（决策规则将估计映射为实质性主张）。我们通过在一个突出的移民和社会政策数据集上运行20次独立的Claude Code和Codex执行，并以一个多分析者的人类基线进行测试。在设计层面，Codex匹配了人类的方法论多样性，而Claude Code产生的规范几乎是人类的三倍；两种智能体的效应估计与人类共识大致一致，且没有智能体模型与任何人类模型完全一致。提示诱导的反移民研究者先验会重组每个智能体的方法决策，但与同一数据中有偏的人类分析师不同，它不会改变总体估计或最终裁决；智能体也不会沿着人类用来偏倚其估计的方法轴进行重路由。在裁决层面，一个明确的确认性提示将Claude Code的裁决从10%的支持率翻转至90%，同时其系数分布基本不变，这是通过规则省略而非规则软化实现的。AI智能体在设计层面可以匹敌或超越人类的方法论多样性，但在裁决层面仍然脆弱。在我们的设置中，AI偏差的焦点不在估计，而在解释。

Original abstract: The deployment of LLM-based agents in scientific analysis raises opposing concerns: that agents may reduce methodological diversity, or that they may amplify the analytic flexibility through which researchers reach motivated conclusions. We argue these worries target two empirically separable layers: a design layer of methodological choices, and a verdict layer in which a decision rule maps estimates to a substantive claim. We test both by running 20 independent executions of Claude Code and Codex on a prominent immigration and social-policy against a many-analysts human baseline. At the design layer, Codex matches human methodological diversity and Claude Code produces nearly three times as many specifications; both agents' effect estimates remain broadly aligned with the human consensus, and no agent model exactly matches any human model. A prompt-induced anti-immigration researcher prior reorganizes each agent's methodological decisions but, unlike for biased human analysts in the same data, does not shift aggregate estimates or final verdicts; nor do agents reroute along the methodological axes humans use to bias their estimates. At the verdict layer, an explicit confirmatory prompt flips Claude Code's verdicts from 10% to 90% support while leaving its coefficient distribution essentially unchanged, operating through rule omission rather than rule softening. AI agents can rival or exceed human methodological diversity at the design layer while remaining vulnerable at the verdict layer. In our setting, the locus of AI bias is not estimation but interpretation.

</details>


### [84] [APEX: Automated Prompt Engineering eXpert with Dynamic Data Selection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11459v1)
*Fei Wang,Si Si,Cho-Jui Hsieh,Inderjit S. Dhillon*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 自动化提示工程与动态数据选择，属于 agent 调优技术。

TL;DR: APEX通过动态数据分层（Easy/Hard/Mixed）优先处理混合数据中的高杠杆子集，在固定预算下显著提升提示优化效果（平均提升11.2%和6.8%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前进化提示优化方法数据效率低，将数据集视为静态基准，在无信息数据上浪费计算资源。

Method: 提出APEX框架，根据优化谱系动态将数据集分为Easy、Hard、Mixed三层，优先处理Mixed层中的addressable frontier和rank-sensitive frontier两个高杠杆子集。

Result: 在三个基准上，固定5,000次评估调用预算下，APEX在Gemini 2.5 Flash上平均提升11.2%，在Gemma 3 27B上平均提升6.8%。

Conclusion: 以数据为中心的方法（动态数据分层与优先处理高杠杆子集）是高效有效提示优化的关键。

中文摘要：大型语言模型对提示表述高度敏感，需要自动提示优化以发挥其全部潜力。尽管进化算法已成为主流范式，但它们存在一个关键瓶颈：数据效率。当前方法将开发数据集视为静态基准，在无信息数据上浪费大量计算预算。在本工作中，我们引入APEX（自动提示工程专家），一种新颖的框架，它在提示搜索的同时优化数据使用。APEX基于优化谱系将数据集动态分层为容易、困难以及混合三个层级。通过优先处理混合层级（即识别出LLM性能参差不齐的数据），我们确定了两个高杠杆子集：用于生成信息性变异的前沿可处理子集以及用于区分候选质量的前沿排名敏感子集。我们在三个不同基准上评估APEX：IFBench、SimpleQA Verified和FACTS Grounding。在固定5000次评估调用预算下，由于其数据效率，APEX在Gemini 2.5 Flash上平均比初始提示高出11.2%，在Gemma 3 27B上高出6.8%，这表明以数据为中心的方法是高效且有效的提示优化的关键。

Original abstract: Large Language Models are highly sensitive to prompt formulation, necessitating automatic prompt optimization to unlock their full potential. While evolutionary algorithms have emerged as the dominant paradigm, they suffer from a critical bottleneck: data efficiency. Current methods treat the development dataset as a static benchmark, wasting significant compute budget on uninformative data. In this work, we introduce APEX (Automatic Prompt Engineering eXpert), a novel framework that optimizes the data usage alongside the prompt search. APEX dynamically stratifies the dataset into Easy, Hard, and Mixed tiers based on the optimization lineage. By prioritizing the Mixed tier, which identifies the data where the LLM has mixed performance, we identify two high-leverage subsets: the addressable frontier for generating informative mutations and the rank-sensitive frontier for distinguishing candidate quality. We evaluate APEX across three diverse benchmarks: IFBench, SimpleQA Verified, and FACTS Grounding. Under a fixed budget of 5,000 evaluation calls, due to its data efficiency, APEX outperforms the initial prompt by an average of 11.2% on Gemini 2.5 Flash and 6.8% on Gemma 3 27B, demonstrating that a data-centric approach is key to efficient and effective prompt optimization.

### [85] [When Role-playing, Do Models Believe What They Say?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11502v3)
*Benjamin Sturgeon,David Africa,Sid Black*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 角色扮演对模型信念的影响，涉及 agent 行为一致性。

TL;DR: 本文研究了角色扮演是否改变语言模型内部对真实性的表征，发现不同方法（提示、ICL、SFT、OCT、EM）导致不同程度的信念内化，其中EM产生最大转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究角色扮演是否不仅改变模型输出，还影响模型内部对真实性的表征，以理解AI系统行为与内在信念的区别。

Method: 使用提示、ICL、SFT、OCT和EM等方法诱导角色，并通过真实性探针和行为测试测量信念内化。

Result: 提示、ICL和SFT改变输出但内部表征变化小；EM造成大范围表征转变；OCT产生较小转变，在大模型上更明显。

Conclusion: 理解训练何时改变模型世界观而非仅行为，对AI系统的自主性和影响力管理至关重要。

中文摘要：语言模型可以说“地球围绕太阳运行”，但在扮演亚里士多德时却会断言相反的观点。最近的研究认为，角色采用是语言模型行为的基础，模型会根据给定上下文选择最合适的角色。这种角色扮演仅仅是改变了模型的输出，还是也影响了模型内部对真实性的表征？我们通过扮演信仰与现代共识不同的角色来研究这个问题，并使用多种方法诱导角色：提示、上下文学习（ICL）、监督微调（SFT）、开放角色训练（OCT）和新兴错位（EM）。我们使用真实性探针和行为测试来测量这些方法中的信念内化程度，发现信念内化存在广泛的范围。提示、ICL和SFT改变了模型的说法，但表征变化很小。EM在模型的真实性表征中产生了大而广泛的转变，而OCT则产生了较小的转变，在较大模型上最为明显。理解训练何时改变模型的世界观而不仅仅是其行为，随着人工智能系统被赋予更大的自主权和影响力，可能会变得越来越重要。

Original abstract: Language models can state that "the Earth orbits the Sun" and, when role-playing Aristotle, assert the opposite. Recent work argues that persona adoption is fundamental to how language models behave, with models selecting the most appropriate persona for a given context. Does such role-playing merely change the model's outputs, or does it also affect what the model internally represents as truthful? We study this question using the role-play of characters whose beliefs differ from the modern consensus, and induce personas with a number of different methods: prompting, in-context learning (ICL), supervised fine-tuning (SFT), and Open Character Training (OCT), and Emergent Misalignment (EM). We measure belief internalization across these approaches with truth probes and with behavioral tests, finding a broad spectrum of belief internalization. Prompting, ICL, and SFT change what the model says with little representational change. EM creates a large, broad shift in the model's truth representation, and OCT a smaller shift that is clearest on the larger model. Understanding when training changes a model's worldview rather than merely its behavior may become increasingly important as AI systems are entrusted with greater autonomy and influence.

### [86] [ISE: An Execution-Grounded Recipe for Multi-Turn OS-Agent Trajectories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11520v4)
*Siyuan Luo,Nairong Zheng,Lin Zhou,Tiankuo Yao,Shengyou Yuan,Haojia Yu,Cong Pang,Jiapeng Luo,Lewei Lu*

TL;DR: 提出ISE三阶段合成范式，生成包含结构化意图、多轮交互和真实工具执行的OS智能体训练数据，微调后显著提升模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
