Method: ISE范式：阶段一用4D框架构建结构化意图池；阶段二用角色锁定模拟器生成多轮轨迹；阶段三在实时OS工作空间中执行工具调用，产生真实故障恢复动态。

Result: 在ClawEval上，Qwen3-8B微调后pass@1从19.3提升至37.7，超越零样本GPT-4o和四倍大的Qwen3-32B。

Conclusion: ISE方法有效解决了数据缺失问题，多轮模拟是关键性能提升因素，已开源代码和数据集。

中文摘要：训练有能力的操作系统智能体需要能够同时捕获结构化用户意图、多轮任务委派和基于真实环境的工具执行的数据——这些属性在现有数据集中是缺失的。我们提出ISE（意图→模拟→执行），一种三阶段合成范式，共同解决这些差距。第一阶段通过一个4D框架（人物×领域×任务×复杂度）构建约50000个结构化意图；去重后池中包含43956个独特意图，并在mpnet-base-v2嵌入（余弦核，q=1）上对整个池达到61.57的Vendi分数。第二阶段通过一个角色锁定的用户模拟器驱动多轮用户-智能体交互，该模拟器将每一轮用户话语基于实际执行结果，生成23132条完整轨迹，平均8.12轮用户话语和68.24轮总对话。第三阶段在每个工具调用都在一个实时、隔离的操作系统工作空间中运行，生成真实的故障恢复动态而非模拟响应。在ISETrace上微调后，使用Qwen3-8B在标准协议下的智能体工具使用任务上，ClawEval pass@1从19.3提升到37.7。该结果优于零样本的GPT-4o和大了四倍的更大模型Qwen3-32B基础模型。对第二阶段的消融实验证明，多轮模拟带来了大部分性能提升。我们在https://github.com/Valiere01/ISE-Trace发布了所有源代码和数据集。

Original abstract: Training capable OS agents requires data that simultaneously captures structured user intents, multi-turn task delegation, and grounded tool execution--properties absent from existing datasets. We propose ISE (Intent -> Simulate -> Execute), a three-stage synthesis paradigm that addresses these gaps jointly. Stage 1 constructs roughly 50000 structured intents via a 4D framework (Persona x Domain x Task x Complexity); after deduplication the pool contains 43956 unique intents and attains a Vendi Score of 61.57 over the entire pool on mpnet-base-v2 embeddings (cosine kernel, q=1). Stage 2 drives multi-turn user-agent interaction through a role-locked user simulator that grounds each user turn in actual execution outcomes, producing 23132 complete trajectories averaging 8.12 user turns and 68.24 total dialogue turns. Stage 3 runs every tool call inside a live, isolated OS workspace, generating authentic failure-recovery dynamics instead of simulated responses. Fine-tuning on ISETrace improves ClawEval pass@1 from 19.3 to 37.7 using Qwen3-8B on agent tool-use tasks with a standard protocol. This result outperforms zero-shot GPT-4o and the larger Qwen3-32B base model which is four times bigger. An ablation on Stage 2 proves multi-turn simulation brings a large portion of the performance gain. We release all source code and dataset at https://github.com/Valiere01/ISE-Trace.

</details>

### [87] [LIBERO-Occ: Evaluating and Improving Vision-Language-Action Models under Scene-Induced Occlusion via Viewpoint Imagination](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10862v2)
*Taishan Li,Jiwen Zhang,Siyuan Wang,Xuanjing Huang,Zhongyu Wei*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 场景遮挡下VLA模型，提出视点想象方法，可迁移至coding agent处理不完整信息。

TL;DR: 针对VLA模型在遮挡场景下性能下降的问题，提出视点想象（VIM）方法，通过生成互补视图并融合观测与想象信息来提升鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型评估假设物体完全可见，但现实场景中遮挡普遍存在，导致模型性能严重下降。

Method: 提出Viewpoint Imagination (VIM)，从被遮挡的主观测中生成互补视角，并将观测与想象特征共同用于动作预测。

Result: VIM在多个任务套件、遮挡类型和严重程度下显著提升了鲁棒性，且无需额外部署相机。

Conclusion: 视点想象是解决部分可观测操作中感知补全的有前景机制。

中文摘要：视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在标准操作基准上取得了强劲的性能，但大多数评估假设任务相关物体完全可见。这一假设在现实场景中往往不成立，因为遮挡使得操作部分可观测。在本文中，我们研究了场景引起的遮挡作为VLA模型的一个基本挑战，并引入了LIBERO-Occ，一个面向遮挡的LIBERO扩展。实验表明，最先进的VLA在遮挡下性能显著下降。为解决此问题，我们提出了视点想象（Viewpoint Imagination, VIM），该方法从被遮挡的主观测中生成互补视角，并在观测和想象的证据上共同调节动作预测。VIM在不增加部署时额外相机的情况下，提高了跨任务套件、遮挡类型和严重程度的鲁棒性，表明视点想象是部分可观测操作中感知补全的一种有前景的机制。我们的基准和相应代码可在https://github.com/litsh/Libero-Occ获取。

Original abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models achieve strong performance on standard manipulation benchmarks, but most evaluations assume that task-relevant objects are fully visible. This assumption often fails in realistic settings, where occlusion makes manipulation partially observable. In this paper, we study \textit{scene-induced occlusion} as a fundamental challenge for VLA models and introduce \textbf{LIBERO-Occ}, an occlusion-oriented extension of LIBERO. Experiments show that state-of-the-art VLAs suffer substantial performance degradation under occlusion. To address this issue, we propose \textbf{Viewpoint Imagination (VIM)}, which generates a complementary view from an occluded primary observation and conditions action prediction on both observed and imagined evidence. VIM improves robustness across task suites, occlusion types, and severity levels without requiring additional cameras at deployment time, suggesting that viewpoint imagination is an promising mechanism for perception completion in partially observable manipulation. Our benchmark and corresponding code are available at: \href{https://github.com/litsh/Libero-Occ}{https://github.com/litsh/Libero-Occ}.

### [88] [An Ocean Model Ported by a Large Language Model: Experience and Lessons from FESOM2 (Fortran to C to C++/Kokkos)](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11356v1)
*Nikolay V. Koldunov,Suvarchal K. Cheedela,Sergey Danilov,Dmitry Sidorenko,Sebastian Beyer,Thomas Jung*

Main category: physics.ao-ph

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LLM成功将完整海洋模型FESOM2从Fortran移植到C和C++/Kokkos，保持物理准确性，GPU性能优于CPU。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证LLM是否能将完整的生产地球物理模型移植到不同语言而不降低物理准确性，并实现性能可移植性。

Method: 使用代理式LLM编码助手，分两阶段翻译：先Fortran到C（保留数值计算），再C到C++/Kokkos（引入并行）；要求严格字面翻译，每阶段用不同验收标准验证。

Result: C移植在五年统计量上匹配Fortran；Kokkos在CPU上逐位一致，GPU上统计接近；单个GPU比CPU快1.6-3.7倍，达到生产运行速度。

Conclusion: LLM可以在几周内将完整Fortran海洋模型移植到其他语言和加速器，同时保持物理特性，但需遵循严格验证程序。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）可以翻译和修改源代码，并且已被证明可以对不同复杂度的代码进行此类操作。但它们是否能够在不降低物理准确性的情况下，将一个完整的生产地球物理模型移植到不同的语言，这一点尚未得到证实。我们证明，LLM辅助的代码翻译可以在将完整生产海洋模型移植到现代性能可移植形式的同时，保持其物理特性。我们报告了使用一个由领域专家指导的代理式LLM编码助手，将FESOM2非结构化网格海洋-海冰模型（约74000行核心Fortran代码）首先移植到C，然后移植到C++/Kokkos以实现跨CPU和GPU的性能可移植性的经验。我们描述了被证明必要的实践、哪些方法有效、哪些无效，以及我们遇到的失败模式。有三个实践最为重要：分两阶段进行翻译，将重现数值计算（从Fortran到干净的C参考）与引入并行性（从C到Kokkos）分开；要求严格逐字翻译，不允许助手“改进”源代码；以及针对每个阶段使用适合该阶段的验收标准进行验证。C移植在五年长期模拟统计量水平上重现了原始Fortran。Kokkos移植在CPU上与C参考逐位相同，在GPU上多年运行统计接近。在涡旋丰富的网格上，最高740万个表面顶点，单个A100 GPU节点运行速度比CPU节点快1.6-3.7倍，达到了生产集成所需的每天1-2模拟年。结果不仅仅是单个GPU移植：通过遵循明确的验证程序，LLM在几周内将一个完整的Fortran海洋模型移植到了另一种语言和加速器上，同时保持了其物理特性。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can translate and modify source code, and have been shown to do so for codes of different complexity. Whether they can port a complete, production geophysical model to a different language without degrading its physics has not been established. We demonstrate that LLM-assisted code translation can preserve the physics of a complete production ocean model while moving it into a modern performance-portable form. We report our experience using an agentic LLM coding assistant, directed by domain experts, to port the FESOM2 unstructured mesh ocean--sea-ice model (about 74000 lines of core Fortran) first to C and then to C++/Kokkos for performance portability across CPUs and GPUs. We describe the practices that proved necessary, what worked and what did not, and the failure modes that we encountered. Three practices mattered most: translating in two stages that separate reproducing the numerics (Fortran to a clean C reference) from introducing parallelism (C to Kokkos); requiring a strictly literal translation in which the assistant was not permitted to ``improve'' the source; and validating each stage against an acceptance criterion suited to it.
  The C port reproduces the original Fortran at the level of long-term simulation statistics over five years. The Kokkos port is bit-for-bit identical to the C reference on CPU and statistically close on GPU over multi-year runs. On eddy-rich meshes up to 7.4 million surface vertices a single A100 GPU node runs 1.6--3.7 times faster than a CPU node, reaching the 1-2 simulated-years-per-day required for production integrations. The result is more than a single GPU port: by following a clear validation procedure, an LLM moved a full Fortran ocean model into another language and onto accelerators while preserving its physics in a matter of weeks.

</details>

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [89] [Drawing with Strangers: Population Scaling Drives Zero-Shot Mutual Intelligibility in Emergent Sketching](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10582v1)
*Jooyeon Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 涌现通信中零样本互通性，多agent协作启发

TL;DR: 通过扩展训练群体规模，实现了独立智能体群体间的零-shot 相互可理解性，该过程由感知基础驱动并形成结构趋同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索智能体与来自完全不同社群的陌生人进行通信的能力，即零-shot 相互可理解性，这一能力在涌现通信中尚未被充分研究。

Method: 采用涌现素描作为视觉通信模态，训练不同规模的独立群体，分析群体内与群体间的通信变异及视觉相似性锚定。

Result: 扩展群体规模显著提升了零-shot 相互可理解性：群体内变异增加防止同质化，群体间变异减少表明结构趋同，且趋同源于对目标图像的客观视觉相似性的锚定。

Conclusion: 零-shot 相互可理解性成为涌现通信中泛化的一个新维度，并为构建社交互操作的人工智能体提供了可行路径。

中文摘要：抽象：涌现通信中的泛化主要关注新颖输入或语言结构，但智能体与严格分离的社群中的陌生人进行通信的能力仍然相对未被探索。在这项工作中，我们将这种能力形式化为零-shot 相互可理解性（ZMI）：独立训练的群体在没有先前接触的情况下成功通信。利用涌现素描（智能体通过一组绘制的笔划进行通信）作为视觉基础的模态，我们发现扩展训练群体规模显著提高了独立群体之间的 ZMI。关键在于，随着群体规模扩大，群体内通信变异增加，防止了共同适应导致的同质化。同时，群体间变异减少，表明向某种类型的普遍性结构趋同。进一步分析揭示，这种普遍性是通过感知基础实现的：规模扩大的群体越来越将其涌现素描锚定在目标图像的客观视觉相似性上。这些结果共同将 ZMI 定位为涌现通信中一个独特的泛化轴，并指出了通向社交互操作的人工智能体的路径。

Original abstract: Generalization in emergent communication has largely focused on novel inputs or linguistic structures, yet the capacity for agents to communicate with strangers from strictly disjoint communities remains relatively unexplored. In this work, we formalize this capability as \textit{zero-shot mutual intelligibility (ZMI)}: successful communication between independently trained populations without prior exposure. Leveraging emergent sketching -- in which agents communicate through sets of drawn strokes -- as a visually grounded modality, we find that scaling the training population substantially improves ZMI across independent groups. Crucially, as we scale the population size, in-group communicative variation increases, preventing co-adaptation into homogeneity. Simultaneously, cross-group variation decreases, indicating a structural convergence toward a certain type of universality. Further analysis reveals that this universality is achieved through perceptual grounding: scaled populations increasingly anchor their emergent sketches on the objective visual resemblance of the target images. Together, these results position ZMI as a distinct axis of generalization in emergent communication and suggest a route toward socially interoperable artificial agents.

</details>


### [90] [Causal Ensemble Agent: Hierarchical Causal Discovery with LLM-guided Expert Reweighting](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10607v1)
*Xinyu Li,Yuanyuan Wang,Haoxuan Li,Chuan Zhou,Erdun Gao,Bo Han,Tongliang Liu,Kun Zhang,Howard Bondell,Mingming Gong*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 使用LLM作为元裁判聚合因果发现专家，涉及LLM agent元分析，可迁移至agent集成。

TL;DR: CEA框架通过聚合统计因果发现专家并使用LLM动态调整权重，显著提升了因果图的质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有因果发现方法结果冲突且未充分利用领域知识，直接使用LLM推断因果不准确。

Method: 提出CEA，整合多个统计因果发现专家，通过线性意见池化聚合，并用LLM作为元裁判在置信度边界附近动态重加权专家。

Result: 在合成和真实数据集上，CEA在多种因果发现方法中取得最强整体性能。

Conclusion: 使用LLM进行元分析能有效提升因果发现性能。

中文摘要：因果发现旨在从观测数据中发现因果结构，这对现实世界的决策至关重要。然而，不同的因果发现算法可能产生相互冲突的不同结果，使得准确因果图的识别变得复杂。传统方法依赖数值和统计假设，常常忽略丰富的领域特定信息，例如特征描述，这些信息也有助于结构学习。虽然最近的工作探索使用大型语言模型（LLMs）通过直接查询来推断因果关系，但由于缺乏与实际数据的一致性，此类方法可能不可靠。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了因果集成代理（CEA），一种新颖的框架，通过线性意见池化在不同图级别上聚合统计发现专家的结构见解，并使用LLM作为元裁判，在聚合置信度接近决策边界时动态重新加权专家，从而构建一个改进且更完整的因果图。在合成和真实数据集上的大量实验表明，CEA在广泛的因果发现方法中实现了最强的整体性能，突显了使用LLM进行因果发现元分析的有效性。

Original abstract: Causal discovery aims to uncover causal structures from observational data, which is crucial for real-world decision-making. However, different causal discovery algorithms can produce divergent results that conflict with each other, complicating the identification of accurate causal graphs. Traditional approaches rely on numerical values and statistical assumptions, often ignoring rich domain-specific information, such as feature descriptions, which could also help structure learning. While recent works explore using Large Language Models (LLMs) to infer causal relations via direct queries, such methods can be unreliable due to a lack of alignment with the actual data. To address these limitations, we propose Causal Ensemble Agent (CEA), a novel framework that aggregates structural insights from statistical discovery experts across different graph levels via linear opinion pooling, and uses an LLM as a meta-referee to dynamically reweight experts when the aggregated confidence is close to the decision boundary, thereby composing an improved and more complete causal graph. Extensive experiments on both synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that CEA achieves the strongest overall performance across a wide range of causal discovery methods, highlighting the effectiveness of using LLMs for meta-analysis in causal discovery.

</details>


### [91] [Divide and Cooperate: Role-Decomposed Multi-Agent LLM Training with Cross-Agent Learning Signals](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10684v1)
*Jaewan Park,Solbee Cho,Jay-Yoon Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 角色分解的多agent训练框架，跨agent学习信号，通用多agent方法，可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出DAC框架，将语言代理的搜索与生成角色分解为两个专用代理，通过弃权信号和硬正证据增强改善信用分配和鲁棒性，在QA任务上超越全微调单一模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将证据获取和答案生成耦合在单一策略中，导致角色冲突、策略空间爆炸、探索低效和信用分配问题，亟需解耦以提高训练效率和性能。

Method: 提出DAC，将代理搜索分解为搜索者和生成者两个子任务，各自用角色特定信号训练；生成者同时作为证据充分性验证者，在证据不足时弃权，弃权信号修正搜索者奖励；搜索者通过硬正证据增强生成者的训练环境。

Result: 在通用和多跳QA基准上，DAC（基于共享骨干的LoRA实现）优于依赖全微调单一模型的各种基线方法。

Conclusion: 角色分解的多代理框架能有效解决耦合策略的缺陷，通过跨代理信用分配和稳健性增强提升知识密集型问答性能。

中文摘要：在知识密集型问答中，执行多步推理的现代语言代理表现出强大性能。然而，现有方法通常将证据获取和答案生成耦合在单一策略中，迫使单个模型扮演多个潜在冲突的角色，导致策略空间组合爆炸并阻碍高效探索。同时，这在训练中引入了信用分配问题：检索到足够证据的搜索行为仍可能因生成失败而受到惩罚，反之亦然。我们提出DAC（分治合作），一种角色分解的多代理训练框架，将代理搜索分为两个合作子任务，每个由专用代理处理，并使用角色特定的学习信号进行训练。生成器扮演双重角色，既作为答案产生者又作为证据充分性验证者，当检索到的证据不足时弃权。此弃权信号被纳入搜索代理的奖励中，提供结构化的跨代理学习信号以改善信用分配。相反，搜索者通过硬正证据增强使生成器暴露于多样且具有挑战性的证据环境，从而提高其鲁棒性。在通用和多跳问答基准上的实验表明，DAC通过共享骨干网络上的参数高效LoRA模块实现，相比依赖全微调单一模型的方法取得了强劲性能。

Original abstract: Modern language agents which perform multi-step reasoning have shown strong performance in knowledge-intensive question answering. However, existing approaches typically couple evidence acquisition and answer generation within a single policy. This forces a single model to play multiple potentially conflicting roles, inducing a combinatorial explosion in the policy space and hindering efficient exploration. It also introduces a credit assignment problem during training: a search action that retrieves sufficient evidence may still be penalized when generation fails, and vice versa. We propose DAC (Divide and Cooperate), a role-decomposed multi-agent training framework that divides agentic search into two cooperative subtasks, each handled by a dedicated agent trained with role-specific learning signals. The generator serves a dual role as both an answer producer and an evidence sufficiency verifier, abstaining when retrieved evidence is insufficient. This abstention signal is incorporated into the search agent's reward, providing structured cross-agent learning signals that improve credit assignment. Conversely, the searcher exposes the generator to diverse and challenging evidence environments by hard-positive evidence augmentation, improving its robustness. Experiments on general and multi-hop QA benchmarks show that DAC, implemented via parameter-efficient LoRA modules over a shared backbone, achieves strong performance against prior baselines that rely on full fine-tuning of monolithic models.

</details>


### [92] [Test-Time Gradient Guidance of Flow Policies in Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11087v1)
*Zhiyuan Zhou,Andy Peng,Charles Xu,Qiyang Li,Tobias Springenberg,Kevin Frans,Sergey Levine*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 测试时策略梯度引导流策略，虽然用于RL但可启发agent的推理时优化方法。

TL;DR: 提出QGF算法，在测试时通过价值梯度引导预训练的流策略生成高价值动作，无需额外策略学习，避免了训练时策略优化的不稳定性，在离线RL基准测试中表现优异且成本更低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表达性策略在监督模仿学习中表现良好，但融入强化学习训练时存在稳定性和可扩展性问题，因此探索仅在测试时进行策略改进的替代方案。

Method: 预训练参考流策略（BC目标）和价值函数评论家，测试时使用价值梯度引导参考策略生成高价值动作，无需额外策略学习。

Result: 在离线RL基准测试中，QGF优于先前测试时RL方法，与训练时算法竞争力相当且成本更低，并随着模型大小增加而良好扩展。

Conclusion: QGF提供了一种实用且有效的RL算法替代方案，通过测试时策略优化避免了训练不稳定性，适用于表达性策略。

中文摘要：表达性的连续控制策略，如扩散模型和流模型，构成了最近在模拟和真实机器人控制中扩展模仿学习进展的基础。虽然已知它们在监督模仿学习设置中能稳定扩展，但将其纳入强化学习（RL）流程以进行策略改进已被证明更为困难。这通常需要专门的训练目标或通过去噪过程进行反向传播，这会导致众所周知的稳定性问题并影响可扩展性。在本文中，我们研究了这样一个问题：仅在测试时使用简单的策略改进方案，同时保持稳定的监督策略训练不变，是否可以成为避免这些问题的竞争性替代方案。为此，我们提出了QGF（Q-Guided Flow），一种完全在测试时进行策略优化的RL算法。QGF的工作原理是预训练一个参考流策略（通过标准的行为克隆目标）和一个价值函数评论家，并在测试时使用价值梯度引导参考策略生成更高价值的动作，而无需任何额外的策略学习。实验上，QGF在高维动作空间的单任务和目标条件离线RL基准测试中优于先前的测试时RL方法，并且与最先进的训练时算法具有竞争力，同时运行成本更低。此外，通过避免演员-评论家训练的不稳定性，它表现出良好的模型大小扩展性，提供了一种实用且有效的使用表达性策略的RL算法替代方案。

Original abstract: Expressive continuous control policies, such as diffusion and flow models, form the backbone of recent advances in scaling imitation learning for simulated and real robot control. While they are known to scale stably in the supervised imitation learning setting, incorporating them into reinforcement learning (RL) pipelines for policy improvement has proven more difficult. It often requires specialized training objectives or backpropagating through denoising processes, which cause well-known issues with stability and affect scalability. In this paper we study the question of whether simple policy improvement schemes at test time alone, leaving stable supervised policy training intact, can be a competitive alternative which sidesteps these issues. To this end, we propose QGF (Q-Guided Flow), an RL algorithm that performs policy optimization entirely at test time. QGF works by pre-training both a reference flow policy (via a standard behavioral cloning objective) and a value function critic and, at test time, using the value gradient to guide the reference policy to generate higher-value actions without any additional policy learning. Empirically, QGF outperforms prior test-time RL methods on single-task and goal-conditioned offline RL benchmarks with high-dimensional action spaces, and is competitive with state-of-the-art training-time algorithms while being much cheaper to run. Moreover, it exhibits favorable scaling with model size by avoiding the instability of actor-critic training, offering a practical and effective alternative RL algorithm with expressive policies.

</details>


### [93] [TRACE: A Unified Rollout Budget Allocation Framework for Efficient Agentic Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11119v1)
*Heming Zou,Qi Wang,Yun Qu,Yuhang Jiang,Lizhou Cai,Yixiu Mao,Ru Peng,Xin Xu,Weijie Liu,Kai Yang,Saiyong Yang,Xiangyang Ji*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 针对agentic RL的rollout预算分配框架，通过树结构展开增强奖励对比，可迁移至coding agent的强化学习训练。

TL;DR: TRACE通过将rollout预算分配到提示根和中间前缀，增强了多轮代理RL中的奖励对比，提升了性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR方法中，奖励对比不足，因为简单或复杂提示导致低方差反馈，且仅结果奖励无法区分多轮决策。以往方法只在提示层分配资源，忽略了轮次内前缀层的信息差异。

Method: 提出TRACE框架，将ReAct轮次建模为语义节点，形成树状rollout。使用共享预测器估计条件成功概率，将预算分配给最可能产生混合奖励的提示根和中间前缀，从而增强奖励对比。

Result: 在典型代理基准上，TRACE实现竞争性性能，如Qwen3-14B多跳问答准确率提升2.8个百分点，且效率更高。

Conclusion: TRACE通过树状rollout分配有效提升了多轮代理RL中的奖励对比和策略更新信号，展示了在固定预算下增强反馈的潜力。

中文摘要：具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）是增强大型语言模型推理和代理行为的一种有前景的方法。然而，基于rollout的策略优化常常受到奖励对比不足的限制，当过于简单或复杂的提示产生低方差反馈，以及当仅基于结果的奖励为多轮rollout中的每个决策分配相同的终端评估时，就会出现这种问题。以往的努力集中在将可用的rollout资源分配给有前景的提示，但它们仅在提示层面利用样本信息性，而忽略了同一rollout中不同轮次间前缀层面信息性的变化。本工作针对多轮代理RL，通过将每个ReAct式的思考-行动-观察轮次建模为语义上不同的节点，使得预算分配从提示根扩展到具有进一步延续的轮次级前缀，这自然形成了树状结构的rollout。我们引入了用于对比探索的树状rollout分配（TRACE），这是一个统一的rollout分配框架，在固定采样预算内增强奖励对比。技术上，TRACE将rollout预算分配给最可能产生混合终端奖励的提示根和中间前缀。一个共享的通用预测器根据前缀历史估计这些锚点的条件成功概率，以指导这种分配。由此产生的自适应树状结构丰富了仅基于结果的反馈，并放大了策略更新信号。实验上，TRACE在典型的代理基准测试中取得了竞争性的性能和效率提升，例如，在相同采样成本下，将Qwen3-14B多跳问答的平均准确率提高了2.8个百分点。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) is a promising approach for enhancing reasoning and agentic behavior in large language models. However, rollout-intensive policy optimization is often limited by insufficient reward contrast, arising when overly simple or complex prompts generate low-variance feedback and when outcome-only rewards assign the same terminal assessment to every decision in a multi-turn rollout. Past efforts have focused on allocating available rollout resources to promising prompts, yet they only leverage sample informativeness at the prompt level and neglect variation in prefix-level informativeness across turns within the same rollout. This work targets multi-turn agentic RL by modeling each ReAct-style thought-action-observation turn as a semantically distinct node, allowing budget allocation to extend from prompt roots to turn-level prefixes with further continuations, which naturally forms tree-structured rollouts. We introduce Tree Rollout Allocation for Contrastive Exploration (TRACE), a unified rollout allocation framework that enhances reward contrast within a fixed sampling budget. Technically, TRACE allocates rollout budget to both prompt roots and intermediate prefixes that are most likely to yield mixed terminal rewards. A shared generalizable predictor estimates conditional success probability at these anchors from prefix histories to guide this allocation. The resulting adaptive tree structure enriches outcome-only feedback and amplifies the policy-update signal. Empirically, TRACE achieves competitive performance and efficiency gains on typical agentic benchmarks, e.g., improving Qwen3-14B Multi-Hop QA average accuracy by 2.8 points over competitive baselines at equal sampling cost.

</details>


### [94] [EEVEE: Towards Test-time Prompt Learning in the Real World for Self-Improving Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11182v1)
*Weixian Xu,Shilong Liu,Mengdi Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 多数据集测试时提示学习框架，使LLM agent在真实任务流中自我改进，直接相关agent方法。

TL;DR: 提出EEVEE框架，通过路由器分区和协同进化实现多数据集测试时提示学习，显著提升异构任务流鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示学习框架多针对单数据集设计，无法处理真实世界多数据集异构输入流，导致跨数据集干扰。

Method: 提出路由器将输入划分到任务聚类并分配提示，采用路由器-提示协同进化策略交替学习以解决相互依赖。

Result: 在多基准测试中，EEVEE相比Qwen3-4B-Instruct和DeepSeek-V3.2分别提升10.38和24.32分，超越SOTA方法GEPA和ACE达37.2%和48.2%。

Conclusion: EEVEE是首个多数据集测试时提示学习框架，在保持单基准性能的同时提升了异构数据流下的鲁棒性。

中文摘要：在本文中，我们提出了EEVEE，这是首个面向LLM智能体的多数据集测试时提示学习框架，能够在真实世界的任务流中进行测试时提示学习。现有方法主要针对单数据集设置设计，而现实应用要求模型处理来自多个数据集、领域和任务分布的异构输入流，限制了其实际适用性。为了减轻跨数据集干扰，EEVEE引入了一个路由器，将输入输入划分到任务聚类中，并分配适当的提示配置。该设计通过路由器-提示协同进化策略进行优化，该策略采用交错的路由器和提示学习阶段来解决它们的相互依赖关系。跨多个数据集的实验表明，该框架在保持单基准学习能力和效率的同时，提高了异构数据流下的鲁棒性。具体来说，EEVEE在Qwen3-4B-Instruct和DeepSeek-V3.2上分别将平均多基准分数提高了10.38和24.32分，比最先进的GEPA和ACE方法分别高出37.2%和48.2%。

Original abstract: In this paper, we propose EEVEE, the first multi-dataset test-time prompt learning framework for LLM agents, enabling test-time prompt learning under real-world task streams. Existing methods are largely designed for single-dataset settings, while real-world applications require models to handle heterogeneous input streams drawn from multiple datasets, domains, and task distributions, limiting their practical applicability. To mitigate cross-dataset interference, EEVEE introduces a router that partitions incoming inputs into task clusters and assigns them to suitable prompt configurations. This design is optimized via a router-prompt co-evolution strategy, which employs interleaved router and prompt learning phases to address their mutual dependency. Experiments across multiple datasets demonstrate that the framework improves robustness under heterogeneous data streams while maintaining single-benchmark learning capability and efficiency. Specifically, EEVEE improves average multi-benchmark scores by 10.38 and 24.32 points over Qwen3-4B-Instruct and DeepSeek-V3.2, surpassing SOTA methods GEPA and ACE by up to 37.2% and 48.2%.

</details>


### [95] [FlowBank: Query-Adaptive Agentic Workflows Optimization through Precompute-and-Reuse](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11290v1)
*Lingzhi Yuan,Chenghao Deng,Fangxu Yu,Souradip Chakraborty,Mohammad Rostami,Furong Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 查询自适应agent工作流优化，通过预计算与复用实现高效部署，通用agent方法可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出FlowBank，一种基于组合的智能体工作流优化框架，通过构建互补工作流库并在推理时自适应选择，在多个基准上取得最佳性能-成本权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作流优化方法要么只部署单个工作流浪费互补信息（任务级），要么为每个查询生成新工作流成本高昂（查询级），需要构建可重用互补库并自适应选择以平衡性能和成本。

Method: 三阶段框架：Diversifying阶段用DiverseFlow生成覆盖不足查询的互补候选池；Curating阶段用CuraFlow压缩为紧凑组合；Matching阶段将部署建模为二分图边值预测，为每个查询路由到预测效用最佳的工作流。

Result: 在五个基准上平均得分最高，且成本竞争力强，相对自动基线提升4.26%，相对手工基线提升14.92%。

Conclusion: FlowBank证明了组合式工作流优化的有效性，在性能与成本之间取得了良好折中，有望成为智能体系统部署的实用方案。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型（LLM）的多智能体系统日益强大，但当前的智能体工作流优化范式存在令人不满意的权衡。任务级方法消耗大量离线计算，却只部署单个工作流，导致互补候选方案未被利用；而查询级方法每次查询都合成新的工作流，推理成本高昂。我们的动机分析表明，这些范式与其说是相互竞争，不如说是相互补充：离线搜索中发现的工作流通常能解决不同的查询子集，并且许多由昂贵的查询级生成处理的查询，已经可以通过更便宜的预计算工作流解决。这表明了不同的目标：与其寻找一个普遍最优的工作流或为每个实例重新生成一个，我们应构建一个紧凑的可重用、互补的工作流库，并在推理时自适应地选择。这需要解决三个耦合问题：生成互补而非冗余的候选方案，将其压缩为可部署的小型组合，以及在性能与成本的权衡下为每个查询分配正确的工作流。为此，我们提出了FlowBank，一个基于组合的智能体工作流优化三阶段框架。多样化阶段提出DiverseFlow，引导搜索覆盖不足的查询，产生高覆盖率的候选池。精选阶段提出CuraFlow，将该池压缩为冗余最小的紧凑组合。匹配阶段将部署建模为查询-工作流二分图上的边值预测，并为每个传入查询路由到预测效用最佳的组合成员。在五个基准测试中，FlowBank在评估方法中取得了最高的平均分数，同时保持成本竞争力，相对于最强的自动和手工基线分别相对提升了4.26%和14.92%。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based multi-agent systems are increasingly powerful, but current agentic workflow optimization paradigms make an unsatisfying trade-off. Task-level methods spend substantial offline compute yet deploy only a single workflow, leaving complementary candidates unused, while query-level methods synthesize a new workflow per query at substantial inference cost. Our motivating analysis shows these paradigms are more complementary than competing: workflows discovered during offline search often solve different subsets of queries, and many queries handled by expensive query-level generation can already be solved by cheaper precomputed workflows. This suggests a different objective: rather than searching for one universally best workflow or regenerating one per instance, we should build a compact bank of reusable, complementary workflows and select among them adaptively at inference time. Doing so requires solving three coupled problems: generating complementary rather than redundant candidates, compressing them into a small deployable portfolio, and assigning each query to the right workflow under a performance-cost trade-off. To this end, we present FlowBank, a three-stage framework for portfolio-based agentic workflow optimization. Diversifying proposes DiverseFlow to steer search toward under-covered queries and produce a high-coverage candidate pool. Curating proposes CuraFlow to compress this pool into a compact portfolio with minimal redundancy. Matching casts deployment as edge-value prediction on a query-workflow bipartite graph and routes each incoming query to the portfolio member with the best predicted utility. Across five benchmarks, FlowBank achieves the highest average score among the evaluated methods while remaining cost-competitive, improving over the strongest automated and handcrafted baselines by 4.26% and 14.92% relative, respectively.

</details>


### [96] [Signed Compression Progress on a Sealed Audit is Goodhart-Resistant](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11417v1)
*Ayush Mittal,Dhruv Gupta*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出 signed compression progress 作为内在奖励，与 agent 自我改进相关，但偏理论。

TL;DR: 证明密封审计下的符号压缩进步作为内在奖励是可信的，能够避免虚假进步，并给出了有限审计面板的理论保证和失败模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 压缩进步作为内在动机的长期提议缺乏严格证明，尤其是其“可信性”声称。本文旨在精确化并证明该奖励在密封审计下可防止虚假奖励。

Method: 定义内在奖励为密封审计损失的符号递减，推导累积奖励的伸缩性质；引入有限审计面板的均匀偏差界；通过Lean 4机械化核心结构，并在ARC-TGI任务上实验验证。

Result: 累积奖励等于端点审计改进加上有限审计偏差界（2Δ_n）；实验显示偏差按n^{-0.527}缩放，符号进步抵抗多种攻击，而可重用审计易被利用。

Conclusion: 密封审计上的符号压缩进步是真正改进的可信信号，具有理论保证和实用价值。

中文摘要：压缩进步是一种长期存在的内在动机提议：当智能体的世界模型在预测或压缩经验方面变得更好时给予奖励。民间声称这种奖励是“可信的”，因为它只在学习时支付。我们使这一点精确化并加以证明。如果内在奖励是固定密封审计损失的符号递减，即 r_t = E(theta_{t-1}) - E(theta_t)，那么累积奖励恰好伸缩到端点审计改进，因此没有任何策略可以在真实审计性能停滞或下降时无限推高奖励。对于有限审计面板，同样的结果成立，但有一个尖锐的假阳性预算：累积经验奖励最多等于真实审计改进加上 2 Delta_n(F, δ)，即模型类的均匀审计偏差。这是无水平线的：一旦密封面板均匀控制该类，随时间适应性不花费任何代价。该定理还识别了失败模式：如果进步被裁剪、在智能体自身流上评分、暴露于可重用面板上的高容量模型，或应用于使 Delta_n 无效的神经类，则保证消失。我们给出了结构核心（伸缩性、有限审计界限、有限吉布斯和熵下限）的 Lean 4 机械化，以及在 ARC-TGI 网格变换生成器上使用自适应保持攻击的实验套件。实验证实了理论：有限审计偏差按 n^{-0.527} 缩放；符号进步抵抗裁剪农场、流泄漏和噪声电视好奇心；天真的可重用审计可被黑盒标量反馈利用，而标准发布防御使攻击保持在 2 Delta_n 阈值以下。密封审计上的符号压缩进步是真正改进的会计信号。

Original abstract: Compression progress is a long-standing proposal for intrinsic motivation: reward an agent when its world model becomes better at predicting or compressing experience. The folk claim is that this reward is "credible" because it is paid only for learning. We make this precise and prove it. If intrinsic reward is the signed decrease of a fixed sealed-audit loss, r_t = E(theta_{t-1}) - E(theta_t), then cumulative reward telescopes exactly to endpoint audit improvement, so no policy can push reward up indefinitely while true audit performance stagnates or degrades. For finite audit panels the same result holds with a sharp false-positive budget: cumulative empirical reward is at most true audit improvement plus 2 Delta_n(F, delta), the uniform audit deviation of the model class. This is horizon-free: adaptivity over time costs nothing once the sealed panel uniformly controls the class.
  The theorem also identifies the failure modes: the guarantee disappears if progress is clipped, scored on the agent's own stream, exposed to a high-capacity model on a reusable panel, or applied to a neural class that makes Delta_n vacuous. We give a Lean 4 mechanization of the structural core (telescoping, the finite-audit bound, finite Gibbs, and the entropy floor) and an experiment suite on ARC-TGI grid-transformation generators with adaptive holdout attacks. Experiments confirm the theory: finite-audit deviation scales as n^{-0.527}; signed progress resists clip-farming, stream leakage, and noisy-TV curiosity; naive reusable audits are exploitable by black-box scalar feedback, while standard release defenses keep the attack below the 2 Delta_n threshold. Signed compression progress on a sealed audit is an accounting signal of genuine improvement.

</details>

### [97] [Human-AI Teaming Through the Lens of Calibration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10906v1)
*Eric Nalisnick,Chi Zhang,Sophia Qian,Yixin Wang*

Main category: stat.ML

Selection reason: 人类-AI团队校准，研究预测组合与委托机制，可迁移至多agent协作与校准。

TL;DR: 从统计校准角度分析人机协作，发现组合方法破坏人类校准，委托方法虽保留预测器校准但给拒绝器带来巨大校准负担，尤其当人类使用系统不可见信息时。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究人机协作中的校准问题，揭示现有方法的缺陷。

Method: 理论分析和实证实验，对比组合与委托两种框架。

Result: 组合方法不保留人类校准；委托方法保留预测器校准但拒绝器需高度精细校准，且随人类专业知识增加而更难。

Conclusion: 人类依赖未观测信息时委托框架的拒绝器校准无法实现。

中文摘要：我们从统计校准的角度研究人机协作模型。我们假设团队由一个人工智能模型和人类组成——两者都相对于特征空间的某种划分进行了校准——并揭示校准假设如何传播到协作框架中。具体而言，我们考虑以下框架：（i）结合人类和模型的预测，或（ii）将预测责任委托给人类或模型。我们通过理论和实证结果表明，现有的组合方法不能保留人类的校准程度。委托方法（通过委托行为本身）保留了下游预测器的校准，但将负担转移到了决定谁进行预测的拒绝元模型上。拒绝元模型必须足够精细地校准，以定位每个成员擅长的区域，这一需求随着人类专业知识的增加而增长，并且当人类依赖系统无法观察到的信息时变得无法实现。

Original abstract: We study models for human-AI teaming through the lens of statistical calibration. We assume the team consists of an AI model and human -- both of which are calibrated with respect to some partitioning of the feature space -- and expose how the calibration assumptions propagate into the teaming framework. In particular, we consider frameworks that either (i) combine human and model predictions or (ii) delegate prediction responsibility to either a human or model. We show via theoretical and empirical results that existing methods for combination do not preserve the human's degree of calibration. Methods for delegation (by the very act of delegation) preserve calibration of the downstream predictors but shift the burden onto the rejector meta-model that decides who predicts. The rejector must be calibrated finely enough to locate where each member is superior, a demand that grows with the human's expertise and becomes unattainable when the human relies on information the system cannot observe.

</details>


<div id='cs.DS'></div>

# cs.DS [[Back]](#toc)

### [98] [The Power of Test-Time Training for Approximate Sampling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11437v1)
*Noah Golowich,Ankur Moitra,Dhruv Rohatgi*

Main category: cs.DS

Selection reason: 测试时训练的抽象理论，与 agent 在线适应相关，但过于理论化。

TL;DR: 本文形式化测试时训练为从已知分布类中采样的问题，给出查询复杂度的二次下界，证明随机游走方法最优，并表明限制分布类大小可规避下界，可作为TTT理论框架的起点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI中LLM采样效率受限于模型与任务关系，TTT通过推理时更新权重适应任务，但缺乏理论框架。本文旨在为TTT建立形式化基础。

Method: 将TTT形式化为从已知分布类F中采样，给定近似密度预言机，利用计数到采样约化思想，通过查询复杂度分析证明下界，并讨论通过限制F大小规避下界。

Result: 得到查询复杂度的二次下界，证明随机游走方法最优，并表明在F大小适度时下界可被打破。

Conclusion: 后一结果可视为TTT的抽象，为TTT理论框架的发展提供起点。

中文摘要：从一个复杂的概率分布中有效采样是一个基本问题，近年来随着生成式人工智能的兴起，这一问题变得越来越重要，因为从LLM中复杂的采样程序已被提出用于解决具有挑战性的推理问题。然而，这种采样算法的有效性受到LLM与特定采样任务之间关系的限制，这推动了测试时训练（TTT）框架的发展。TTT通过根据推理时收到的部分生成和奖励反馈来更新模型的权重，从而适应特定问题。在这项工作中，我们提出了TTT的形式化定义，将其视为从一个已知类F的概率分布中抽取样本的问题，给定一个能够对μ^⋆进行近似密度估计的预言机\hat μ。这与Jerrum、Valiant和Vazirani (1986)以及Jerrum和Sinclair (1989)的开创性工作中研究的将采样问题约化为近似计数问题密切相关：具体来说，当F是所有分布的类时，它恰好与上述计数到采样的约化一致。

在本文中，我们首先证明了对于足够大的类F，在给定对\hat μ的查询访问的情况下，从μ^⋆采样所需的查询复杂度有一个二次下界，从而表明Jerrum和Sinclair (1989)提出并由Hayes和Sinclair (2010)改进的随机游走方法是最优的。这回答了Hayes和Sinclair提出的一个开放问题。然后我们证明，如果F的大小被适当限制，则可以规避这个下界。正如我们讨论的，后一个结果可以被视为TTT的抽象，因此代表了为TTT发展出一个有原则的理论框架的起点。

Original abstract: Efficiently sampling from a complex probability distribution is a fundamental problem which has become increasingly pertinent in recent years with the rise of generative AI, as sophisticated sampling procedures from LLMs have been proposed to solve challenging reasoning problems. The efficacy of such sampling algorithms is limited, however, by the relationship between the LLM and the particular sampling task at hand, which has motivated the framework of test-time training (TTT). TTT works by updating a model's weights in response to partial generations and reward feedback received at inference time, thus adapting to the particular problem. In this work, we propose a formalization for TTT as the problem of producing a sample from a given probability measure $μ^\star$ belonging to a known class ${F}$ of distributions, given an oracle $\hat μ$ which yields approximate density estimates for $μ^\star$. This is closely related to the problem of reducing sampling to approximate counting studied in seminal works of Jerrum, Valiant & Vazirani (1986) and Jerrum & Sinclair (1989): namely, when ${F}$ is the class of all distributions, it coincides exactly with the aforementioned counting-to-sampling reduction.
  In this paper, we first show a quadratic lower bound on the query complexity of sampling from $μ^\star$ given query access to $\hat μ$ (for sufficiently large classes ${F}$), thus showing that the random walk approach proposed by Jerrum & Sinclair (1989) and refined by Hayes & Sinclair (2010), is optimal. This answers an open question posed by Hayes & Sinclair. We then show that this lower bound can be circumvented if the size of ${F}$ is bounded appropriately. As we discuss, this latter result can be viewed as an abstraction of TTT, and thus represents a starting point for the development of a principled theoretical framework for TTT.

</details>


<div id='cs.MA'></div>

# cs.MA [[Back]](#toc)

### [99] [Decoupling Thought from Speech: Knowledge-Grounded Counterfactual Reasoning for Resilient Multi-Agent Argumentation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10475v1)
*Jakub Masłowski,Jarosław A. Chudziak*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: KG-CFR多agent辩论框架通过知识反驳推理提升长程稳定性，可迁移到coding agent的规划与鲁棒性。

TL;DR: 提出知识驱动的反事实推理（KG-CFR）架构，通过解耦规划与执行，增强了多智能体系统在持续扰动下的稳定性，并显著提升了论证质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多智能体辩论框架优化偏向最终输出准确性，忽视过程稳定性，导致长期交互中出现逻辑退化、论点重复和角色漂移。

Method: 提出KG-CFR双阶段架构，强制分离私有的检索增强规划缓冲区和公开的执行层；在DRAU环境下评估，引入多样性和随机环境冲击。

Result: 在270个危机模拟轨迹中，KG-CFR阻止了95%以上的关键冲击后退化，论证质量从0.694提升至0.822；消融实验表明理论依据与规划同等重要。

Conclusion: 架构解耦是增强系统弹性的关键因素，KG-CFR通过保持智能体与原始计划的一致性，有效减少了语义循环，提升了整体稳定性。

中文摘要：多智能体辩论框架已被证明可以改善大型语言模型在收敛任务中的表现，但目前的优化方式严重偏向最终输出准确性，而非过程的稳定性。在长期交互过程中，受到持续扰动的反应式系统经常出现逻辑退化、论点重复和角色漂移。为了从结构上防止身份丢失并保持过程保真度，我们引入了知识驱动的反事实推理（KG-CFR），这是一种双阶段架构，在私有的检索增强规划缓冲区和公开的执行层之间强制实施严格的关注点分离。我们在不确定性条件下的动态资源分配（DRAU）——一个专门的1v1v1环境——中评估该系统，引入了与标准辩论设置不同的多样性。在270个完全因子化的危机模拟轨迹（包含随机环境冲击）中，KG-CFR在超过95%的扰动运行中阻止了裁判检测到的关键冲击后退化（定义为质量变化Δ≤ -0.20），将整体论证质量从0.694提高到0.822。我们的主要贡献是证明了架构解耦是在持续压力下增强系统弹性而不损失质量的重要因素。此外，我们引入了用于话语分歧和计划执行对齐的自定义向量指标，这些指标提供了强有力且方向一致的运行稳定性证据。我们的消融实验表明，适当的理论依据对于论证质量与前瞻性规划同样重要。根据我们的初步指标评估，KG-CFR通过保持智能体与原始计划的一致性，减少了语义循环。

Original abstract: Multi-agent debate frameworks have been shown to improve large language model performance in convergent tasks, but they are currently optimized in a way that heavily favors final output accuracy rather than stability of the process. During long-horizon exchanges reactive systems under sustained perturbations often experience logic degradation, argument repetition, and role drift. To structurally prevent the identity loss and maintain the process fidelity, we introduce Knowledge-Grounded Counterfactual Reasoning (KG-CFR), a dual-stage architecture that enforces a strict separation of concerns between a private, retrieval-augmented planning buffer, and a public execution layer. We assess this system in Dynamic Resource Allocation under Uncertainty (DRAU), a dedicated 1v1v1 environment, introducing diversity as distinct from standard debate settings. Over 270 completely factorial crisis simulation trajectories with stochastic environmental shocks, KG-CFR prevents judge-detected critical post-shock degradation (defined as a quality shift, $Δ\le -0.20$) in more than 95% of perturbed runs, increasing the overall argument quality from 0.694 to 0.822. Our primary contribution is the demonstration of architectural decoupling being an important factor of systemic resilience enhancement under sustained pressure without quality loss. Furthermore, we introduce custom vector metrics for discourse divergence and plan-execution alignment that provide strong, directionally consistent evidence of operational stability. Our ablation experiments suggest that the proper doctrinal grounding can be an equally important factor for argument quality, as the prospective planning. KG-CFR, according to our initial metric evaluations, reduces semantic looping, by preserving the agent's consistency with the original plan.

</details>


### [100] [Decentralized Multi-Agent Systems with Shared Context](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10662v1)
*Yuzhen Mao,Azalia Mirhoseini*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 去中心化多agent系统，在SWE-bench等任务上验证，直接相关coding agent与多agent协作。

TL;DR: 提出去中心化语言模型（DeLM），通过并行智能体、共享验证上下文和任务队列实现去中心化协调，显著提升软件工程测试时间扩展和长上下文推理性能，并降低计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MAS依赖集中式编排，一个主智能体作为通信和集成瓶颈，限制了子任务数量的扩展。

Method: 提出DeLM框架：智能体异步认领子任务、读取共享验证上下文、执行本地推理并写回紧凑验证更新，无需中央控制器。

Result: 在SWE-bench Verified上，Avg.@1/Pass@2/Pass@4均最优，比最强基线提高10.5个百分点，成本降低50%；在LongBench-v2多文档问答上，平均准确率最高，比最强基线提高5.7个百分点。

Conclusion: DeLM通过去中心化协调有效克服了集中式MAS的瓶颈，在多个任务上实现更优的性能和效率。

中文摘要：多智能体系统（MAS）通过将复杂问题分解为并行子任务，可以在测试时扩展大型语言模型的推理能力。然而，现有的大多数MAS依赖于集中式编排，即一个主智能体分配任务、收集输出并合并结果。随着子任务数量的增加，这个控制器会成为通信和集成的瓶颈。我们提出了去中心化语言模型（DeLM），这是一种MAS框架，通过并行智能体、共享验证上下文和任务队列实现去中心化协调。智能体异步认领子任务，读取累积的进度，执行本地推理，并写回紧凑的验证更新。共享上下文作为通用的通信基础，使智能体能够基于彼此的验证进展进行构建，而无需通过中央控制器路由每个更新。实验上，DeLM改进了软件工程测试时的扩展性和长上下文推理。在SWE-bench Verified上，DeLM在Avg.@1、Pass@2和Pass@4上取得了最佳性能，比最强基线提高了高达10.5个百分点，同时每个任务的成本降低了约50%。在LongBench-v2多文档问答上，DeLM在四个前沿模型系列中取得了最高的平均准确率，比最强基线提高了高达5.7个百分点。代码可在项目网站 https://yuzhenmao.github.io/DeLM/ 获取。

Original abstract: Multi-agent systems (MAS) can scale large language model reasoning at test time by decomposing complex problems into parallel subtasks. However, most existing MAS rely on centralized orchestration, where a main agent assigns work, collects outputs, and merges results. As the number of subtasks grows, this controller becomes a communication and integration bottleneck. We propose Decentralized Language Models (DeLM), a MAS framework that decentralizes coordination through parallel agents, a shared verified context, and a task queue. Agents asynchronously claim subtasks, read accumulated progress, perform local reasoning, and write back compact verified updates. The shared context acts as a common communication substrate, enabling agents to build on one another's verified progress without routing every update through a central controller. Empirically, DeLM improves both software-engineering test-time scaling and long-context reasoning. On SWE-bench Verified, DeLM achieves the best performance across Avg.@1, Pass@2, and Pass@4, with gains of up to 10.5 percentage points over the strongest baseline, while reducing cost per task by roughly 50%. On LongBench-v2 Multi-Doc QA, DeLM achieves the highest average accuracy across four frontier model families, improving over the strongest baseline by up to 5.7 percentage points. The code is available on our project website at https://yuzhenmao.github.io/DeLM/.

</details>
